janamejaya uvāca
prādurbhāve muniśreṣṭha māthure caritaṃ śubham
śṛṇvan vai nādhigacchāmi tṛptiṃ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ
dvārakāyāṃ nivasataḥ kṛtadārasya yad guṇam
caritaṃ brūhi kṛṣṇasya sarvaṃ hi viditaṃ tava
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
janamejaya kṛṣṇasya kṛtadārasya bhārata
nibodha caritaṃ citraṃ tasyaiva sadṛśaṃ prabhoḥ
prāptadāro mahātejā vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān
rukmiṇyā sahito devyā yayau raivatakaṃ nṛpa
upavāsāvasānaṃ hi rukmiṇyāḥ pratipūjayan
tarpayiṣyan svayaṃ viprāñ jagāma madhusūdanaḥ
kumārāḥ prayayus tatra putrā bhrātara eva ca
preṣitā vāsudevena nāradasyābhyanujñayā
ṣoḍaśa strīsahasrāṇi jagmur eva ca dhīmataḥ
ṛddhyā paramayā rājan viṣṇor evānurūpayā
tatas tatra dvijātīnāṃ kāmān prādād adhokṣajaḥ
arthināṃ dharmanityānāṃ bandinām iṣṭavādinām
kalyāṇanāmagotrāṇāṃ mahatāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām
yaunaiḥ śrautaiś ca mākhaiś ca śuddhānāṃ kurunandana
tarpayitvā dvijān kāmair iṣṭair iṣṭaḥ satāṃ hariḥ
jñātīn saṃtarpayām āsa yathārhaṃ dharmavatsalaḥ
upavāsāvasāne ca bhagavān saviśeṣataḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
bahu mene priyāṃ bhāryāṃ rukmiṇīṃ bhīṣmakātmajām
vasatas tasya kṛṣṇasya sadārasyāmitaujasaḥ
sahāsīnasya rukmiṇyā nārado 'bhyāyayau muniḥ
āgataṃ cāprameyātmā munim indrānujas tadā
śāstradṛṣṭena vidhinā arcayām āsa keśavaḥ
so 'rcito vāsudevena munir arcyatamaḥ satām
pārijātataroḥ puṣpaṃ dadau kṛṣṇāya bhārata
tad vṛkṣarājakusumaṃ rukmiṇyāḥ pradadau hariḥ
pārśvasthā sā hi kṛṣṇasya bhojyā naravarābhavat
pratigṛhya tu tat puṣpaṃ kāmāraṇir aninditā
śirasy amalapatrāḍhyaṃ dadau kṛṣṇeṅgitānugā
trailokyarūpasarvasvaṃ nārāyaṇamanoharā
śuśubhe tena puṣpeṇa dviguṇaṃ rukmiṇī tadā
tāṃ nāradas tathovāca munir brahmasutas tadā
tavaivaupayikaṃ puṣpam ekaṃ devi pativrate
alaṃkṛtaṃ puṣpam etat saṃsargāt tava sarvathā
atyarhā ca matā me tvam etat puṣpaṃ dhṛtavrate
kalyāṇaguṇasaṃpanne satataṃ bhartṛvatsale
amlānam etat satataṃ puṣpaṃ bhavati kāmini
saṃvatsaraparaṃ kālaṃ kālajñe guṇasaṃmate
īpsitān api gandhāṃś ca dadāti vadatāṃ vare
śītoṣṇe cepsite devi puṣpam etat prayacchati
sravaty api rasān devi manasā kāṅkṣitān varān
sevyamānaṃ ca saubhāgyaṃ dadāti varavarṇini
sravaty api tathā gandhān īpsitān prativardhanān
yāni yāni ca puṣpāṇi tvaṃ devy abhilaṣiṣyasi
kusumaṃ vṛkṣarājasya tāni tāni pradāsyati
etad eva bhagādhānaṃ dharmiṣṭhe dharmadaṃ tathā
matiṃ ca nāśubhe dhatte dhāryamāṇaṃ sadā śubhe
yad yad icchasi varṇaṃ ca tat sarvaṃ dhārayiṣyati
svalpaṃ vā yadi vā sthūlaṃ chandatas te bhaviṣyati
aniṣṭagandhaharaṇam etat sadgandhavardhanam
pradīpakarma rātrau ca karoti kamalekṣaṇe
saṃtānakasrajo mālāṃ puṣpavastrādi vācyutam
puṣpamaṇḍapamukhyāni cintitena pradāsyati
bubhukṣā vā pipāsā vā glānir vāpy atha vā jarā
devy etaddhārayantyās te svacchandena bhaviṣyati
anugītāni gītāni dāsyaty api ca cintite
suvāditrān sumadhurāṃs tathaiva tava saṃmatān
pūrṇe saṃvatsare devi puṣpam etat tavāntikāt
nivartsyate taruvaraṃ samayena prayāsyati
kṛtir eṣā hi bhadraṃ te pārijātasya suprabhe
nisargataḥ sargakṛtā satkārārthe 'suradviṣām
umā devavarasyeṣṭā himācalasutā satī
dhārayed īśvarī nityaṃ puṣpāṇy etāni suprabhe
aditiś ca sapaulomī mahendrasuratāraṇī
sāvitrī vedamātā ca śrīś ca sarvaguṇodite
devapatnyas tathaivānyā devāś ca vasudevatāḥ
saṃvatsaraḥ paraḥ kālaḥ sarveṣāṃ tu na saṃśayaḥ
ṣoḍaśastrīsahasrāṇāṃ madhye tvaṃ khalu vartase
adyeṣṭāṃ vāsudevasya vedmi tvāṃ bhojanandini
sapatnyas te guṇopete sarvāḥ sarveśvarapriye
avamānāvasekena tvayā siktādya bhāmini
prakāśam adya saubhāgyam anivāryaṃ yaśaś ca te
mandārakusumaṃ dattaṃ yat te madhunighātinā
adya sātrājitī devī jñāsyate varavarṇinī
saubhāgyāḍhyaṃ sadā vetti yātmānaṃ subhagā satī
sāmbamātātha gāndhārī bhāryāś cānyā mahātmanaḥ
saubhāgyārthodyatākāṅkṣām adya mokṣyanti niḥspṛhāḥ
saubhāgyaikaratho jaitras tava devy adya niḥsṛtaḥ
manoratharathānāṃ yaḥ sahasrair api durjayaḥ
adyāham avagacchāmi sarvathā sarvaśobhane
ātmā dvitīyaḥ kṛṣṇasya bhoje tvam iti bhāmini
trailokyaratnasarvasvam adadād yat tavācyutaḥ
jīvitātiśayas tena tvayā prāpto haripriye
nāradenaivam uktaṃ tu tathyaṃ vākyaṃ narādhipa
tatrasthāḥ śuśruvuḥ preṣyāḥ preṣitāḥ satyabhāmayā
devīnāṃ ca tathānyāsāṃ sapatnīnāṃ viśāṃ pate
dṛṣṭvā tāṃ saviśeṣaṃ ca nāradenābhyudāhṛtam
tac ca śrutvā sunikhilaṃ preṣyābhiḥ strīsvabhāvataḥ
prakāśīkṛtam evāsīd viṣṇor antaḥpure tadā
karṇākarṇi tato devyaḥ kaulīnam iva sarvaśaḥ
mantrayāṃ cakrire hṛṣṭāḥ rukmiṇyātiguṇodayam
arheti putramāteti jyeṣṭheti ca samāgatāḥ
prāyeṇa pravadanti sma hṛṣṭā dāmodarastriyaḥ
mamṛṣe na sapatnyās tu tat saubhāgyaguṇodayam
satyabhāmā priyā nityaṃ viṣṇor atulatejasaḥ
rūpayauvanasaṃpannā svasaubhāgyena garvitā
abhimānavatī devī śrutvaiverṣyāvaśaṃ gatā
samutsṛjantī vasanaṃ sakuṅkumaṃ
śucismitā śuklatamaikam aṃśukam
jagrāha roṣākulitena cetasā
vahneḥ śikhā śrīr iva vardhitendhanā
daṃdahyamānā jvalanena vardhatā
īrṣyāsamutthena gataprabheva
krodhānvitā krodhagṛhaṃ viviktaṃ
viveśa tāreva ghanaṃ satoyam
badhvā lalāṭe himacandraśuklaṃ
dukūlapaṭṭaṃ priyaroṣacihnam
paryantadeśaṃ sarasena devī
vilipya sā lohitacandanena
saṃsmṛtya saṃsmṛtya śiraḥ saroṣaṃ
prakampamānā samayopaviṣṭā
dīrghopadhāne śayane 'panīya
vibhūṣaṇāny ekanibaddhaveṇī
akāraṇārthena viruṣyamānā
preṣyājanasyābhijanena yācitā
vicūrṇayām āsa kuśeśayaṃ sā
niḥśvasya niḥśvasya nakhair natabhrūḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
upaviṣṭaṃ muniṃ jñātvā rukmiṇyā saha keśavaḥ
niścakrāmāprameyātmā vyapadeśena sarvakṛt
jagāma tvaritaś caiva satyabhāmāgṛhaṃ mahat
ramye raivatakoddeśe nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
abhimānavatīm iṣṭāṃ prāṇair api garīyasīm
jānan sātrājitīṃ viṣṇur viveśa śanakair iva
ruṣitām iva tāṃ devīṃ snehāt saṃkalpayann iva
bhītabhīto 'tiśanakair viveśa yadunandanaḥ
dārukaṃ dvāradeśe tu tiṣṭhety uktvā viveśa ha
nāradasyopacārārthaṃ pradyumnaṃ viniyujya ca
sa dadarśa priyāṃ dūrat krodhāgāragatāṃ tadā
preṣyāmadhyasthitāṃ krodhān niḥśvasantīṃ muhur muhur
karajāgrāvalīḍhaṃ tu paṅkajaṃ mukhapaṅkaje
saṃśleṣayitvā niḥśvasya viharantīṃ punaḥ punaḥ
kiṃcid ākuñcitāgreṇa caraṇena vasuṃdharām
kṛtvā pṛṣṭhe 'tha vadanaṃ vihasantīṃ punaḥ punaḥ
karapadme punaḥ śaśvan mukhapadmaṃ niveśya ca
vinatāṃ cārusarvāṅgīṃ dhyāyantīṃ kamalekṣaṇām
sarasaṃ candanaṃ gṛhya preṣyāhastād aninditām
prasādhayitvā hṛdayaṃ kṣipantīṃ nirdayaṃ punaḥ
punar utthāya śayanāt patantīṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ
tās tāś ceṣṭās tathānyāś ca priyāyā dadṛśe hariḥ
avaguṇṭhya yadā vaktram upadhāne nyaveśayat
idam antaram ity eva tato matvā janārdanaḥ
preṣyājanaṃ samājñāpya anākhyeyo śmi saṃjñayā
saśaṅkitapracāraś ca tvarito 'nvagamac ca tām
jagrāha vyajanaṃ caiva sthitvā sa paripārśvataḥ
śanair avāsṛjad vātaṃ jahāsa śanakair iva
sa parijātapuṣpasya saṃsargād anuvāsitaḥ
babhāra bhagavān gandhaṃ divyaṃ mānuṣadurlabham
atyadbhutaṃ sugandhaṃ ca jighritvā vismayānvitā
apāvṛṇon mukhaṃ satyā kim etad iti cābravīt
sotthitā pṛṣṭhato devam apaśyantī suvismitā
paryapṛcchad atho preṣyā gandhasya prabhavaḥ tadā
tāḥ pṛṣṭās tv aprabhāṣantyo jānubhyāṃ dharaṇīṃ gatāḥ
adhomukhyas tatas tasthuḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭās tadā
tad apūrvam adṛṣṭvaiva gandhaṃ muñcati medinīm
katham ekataras tasyā gandho 'yam udabhūt khalu
kiṃ tv idaṃ syād iti ca sā vivekṣantī samantataḥ
dadṛśe keśavaṃ devī sahasā lokabhāvanam
yujyatīti tadovāca sahasāsrāvilekṣaṇā
avasikteva roṣeṇa babhūva praṇayānvitā
sā prasphuritacārvoṣṭhī niḥśvasyādhomukhī tadā
muhūrtam asitāpāṅgī tasthāv anyamukhī śubhā
nibadhya bhrūkuṭīṃ vāmāṃ samyag utkṣipya locane
niveśya vadanaṃ haste śobhasīty abravīd dharim
tasyāḥ susrāva netrābhyāṃ vāri praṇayakopajam
kuśeśayapalāśābhyām avaśyāyajalaṃ yathā
samutpatya jalaṃ tatra patitaṃ vadanāmbujāt
pratijagrāha padmākṣaḥ karābhyām api satvaram
athorasi patat toyaṃ śrīvatsāṅko 'mbujekṣaṇaḥ
priyānayanajaṃ devaḥ parimṛjyedam abravīt
sravaty asitapatrākṣi kimarthaṃ tava bhāmini
toyaṃ sundari netrābhyāṃ puṣkarābhyām ivodakam
prabhāte pūrṇacandrasya madhyāhne paṅkajasya ca
bibharti tava kiṃ vaktraṃ vapur mama manoharam
kimarthaṃ kauṅkumaṃ vāso mahārajatam eva ca
nānugṛhṇāsi suśroṇi śuklaṃ vāso 'nugṛhyate
vāsasy ete tavābhīṣṭe mahārajatakauṅkume
devābhigamanād ūrdhvaṃ śuklaṃ neṣṭaṃ hi te priye
kiṃ cānābharaṇaṃ gātraṃ sugātri tava kathyatām
citrakasthānam ākrāntaṃ kasmāc ca varavarṇini
śvetena tava paṭṭena vāsasā priyadarśane
lalāṭaṃ sevyate kasmāc candanena sugandhinā
sarasenāyatāpāṅgi kāntena hṛdayapriye
prabhopamardaḥ kenātha kāraṇenānanasya ca
karoṣi mama cātyarthaṃ mano glāpayasi priye
prasṛtaś candanarasaḥ kapolapraṇayī tava
patralekhāsapatnatvaṃ prāpto nātivirājate
ratnasyābharaṇair muktā tava grīvā na śobhate
grahanakṣatrarahitā dyaur ivāvyaktaśāradī
pūrṇacandrasapatnena smereṇābahubhāṣiṇā
kim u nābhāṣase mādya sukhenotpalagandhinā
ardhākṣṇāpi hi tāvan māṃ kimarthaṃ na nirīkṣase
muñcasy eva saniḥśvāsaṃ toyam añjanadurdinam
alam indīvaraśyāme ruditena manasvini
jalam añjanakalmāṣaṃ mā mokṣīr ānanadviṣam
tvadīyo 'haṃ yadā devi khyāto jagati kiṃkaraḥ
nājñāpayasi māṃ kiṃ tvaṃ pureva varavarṇini
kim akārṣam ahaṃ devi vipriyaṃ tava bhāmini
yenātimātram ātmānam āyāsayasi sundari
manasā karmaṇā vācā na tvām aticarāmy aham
sarvathā sarvacārvaṅgi satyam etad bravīmy aham
bahumāno mamānyāsu strīṣu sarvāsu śobhane
snehaś ca bahumānaś ca tvām ṛte 'nyāsu nāsti me
naiva tvāṃ madano jahyād amṛte mayi māmakaḥ
iti me niścitaṃ viddhi cetaḥ surasutopame
kṣamādayaś ca medinyāṃ śabdādyāś cāmbare guṇāḥ
dhruvaṃ paṅkajagarbhābhe tvayi snehas tathā mama
rucir agnau yathā divyā prabhā caiva divākare
kāntiś ca cāśvatī candre snehas tvayi tathā mama
evaṃvādinam ātmeṣṭaṃ satyabhāmā janārdanam
śanair uvāca netrābhyāṃ pramṛjya subhagā jalam
madīyas tvam iti hy āsīn mama nityaṃ manaḥ prabho
adya sādhāraṇasnehas tvam ity avagatā hy aham
nājñāsiṣam ahaṃ pūrvam anityaṃ kālaparyayam
adya lokagatiṃ kṛtsnām avagacchāmi na dhruvām
amṛtāyā dvitīyaṃ hi janmedaṃ mama sarvathā
kim atra bahunoktena hṛdayaṃ vetti te 'cyuta
vāṅmātram iva paśyāmi mādhuryaṃ saṃprayujyate
mayi snehaś ca kṛtakas tavānyatra na kṛtrimaḥ
ṛjusvabhāvāṃ bhaktāṃ ca sarvathā puruṣottama
avajānāsi jānan māṃ kaitavīṃ vṛttim āsthitaḥ
etāvat khalu paryāptaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ draṣṭavyam adya yat
śrutaṃ vāpy atha vā śrāvyaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ snehaphalodayaḥ
yadi tv aham anugrāhyā mām anujñātum arhasi
tapasyeyaṃ paraṃ kṛtvā niścayaṃ puruṣottama
bhartuś chandena nārīṇāṃ tapo vā vratakāni vā
niṣphalaṃ khalu yad bhartur acchandena kriyeta yat
itīdam uktvā punar eva śobhanā
mumoca toyaṃ nayanodbhavaṃ satī
grahāya pītaṃ harivāsasaḥ śubhā
paṭāntam ādhāya mukhe śucismitā
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
nārāyaṇaḥ satyabhāmāṃ punar evātha bhārata
provāca praṇayāt kruddhām abhimānavatīṃ satīm
dahatīva mamāṅgāni śokaḥ kamalalocane
kim u tatkāraṇaṃ yena tvam evam ativiklavā
śāpitāsi mama prāṇair ācakṣvānatyayo yadi
śrotavyaṃ yadi bhaktena bhartrā sarvāṅgaśobhane
tataḥ provāca bhartāraṃ satyā satyavrate sthitam
bāṣpagadgadayā vācā tathaivādhomukhī sthitā
tvayaiva sthāpitaṃ pūrvaṃ saubhāgyaṃ mama mānada
jagaty amalapatrākṣe tat khyātaṃ keśināśana
śiro vahāmi ceṣṭatvāt tavāhaṃ deva garvitā
sarvasīmantinīmadhye spṛhaṇīyāsmi sarvathā
sāham adyāvahāsyāsmi sapatnīnāṃ janasya ca
iti preṣyābhir ākhyātaṃ śrutvā tathyaṃ tatas tataḥ
yat pārijātakusumaṃ dattavān nāradas tava
tat kileṣṭajane dattaṃ tvayāhaṃ parivarjitā
ratnātiśayadānena tasyām abhyadhikaḥ kila
snehaś ca bahumānaś ca prakāśaṃ gamitas tvayā
tām astauṣīt samakṣaṃ te priyāṃ sa kila nāradaḥ
tam aśrauṣīś ca hṛṣṭas tvaṃ priyāyāḥ saṃstavaṃ kila
stotavyā yadi tāvat sā nāradena tavāgrataḥ
durbhago 'yaṃ janas tatra kimartham anuśabditaḥ
praṇayasya rasaṃ dattvā paścāttāpaḥ prabho yadi
anujñāṃ me prayacchasva tapaḥ kartuṃ prasīda me
svapnenāpi na dṛṣṭvāhaṃ śraddadhyāṃ puṣkarekṣaṇa
yad anyad eva nirvṛttam aśrauṣaṃ paśyatas tava
kāmaḥ kāmaṃ tu tasyaiva muner atulatejasaḥ
atra manyus tu me deva sāṃnidhyaṃ tava tatra yat
mānārthaṃ jīvyate loke sadbhir ity uktavān asi
tad evaṃ sati necchāmi jīvituṃ mānavarjitā
mamābhavad yato rakṣā bhayam adya tato mama
sarvato rakṣate yo māṃ sa māṃ nādyābhirakṣati
hā gatiṃ kāṃ gamiṣyāmi tyaktā deva tvayā vibho
kumudvatīgatāṃ nūnaṃ gatiṃ yāsyāmy asaṃgatā
kim akārṣam ahaṃ mohād īśvarāṇāṃ priyāpriyam
priyā bhūtvāpriyā bhūtā yad ahaṃ tava mānada
vasantakusumaiś citraṃ sadā raivatakaṃ girim
priyā bhūtvāpriyā bhūtā kathaṃ drakṣyāmy ahaṃ punaḥ
parapuṣṭasvanonmiśraṃ puṣpagandhavahaṃ śucim
kathaṃ nāmānilaṃ dveṣyā seveyaṃ durbhagā satī
jalakrīḍāṃ tavāṅkasthā deva kṛtvā mahodadhau
kathaṃ daurbhāgyam āpannā paśyeyam api sāgaram
sātrājiti priyā nānyā tvatto me 'stīti viddhi mām
tvam avocaḥ kva tad yātam atha vā kaḥ smariṣyati
yad adrākṣīd dhi māṃ śvaśrūr bahumānena nandinīm
avajñātā tvayā rājñī nūnaṃ daurbhāgyakīrtitā
kiṃ nu gūḍhena me premṇā susnigdhenāpi mānada
yat samānāṃ janair devo māṃ na paśyati nityadā
nāhaṃ tvāṃ kitavaṃ dhūrtam ajñāsiṣam ariṃdama
adya jñāto 'si tatpakṣaś cañcalo janavañcakaḥ
svaravarṇeṅgitākārair nigūḍho deva yatnataḥ
cora jñāto 'si tatpakṣo vāṅmātramadhuraḥ śaṭhaḥ
evam īrśyāvaśaṃ prāptāṃ devīṃ sātrājitīṃ hariḥ
abhimānavatīṃ devaḥ sāntvapūrvam athābravīt
maivaṃ padmapalāśākṣi mameśvari vada priye
kim atra bahunoktena tvadīyam avagaccha mām
tat pārijātakusumaṃ tasyā devi mamāgrataḥ
nārado matpriyaṃ kurvan munir akliṣṭakarmakṛt
dākṣiṇyād anurodhāc ca dattavān nātra saṃśayaḥ
prasīdaikāparādhaṃ me marṣayasva śucismite
pārijātasya puṣpāṇi yadīcchasy atikopane
tadā dātāsmi suśroṇi satyam etad bravīmi te
svargāspadād ānayitvā pārijātaṃ drumeśvaram
gṛhe te sthāpayiṣyāmi yāvatkālaṃ tvam icchasi
evam uktvā tu hariṇā provāca harivallabhā
yady evaṃ sa drumaḥ śakya ihānayitum acyuta
manyur eṣa pramṛṣṭo hi bhaved bahuguṇo mama
sīmantinīnāṃ sarvāsām adhikā syām adhokṣaja
tathāstu prathamaḥ kalpa iti tāṃ madhusūdanaḥ
provācāpratimo devo jagataḥ prabhavo 'vyayaḥ
tathetyukte 'tha kṛṣṇena tutoṣa samitiṃjaya
satyabhāmā satām iṣṭā kaṃsanāśanavallabhā
tataḥ snāto jagannāthaḥ sarveśaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ
cakārāvaśyakaṃ sarvaṃ sarvakāmapradaḥ satām
dadhyau ca nāradaṃ devaḥ snāto devamuniṃ nṛpa
abhyājagāma snānānte muniśreṣṭho mahodadhau
tam āgataṃ narapate satāṃ gatir adhokṣajaḥ
satyayā saha dharmātmā yathāvidhim apūjayat
pādau prakṣālayāṃ cakre muneḥ sātrājitī svayam
jalaṃ devaḥ svayaṃ kṛṣṇo bhṛṅgāreṇa dadau tadā
athopakalpayām āsa sukhāsīnāya keśavaḥ
paramānnaṃ sa munaye prayatātmā jagadguruḥ
tal lokakartrā satkṛtya dattaṃ munir udāradhīḥ
bubhuje vadatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ śraddhayā parayānvitaḥ
upaspṛśya tatas tṛptaḥ pradadau cāśiṣaḥ prabhoḥ
tāś ca prītena manasā pratijagrāha keśavaḥ
tataḥ sātrājitīṃ devīṃ praṇatāṃ nārado 'bravīt
prasārya dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ sajalaṃ jalajekṣaṇām
yathedānīṃ tathaiva tvaṃ bhava devi pativratā
saviśeṣaṃ ca subhagā bhava tvaṃ tapaso balāt
ity uktā munimukhyena satyabhāmā haripriyā
uttasthau mahatā yuktā harṣeṇa tu narādhipa
sa kṛṣṇo 'py abhyanujñāṃ tu labdhvā munivarāt tadā
bubhuje vighasaṃ dhīmān aprameyaparākramaḥ
tatas tv āvaśyakaṃ kṛtvā satyabhāmāpi bhārata
anujñayā tadā bhartur viveśāntargṛhaṃ mudā
tato vinirgatā devī kṛṣṇasyaivābhyanujñayā
sthitā pārśve ca kṛṣṇasya namaskṛtvā mahātmane
tato muhūrtam āsitvā nāradaḥ kṛṣṇam abravīt
āpṛcche tvāṃ gamiṣyāmi śakralokam adhokṣaja
tatrādyaṃ devam īśānaṃ namaskṛtya maheśvaram
gāsyanti devagandharvās tathaivāpsarasāṃ varāḥ
māsi māsy ucitaṃ hy etan mahendrasadane vibho
pūjārthaṃ devadevasya gāndharvaṃ nṛtyam eva ca
antarhito devadevaḥ somaḥ sapravaro vibhuḥ
paśyaty amaramukhyena kṛtaṃ bhaktyādrighātinā
nimantrito 'haṃ pūrvedyuḥ puṣpaṃ dātuṃ mahādyute
pārijātasya bhadraṃ te tarurājño mahātmanaḥ
yad etad āhṛtaṃ svargāt tat tvadarthaṃ mayā vibho
devopabhogyam etad dhi tarurājasamudbhavam
iṣṭaḥ sa vṛkṣaḥ satataṃ śacyāḥ puṣkaralocana
saubhāgyam āvahaty eva pūjyamāno 'pi nityaśaḥ
puṇyaṃ kartuṃ tadā sṛṣṭaḥ pārijāto mahādrumaḥ
adityā dharmanityena kaśyapena mahātmanā
purādityā mahātejās toṣitaḥ kila kaśyapaḥ
vareṇa cchandayām āsa mārīcas tapaso nidhiḥ
sovāca subhagā yena bhaveyaṃ munisattama
svalaṃkṛtā kāmataś ca sarvair eva vibhūṣaṇaiḥ
īpsitaṃ gītanṛtyaṃ ca bhaven mama tapodhana
kumārī nityadā caiva bhaveyaṃ tapasāṃ nidhe
virajāḥ śokarahitā bhaveyam api nityadā
patibhaktimatī caiva dharmaśīlā tathaiva ca
pārijātaṃ tato 'srākṣīd adityāḥ priyakāmyayā
sarvakāmapradaiḥ puṣpair āvṛtaṃ divyagandhadaiḥ
triśākhaṃ sarvadā dṛśyaṃ sarvabhūtamanoharam
sarvapuṣpāṇi dṛśyante tasminn eva mahādrume
īdṛśāny asya puṣpāṇi bibharty ekātirūpiṇī
bahurūpāṇi cāpy anyā padmāni ca tathāparā
mandārād api vṛkṣāc ca sāras uddhṛtya kaśyapaḥ
tasmād eṣa taruśreṣṭhaḥ sarveṣāṃ śreṣṭhatāṃ gataḥ
tatas tatra nibadhyātha kaśyapaṃ pradadau śubhā
aditir mama puṇyārthaṃ saubhāgyārthaṃ tathaiva ca
niṣkrayeṇa mayā muktaḥ kaśyapas tu tapodhanaḥ
indro dattas tathendrāṇyā saubhāgyārthaṃ tato mama
somaś cāpy atha rohiṇyā ṛddhyā ca dhanadas tathā
evaṃ saubhāgyado vṛkṣaḥ pārijāto na saṃśayaḥ
pārijāto viṣṇupadyāḥ pārijāteti śabditaḥ
mandārapuṣpair yad yukto mandāras tena kathyate
ko 'py ayaṃ dārur ity āhur ajānanto yato janāḥ
kovidāra iti khyātaḥ saṃtataḥ sa mahātaruḥ
mandāraḥ kovidāraś ca pārijātaś ca nāmabhiḥ
sa vṛkṣo jñāyate divyo yasyaitat kusumottamam
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tato jigamiṣuṃ tatra nāradaṃ munisattamam
provāca bhagavān viṣṇur aprameyaparākramaḥ
maharṣe dharmatattvajña svargaṃ gatvā tvayānagha
dṛṣṭvā sadasyān devasya tripuraghnasya dhīmataḥ
anujñayā madvacanād vijñāpyaḥ pākaśāsanaḥ
saṃvarṇayitvā bhrātṛtvaṃ paurāṇaṃ vetsi yan mune
yad asrākṣīn muniśreṣṭho bhagavān kaśyapas tarum
pārijātaṃ purādityāḥ priyārthaṃ dharmavittama
sa puṇyam atisaubhāgyaṃ dadāti tarusattamaḥ
tava dattaṃ purā dānaṃ vrate ca tarusattamam
devībhir dharmanityābhir dharmārtham amarottama
dattaṃ śrutvābhikāṅkṣanti dātuṃ patnyo mama prabho
puṇyārthaṃ dānadharmārthaṃ mama prītyartham eva ca
ānāyya ca dvāravatīṃ pārijātaṃ mahātarum
datte dāne punaḥ svargaṃ tatra taṃ nāyayiṣyasi
sa vācya evaṃ bhagavān balabhid bhagavaṃs tvayā
tathā tathā prayatnaś ca kāryo munivara tvayā
yathā taruvaraṃ dadyāt pārijātaṃ sureśvaraḥ
tatra dūtaguṇaṃ tāvat paśyāmas te tapodhana
saṃbhāvyā sarvakṛtyānāṃ saṃpad dhi tvayi me matā
evaṃ nārāyaṇenokto nārado bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
prahasyovāca keśighnam idaṃ vākyaṃ tapodhanaḥ
bāḍham evaṃ pravakṣyāmi yadumukhya sureśvaram
na tu dāsyati devendraḥ pārijātaṃ kathaṃcana
mandaraṃ parvataśreṣṭhaṃ dānavais tridaśais tathā
nikṣipya toyadhau pūrvaṃ pārijātaḥ samāhṛtaḥ
mandaraṃ parvataśreṣṭhaṃ nayituṃ preṣitaḥ purā
pārijātaṃ hareṇāpi lokakartrā janārdana
svayaṃ vijñāpito gatvā tataḥ śakreṇa śaṃkaraḥ
ākrīḍadruma udyāne śacyāḥ syād iti yācitaḥ
tathāstv iti varo datto mahādevena cānagha
na ca nītaḥ pārijāto mandaraṃ citrakandaram
krīḍāvṛkṣaḥ sa śacyeti vyapadeśena mokṣitaḥ
mahendreṇa mahābāho pārijātas taruḥ purā
priyārtham umayāsrākṣīt pārijātavanaṃ haraḥ
gavyūtimātravistīrṇaṃ mandarasyaikakandare
na tatra sūryabhāḥ kṛṣṇa praviśanti nagottame
na ca candraprabhāḥ śītā naiva kṛṣṇa sadāgatiḥ
śītoṣṇe chandatas tatra śailaputryā bhavanti hi
svayaṃprabhaṃ vanaṃ tad dhi mahādevasya tejasā
varjayitvā mahādevaṃ sagaṇaṃ yaduvardhana
māṃ cānyas tad vanaṃ divyaṃ na prayāti kathaṃcana
sravanti tatra vārṣṇeya pārijātāḥ samantataḥ
sarvaratnāni mukhyāni manasā kāṅkṣitāni vai
gaṇās tāny upabhuñjanti pravarāṇāṃ mahātmanām
ājñayā devadevasya lokanāthasya keśava
pārijātād bahuguṇaṃ phalaṃ teṣāṃ tathā dhanam
abhimānaṃ prabhā caiva guṇā bhūriguṇās tathā
mūrtimantaś ca te vṛkṣāḥ somaṃ devaṃ vṛṣadhvajam
upatiṣṭhanti satataṃ pravaraiḥ saha keśava
raudreṇa tejasā juṣṭā hīnā duḥkhaiḥ sukhānvitāḥ
taravo mandare te hi dayitāḥ śailakanyayā
praviveśāndhako nāma ghoras tatra mahābalaḥ
daiteyo varadānena darpitaḥ pāpaniścayaḥ
sa hato devadevena hareṇāmitraghātinā
avadhyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ vṛtrād daśaguṇaṃ balī
evaṃ duḥkhena te deva pārijātaṃ pradāsyati
puṣkarākṣa sahasrākṣaḥ satyam etad bravīmi te
satataṃ sahito devyā śacyā sa hi varadrumaḥ
sarvakāmapradaḥ kṛṣṇa tathendrasyāmitaujasaḥ
vāsudeva uvāca
mune tad yujyate sādhu mahādevena dhīmatā
yac chacīṃ kāraṇaṃ kṛtvā na nītaḥ sa taruḥ purā
sa jyeṣṭhaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ lokakṛt prabhavo 'vyayaḥ
pārāvaryasya sadṛśaṃ kṛtavān iti me matiḥ
ahaṃ yavīyān devasya sarvathā balaghātinaḥ
lālanīyaś ca bhagavañ jayanta iva sattama
sarvathā bhagavāṃs tāvad upāyair bahuvistaraiḥ
karotu yatnaṃ prītyarthaṃ śakto hy asi tapodhana
mayā mune pratijñātaṃ puṇyārthaṃ satyabhāmayā
svargād ihānayiṣyāmi pārijātam iti prabho
mayā tad anṛtaṃ śakyaṃ kathaṃ kartuṃ tapodhana
nānṛtaṃ hi vaco vipra proktapūrvaṃ mayānagha
mayi bhagnapratijñe hi lokānāṃ saṃplavo bhavet
yan mayā hi muniśreṣṭha lokā dharmaguṇānvitāḥ
paripālyāḥ sthitau sarve sa kathaṃ hy anṛtaṃ vadet
na devagandharvagaṇā na rākṣasā
na cāsurā naiva ca yakṣapannagāḥ
mama pratijñām apahantum udyatāḥ
sukhāya jīvanti ciraṃ mahāmune
sa pārijātaṃ yadi na pradāsyati
prayācyamāno bhavatāmareśvaraḥ
tataḥ śacīvyāmṛditānulepane
gadāṃ vibhokṣyāmi puraṃdarorasi
iti pravācyo yadi sāmapūrvakaṃ
prayācyamāno na taruṃ prayacchati
suniścitaṃ mām avagamya sarvathā
tvayāpi kāryaḥ khalu tatra niścayaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
nārado 'tha munir gatvā mahendrasadanaṃ prabhuḥ
tāṃ rātrim avasat tatra dadṛśe ca mahotsavam
tatrādityā mahātmāno vasavaś ca surottamāḥ
rājarṣayaś ca vidvāṃsaḥ svargatāḥ karmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ
nāgā yakṣāś ca siddhāś ca cāraṇāś ca tapodhanāḥ
brahmarṣayaś ca śataśo devarṣimanavas tathā
suparṇāś ca mahātmāno marutaś ca mahābalāḥ
divaukasāṃ nikāyāś ca śataśo 'nye samāgatāḥ
upary upari sarveṣāṃ somo devo maheśvaraḥ
tasthāv amitavikrāntaḥ svair gaṇaiḥ parivāritaḥ
devarṣibhir muniśreṣṭhaiḥ saṃvṛtaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ
kalpāntarasahasreṣu kṣayo yeṣāṃ na vidyate
yān arcayanti satataṃ devā deveśvaropamāḥ
ātmajñā nāvalepāndhā ye ca dharmapathe sthitāḥ
rudrāś ca kāśyapā devam adhyupāsanta bhārata
skandaś ca bhagavān raudrir gaṅgā ca saritāṃ varā
arciṣmāṃs tumburuś caiva bhāriś ca vadatāṃ varaḥ
netāro devadevānām ete hi tapasānvitāḥ
etān anuvidhīyante sarvadevagaṇā nṛpa
dharmanityās taponityāḥ satāṃ mārgam upāśritāḥ
ye tv ime mānuṣā devān arcayanti śubhārthinaḥ
tān arcayanti hy amarās tathā rājañ śubhārthinaḥ
pitṛkṛtyeṣu devānāṃ saṃnyāsaṃ ye tv anuṣṭhitāḥ
svādhyāyavantaḥ kauravya sadā niyamacāriṇaḥ
gandharvādhipatiḥ śrīmāṃs tatra citraratho nṛpa
saputro vādayām āsa devavādyāni hṛṣṭavat
ūrṇāyuś citrasenaś ca hāhā hūhūs tathaiva ca
ḍambaras tumburuś caiva jagur anye ca tadgaṇāḥ
urvaśī pūrvacittiś ca hemā rambhā ca bhārata
hemadantā ghṛtācī ca sahajanyā tathaiva ca
jujoṣa bhagavān devas tadupasthānam ātmavān
vṛttena tuṣṭaḥ śakrasya jagāma jagataḥ patiḥ
gate bhūtapatau sarve nṛpā jagmur yathāgatam
mahendreṇārcitā devāḥ svān eva nilayān gatāḥ
tataḥ sarveṣu yāteṣu sukhāsīnaṃ puraṃdaram
sadasyaiḥ svaiḥ sahāsīnaṃ nārado 'bhyāyayau muniḥ
tam indraḥ pūjayām āsa samutthāya tapodhanam
dideśa kuśagarbhaṃ ca pīṭham ātmāsanopamam
nārado 'tha mahātejā mahendram idam abravīt
dūto 'ham amaraśreṣṭha viṣṇor atulatejasaḥ
kiṃcit kāryaṃ puraskṛtya preṣito 'smi mahātmanā
ānartād ārtiharaṇaṃ tasyaivānaghatejasaḥ
prītivākyāni hṛdyāni prayujya munaye tadā
tataḥ prahṛṣṭo bhagavān abravīt pākaśāsanaḥ
kim āha puruṣaśreṣṭhaḥ śīghram ācakṣva me mune
cirasya khalu kṛṣṇena saṃsmṛtāḥ sma mahātmanā
priyavākyāni hṛdyāni brūhi dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
nārada uvāca
mahendrendrānujaṃ draṣṭuṃ gato 'haṃ bhrātaraṃ tava
dvārakāṃ puruṣaśreṣṭha kāśyapānāṃ yaśaskaram
taṃ tu raivatake 'drākṣaṃ tadāsīnam ariṃdamam
rukmiṇyā sahitaṃ vīram umayeva vṛṣadhvajam
pārijātataroḥ puṣpaṃ tasya dattaṃ mayānagha
vismāpanārthaṃ deveśa patnīnām urutejasaḥ
tad dṛṣṭvā tasya patnyas tu vismayaṃ paramaṃ yayuḥ
bahukāmapradaṃ puṣpaṃ vṛkṣarājasamudbhavam
guṇās tāsāṃ mayākhyātās tasya puṣpasya mānada
sṛṣṭiś ca pārijātasya kaśyapenātitejasā
adityā kaśyapo dattaḥ puṇyārthaṃ ca yathā mama
puṣpadāmnā veṣṭayitvā kaṇṭhe puṇyārtham ātmavān
tvaṃ ca datto yathā śacyā devāś cānye sureśvara
niṣkrayaś ca yathā dattaḥ kaśyapādyair mahātmabhiḥ
tac chrutvā tasya patny ekā satyabhāmeti viśrutā
puṇyakārthaṃ manaś cakre dayitā te yavīyasaḥ
tayā cābhyarthito bhartā devyā devagaṇeśvaraḥ
pratijajñe sa dharmātmā yavīyāṃs tava mānada
tato mām uktavān vīro viṣṇur balavatāṃ varaḥ
yathāvat suramukhyeśa bruvataḥ śṛṇu bhāvana
lālanīyo yavīyāṃs tu praṇipatyācyuto 'bravīt
ānāyaya suraśreṣṭha pārijātaṃ varadrumam
manoratho 'stu saphalo vadhvās te 'surasūdana
dharmakṛtye viśeṣeṇa vadhvās te 'marasattama
ayaṃ durlabhakalyāṇo loke lokagaṇeśvara
paśyantv amarakalyāṇaṃ matprabhāvāc ca mānuṣāḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
vāsudevavacaḥ śrutvā mahendraḥ kurunandana
nāradaṃ vadatāṃ śreṣṭham idaṃ vākyam athābravīt
bhajāsanaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha śrutam uktaṃ tvayā dvija
saṃdeśaṃ pratidāsyāmi viṣṇor atulatejasaḥ
āsīne nārade śakro labdhānujño 'tha nāradāt
svam āsanaṃ tato bheje tasyaiva sadṛśaṃ vibho
upaviṣṭaḥ surapatir athovāca tapodhanam
nirīkṣya svabalaṃ vīryaṃ pārṣadaṃ vṛtranāśanaḥ
maharṣe kuśalaṃ pṛṣṭvā vaktavyas te janārdanaḥ
vacanān mama dharmajña sarvabhūtasukhāvaham
madanantaram īśas tvaṃ jagato nātra saṃśayaḥ
tvadīyaḥ pārijātaś ca ratnāny anyāni cācyuta
tvaṃ tu bhārāvataraṇaṃ kartuṃ deva mahīṃ gataḥ
mānuṣyaṃ sarvabhūtānām āsthitaḥ kāryasiddhaye
tvayi tīrṇapratijñe hi punaḥ prāpte triviṣṭapam
pūrayiṣyāmi vadhvās te iṣṭān kāmān adhokṣaja
svargīyāṇi na ratnāni nayitavyāni keśava
svalpārthe mānuṣaṃ lokam iti pūrvakṛtā sthitiḥ
utkramya hi sthitiṃ daivīṃ pravartāmi mahābala
yady ahaṃ kiṃ pravakṣyanti prajāpatigaṇāḥ prabho
brahmaṇā sahaputreṇa sapautreṇa mahātmanā
niyamāḥ sarvakṛtyānāṃ sthāpitā jagato dhruvāḥ
prajāpatikṛtaṃ mārgam apāsya vrajato mama
śrutvā prajāpatir dhīmāñ śāpam apy utsṛjet prabhuḥ
asmābhir bhidyamānaṃ hi māryādasetubandhanam
bhetsyanty aśaṅkitā daityā daityapakṣās tathāpare
strīnimittam ito nīte pārijāte drumeśvare
svargaukaso bhaviṣyanti vimanaskāś ca mānada
upabhogā manuṣyāṇāṃ vihitā ye svayaṃbhuvā
tais tu tuṣyatu me bhrātā saṃpaśyan kālaparyayam
ihāpi tāvat tridive mama yaḥ syāt parigrahaḥ
tridivastho 'pi taṃ kṛṣṇaḥ sarvaṃ bhoktum ihārhati
tṛpto hy āmiṣabhojyānām abhimānāj janardanaḥ
tato dharmaṃ samutsṛjya pāpam evānuvartate
strīvaśyatā khyāpyamānā kṛṣṇasya hi mahātmanaḥ
jagaty ayaśaso yogaṃ janayed iti me matiḥ
mānuṣyaṃ mānuṣe prāpto yad etan madhusūdanaḥ
kuryān nirbandhanīyaṃ yad bhrātrā jyeṣṭhena nārada
svargaratnavilopena dharṣaṇā syān mamānagha
jñātito dharṣaṇā caiva viśeṣeṇa hi garhitā
dharmam arthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca krameṇa madhusūdanaḥ
sevatv eṣa satāṃ dharmān sthāpitān padmayoninaḥ
mahītalaṃ pārijātam arpayiṣyāmi te yadi
paulomīm āditaḥ kṛtvā ko nu māṃ bahu maṃsyate
pārijātaṃ mahīpṛṣṭhe dṛṣṭvā spṛṣṭvā ca mānuṣāḥ
svargārthaṃ nodyamiṣyanti dṛṣṭvā svargaphalaṃ kṣitau
pārijātaguṇān martyā juṣanti yadi nārada
devānāṃ manuṣāṇāṃ ca na viśeṣo bhaviṣyati
tatra yat kriyate karma iha tad bhujyate naraiḥ
svargārthaṃ na yatiṣyanti pārijātaguṇānvitāḥ
sarvaratnavaraḥ svarge pārijātas tapodhana
tulyaṃ devasamair martyaiḥ sarvadaiva jagad bhavet
yajñair martyā na yakṣyanti labdhasvargaphalā bhuvi
na pūrtāni pradāsyanti tulyatvam amarair gatāḥ
yajñair japyāhnikaiś caiva nityam āpyāyayanti naḥ
mānuṣāḥ svargam icchantaḥ śraddadhānās tapodhana
tat sarvaṃ na kariṣyanti pārijātaguṇānvitāḥ
nistejaso bhaviṣyāmas te gatās tadvihīnatām
itaḥ suvṛṣṭyā sasyais te jīvanti puruṣā bhuvi
āpyāyayantas te 'py asmān dānair yajñais tathaiva ca
na bubhukṣā pipāsā vā bādhate yadi mānuṣān
rogo jarā vā dharmajña mṛtyur vā ratir eva vā
daurgandhyaṃ vā sughorā va ītayaḥ karmasaṃbhavāḥ
kim udyogaṃ kariṣyanti pārijātaguṇānvitāḥ
sarvathā nayanaṃ tatra pārijātasya na kṣamam
iti vācyas tvayā vipra viṣṇur akliṣṭakarmakṛt
yathā yathā ca me bhrātā tuṣyaty etad vicārayan
tathā tathā tvayā kāryaṃ kāryaṃ matprītim icchatā
hārāṃś ca maṇayaś caiva candanāny agurūṇi ca
vastrāṇi ca vicitrāṇi vadhvās tvaṃ dvārakāṃ naya
yogyāni yāni martyānāṃ yavad icchati keśavaḥ
na svargaparimoṣaṃ tu kartum arhati keśavaḥ
dadāmi ratnāni yathepsitāny ahaṃ
bahūni citrāṇi vibhūṣaṇāni ca
na pārijātaṃ ca kathaṃcana drumaṃ
mune pradāsyāmi divaukasāṃ priyam
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
devarājavacaḥ śrutvā nāradaḥ kurunandana
provāca vākyaṃ vākyajño mahātmā dharmavittamaḥ
avaśyam eva vaktavyaṃ hitaṃ balaniṣūdana
mayā tava mahābāho bahumāno 'sti me tvayi
ukto mayā vāsudevo jānatā bhavato matam
na dattaḥ pārijāto hi harasyāpi tvayā purā
hetavaś ca mayā tasya darśitā bhoḥ samāsataḥ
na cāvagatavān devaḥ satyam etad bravīmi te
upendro 'haṃ mahendreṇa lālanīyaḥ sadeti mām
athāha puṇḍarīkākṣas tat tad uttaram eva ca
punaḥ punar mayā cāsya hetavo deva darśitāḥ
tato na buddhir vyāvṛttā vṛtranāśana tasya vai
api cāpy uktavān devo vākyaṃ te madhusūdanaḥ
prahasya puruṣaśreṣṭhaḥ saroṣam iva vāsavaḥ
na devagandharvagaṇā na rākṣasā
na cāsurā naiva ca pannagottamāḥ
mama pratijñām apahantum udyatā
mune samarthāḥ khalu bhadram astu te
sa pārijātaṃ yadi na pradāsyati
prayācyamāno bhavatāmareśvaraḥ
tataḥ śacīvyāmṛditānulepane
gadāṃ vimokṣyāmi puraṃdarorasi
upendrasya mahendrāyaṃ bhrātus te niścayaḥ paraḥ
yad atra manyase nyāyyaṃ saṃpradhārya kuruṣva tat
tattvaṃ hitaṃ ca deveśa śrūyatāṃ vadato mama
nayanaṃ pārijātasya dvārakāṃ mama rocate
nāradenaivam uktas tu pravyaktaṃ baladehabhit
roṣāviṣṭaḥ sahasrākṣo 'bravīd etan narādhipa
anāgasi mayi jyeṣṭhe sodare yadi keśavaḥ
evaṃ pravṛttaḥ kiṃ śakyaṃ kartum adya tapodhana
bahūni pratilomāni purā sa kṛtavān mayi
kṛṣṇo nārada soḍhāni bhrāteti sma mayānagha
khāṇḍave cārjunarathaṃ purā vāhayatā satā
madīyā vāritā meghāḥ śamayanto 'gnim uddhatam
govardhanaṃ dhārayatās vipriyaṃ ca kṛtaṃ mama
tathā vṛtravadhe prāpte sāhāyyārthaṃ vṛto mayā
samo 'ham iti sarveṣāṃ bhūtānām iti coktavān
svabāhubalam āśritya vṛtraś ca nihato mayā
devāsureṣu prāpteṣu saṃgrāmeṣu ca nārada
yudhyaty ātmecchayā kṛṣṇo mune suviditaṃ tava
bahunātra kim uktena tasmād iṣṭyā pravartatām
jñātibhedo na me kāryaḥ sākṣī tvaṃ mama nārada
mamorasi gadāṃ moktum udyato yadi keśavaḥ
anuśocyātha paulomī guṇaḥ ka iha dṛśyate
udavāsagato dhīmān pitā naḥ kaśyapaḥ prabhuḥ
adityā saha me mātrā tayor vācyam idaṃ bhavet
ajitātmā mama bhrātā rajasā mahatā vṛtaḥ
kāmena ca striyā vākyād evaṃ mām uktavān gurum
sarvathā dhik striyo vipra dhig rajastamasī tathā
yatrādhikṣiptavān viṣṇur evaṃ māṃ strījito dvija
na dṛṣṭaṃ kaśyapakulaṃ vyapadeśyaṃ mahāmune
naiva dakṣakulaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ mātur me yatra saṃbhavaḥ
na jyeṣṭhatā na rājatvaṃ devānāṃ pratimānitam
kāmarāgābhibhūtena kṛṣṇena khalu nārada
putradārasahasrair hi bhrātānagha viśiṣyate
sadvṛtto jñānasaṃpanna iti brahmā purābravīt
nāsti bhrātṛsamo bandhur āhārya itaro janaḥ
iti mām abravīn mātā pitā caiva prajāpatiḥ
sodareṣu viśeṣaṃ tu pitā me kaśyapo 'bravīt
dṛptā mayā virudhyante dānavāḥ pāpaniścayāḥ
kāmam etan na vaktavyaṃ svayam ātmastavānvitam
prāptas tv avasaro vipra yad ihādyocyate mayā
dhanur jyāyāṃ muniśreṣṭha cchinnāyāṃ hi purānagha
dhanvibhir amarāṇāṃ ca varadānān mahāmate
utkṛttaśiraso viṣṇoḥ purā deho dhṛto mayā
saṃdhitaṃ ca śiro yatnāc chinnaṃ raudreṇa tejasā
ahaṃ viśiṣṭo devānām ity uktvā punar acyutaḥ
dhanur āropya darpeṇa sthito nārada keśavaḥ
kiṃ māṃ pitā vā mātā va vakṣyatīti mayā mune
snehena vidhṛtaṃ viṣṇoḥ śarīraṃ munisattama
aindraṃ vaiṣṇavam asyaiva mune bhāgam ahaṃ dadau
yavīyāṃsam ahaṃ premṇā kṛṣṇaṃ paśyāmi nārada
saṃgrāmeṣu prahartavyaṃ tena pūrvaṃ tapodhana
rājā kilāhaṃ samare praharāmy agrato dhruvam
prādurbhāveṣu sarveṣu svaśarīram ivānagha
yatto rakṣāmi dharmajña keśavaṃ bhaktim āśritam
idaṃ bhaṅktvā madīyaṃ ca bhagavan viṣṇunā kṛtam
uparyupari lokānāṃ adhikaṃ bhavanaṃ mune
avamānaḥ sa ca mayā pṛṣṭhataḥ kriyate mune
lālanīyo mayā bāla ity evaṃ bhrātṛgauravāt
bālo 'yaṃ mama putreti yavīyān iti nārada
pitrā mātrā ca govindo nātīva paribhāṣitaḥ
iṣṭas tatra jananyāḥ sa keśavaḥ saviśeṣataḥ
vayaṃ dveṣyā na saṃdehas tatra sneho 'tiricyate
sarvajño balavāñ śūraḥ pātraṃ mānayitā tathā
keśavety eva ca dhyānaṃ yat tad vitathatāṃ gatam
gaccha nārada vaktavyaḥ keśavo vacanān mama
āhūto na nivarteyaṃ samaraṃ prati śatrubhiḥ
yadīcchasi tad āgaccha sahyaṃ te yat tvam icchasi
praharasva ca pūrvaṃ tvaṃ bhāryājita yathecchasi
rathāṅgenātha śārṅgeṇa gadayā nandakena vā
praharāruhya garuḍaṃ dṛḍho bhūtvā janārdana
prahṛte prahariṣyāmi yathāśaktyā ca keśava
aho dhig yadi māṃ sneho viklavaṃ na kariṣyati
yāvan na saṃgrāmagato jito 'haṃ cakrapāṇinā
pārijātaṃ na dāsyāmi tāvad bho munisattama
māṃ samāhvayate jyeṣṭhaṃ yavīyāṃsas tapodhana
ahaṃ taṃ marṣayiṣyāmi kimarthaṃ strījitaṃ harim
adyaiva gaccha bhagavan dvārakāṃ kṛṣṇapālitām
vivādaḥ saṃsthitaḥ so 'dya iti vācyas tvayācyutaḥ
palāśapatrārdham api tvayājito
na pārijātasya tava pradāsyati
iti pravācyo madhusūdanas tvayā
vaco madīyaṃ smaratā tapodhana
punaḥ pravācyo bhagavaṃs tvayācyuto
mama priyārthaṃ khalu nirviśaṅkitam
na māyayā hartum ihārhasi drumaṃ
suyuddham evāstu dhig astu jihmatām
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
mahendravacanaṃ śrutvā nārado vadatāṃ varaḥ
vivikte devarājānam idaṃ vacanam abravīt
kāmaṃ priyāṇi rājāno vaktavyā nātra saṃśayaḥ
prāptakālaṃ tu vaktavyaṃ hitam apriyam acyuta
aniyuktaḥ purobhāgo na syād iti vadanti hi
sa lokagatitattvajño nayavijñānakovidaḥ
kāryākārye samutpanne paripṛcchati māṃ bhavān
yatas tataḥ pravakṣyāmi gṛhyatāṃ yadi rocate
anuktenāpi suhṛdā vaktavyaṃ jānatā hitam
nyāyyaṃ ca prāptakālaṃ ca parābhavam anicchatā
vaktavyaṃ sarvathā sadbhir apriyaṃ cāpi yad dhitam
ānṛṇyam etat snehasya sadbhir evādṛtaṃ purā
anṛte dharmabhagne ca na śuśrūṣati cāpriye
na priyaṃ na hitaṃ vācyaṃ sadbhir ete vininditāḥ
sarvathā deva vaktavyaṃ śrūyatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ vara
śrutvā ca kuru sarvajña mama śreyaskaraṃ vacaḥ
anyonyabhedo bhrātṝṇāṃ suhṛdāṃ vā balāntaka
bhavaty anandakṛd deva dviṣatāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
hitānubandhasahitaṃ kāryaṃ jñeyaṃ sureśvara
viparītaṃ ca tad buddhvā nityaṃ buddhimatāṃ vara
yat syāt tāpakaraṃ paścād ārabdhaṃ kāryam īdṛśam
ārabhen naiva tad vidvān eṣa buddhimatāṃ nayaḥ
vipākam asya kāryasya nānupaśyāmi śobhanam
yat tu tatkāraṇaṃ deva nibodha vibudhādhipa
ya eko viśvam adhyāste pradhānaṃ jagato hariḥ
prakṛtyā yaṃ paraṃ sarve kṣetrajñaṃ vai vidur budhāḥ
tasyāvyaktasya yo vyakto bhāgaḥ sarvabhavodbhavaḥ
tasyātmā prathamo devo viṣṇuḥ sarvasya dhīmataḥ
prakṛtyāḥ prathamo bhāga umā devī yaśasvinī
vyaktaḥ sarvamayo viṣṇuḥ strīsaṃjño lokabhāvanaḥ
rukmiṇyādyāḥ striyas tasya vyaktatve prathamo guṇaḥ
avyayā prakṛtir devī guṇadevo maheśvaraḥ
na viśeṣo 'sti rudrasya viṣṇoś cāmarasattama
guṇinaś cāvyayaḥ śaśvat sadā ca prathamo guṇaḥ
nārāyaṇo mahātejāḥ sarvakṛl lokabhāvanaḥ
bhoktā maheśvaro devaḥ kartā viṣṇur adhokṣajaḥ
brahmā devagaṇāś cānye paścāt sṛṣṭā mahātmanā
mahādevena deveśa prajāpatigaṇās tathā
evaṃ purāṇapuruṣo viṣṇur deveṣu paṭhyate
acintyaś cāprameyaś ca guṇebhyaś ca paras tathā
adityā tapasā viṣṇur mahātmārādhitaḥ purā
vareṇa cchanditā tena parituṣṭena cāditiḥ
tayoktas tvām ahaṃ putram icchāmīti surottama
praṇataṃ deva vijñāya nārāyaṇam adhokṣajam
tenoktā bhuvane nāsti matsamaḥ puruṣo 'paraḥ
aṃśena tu bhaviṣyāmi putraḥ khalv aham eva te
sa jātaḥ sarvakṛd devo bhrātā tava sureśvara
nārāyaṇo mahātejā yam upendraṃ pracakṣate
icchann eva harir devaḥ kāśyapatvam upāgataḥ
tais tair bhāvair vikurute bhūtabhavyabhavo 'vyayaḥ
prādurbhāvaṃ gato devo jagato hitakāmyayā
māthuraṃ jagato nāthaḥ kartā hartā ca keśavaḥ
yathā ca tilapiṇḍaḥ syād vyāptaḥ snehena mānada
tathā jagad idaṃ vyāptaṃ viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
brahmaṇyadevaḥ sarvātmā tais tair bhāvair vikurvate
jagaty atiguṇo devo vaikuṇṭhaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ
ataḥ samastadevānāṃ pūjya eva ca keśavaḥ
padmanābhaś ca bhagavān prajāsargakaro vibhuḥ
ananto dhāraṇārthaṃ ca bibharti ca mahad yaśaḥ
yajña ity api sadbhiś ca kathyate vedavādibhiḥ
śvetaḥ kṛtayuge devo raktas tretāyuge tathā
dvāpare ca yathā pītaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ kaliyuge vibhuḥ
avadhīt sa hiraṇyākṣaṃ divyarūpadharo hariḥ
jaghne hiraṇyakaśipuṃ nārasiṃhavapur hariḥ
dadhārāpsu nimajjantīm eṣa devo vasuṃdharām
vārāhaṃ vapur āśritya jagato hitakāmyayā
jigāya jagatīṃ caiva viṣṇur vāmanarūpadhṛk
babandha ca baliṃ devaḥ śrīmān pannagabandhanaiḥ
devadānavasaṃbhūtām akāmayad api śriyam
tvayy āyattaḥ purā viṣṇur udāram ativikramaḥ
sāvaśeṣaṃ tapo yasya taṃ nihanti janārdanaḥ
alīkeṣv api vartantaṃ vrataṃ etan mahātmanaḥ
jaghne ca dānavān mukhyān devānāṃ ye ca śatravaḥ
tava priyārthaṃ govindo dharmanityaḥ satāṃ gatiḥ
rāmatvam api cāvāpya jaghne rāvaṇam ātmavān
bhūtvā kāmaguṇaś caiva jaghāna dviradaṃ hariḥ
hitāya jagato 'dyāpi loke vasati mānuṣe
upendro jagato nāthaḥ sarvabhūtottamottamaḥ
jaṭī kṛṣṇājinī daṇḍī dṛṣṭapūrvo mayā hariḥ
daiteyeṣu caran devas tṛṇeṣv agnir ivoddhataḥ
adrākṣam api govindaṃ dānavaikārṇavaṃ jagat
kurvāṇaṃ dānavair hīnaṃ jagato hitakāmyayā
avaśyaṃ pārijātaṃ te nayiṣyati janārdanaḥ
dvārakām amaraśreṣṭha nānṛtaṃ ca bravīmy aham
bhrātṛsnehābhibhūtas tvaṃ kṛṣṇe na prahariṣyasi
nāpi kṛṣṇas tvayi jyeṣṭha prahariṣyati vāsava
naiva cec chroṣyasi proktaṃ mayā deva kathaṃcana
pṛccha tvaṃ nayadharmajñān ye hitās tava mantriṇaḥ
nāradenaivam uktas tu mahendro janamejaya
idam uttaram īśo 'tha pratyuvāca jagadgurum
evaṃvidhaprabhāvaṃ tvaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ vadasi yad dvija
evam etat subahuśaḥ śrutaṃ khalu mayā mune
yataś caivaṃvidhaḥ kṛṣṇas tato 'haṃ tasya taṃ tarum
na pradāsyāmi dātavyaṃ satāṃ dharmam anusmaran
mahāprabhāvo nālpārthe ruṣyed iti vicintayan
vyavasthito 'haṃ bhadraṃ te mune sarvaguṇoditaḥ
mahāprabhāvāḥ satataṃ bhavanti hi sahiṣṇavaḥ
śrotāraś caiva satataṃ vṛddhānāṃ jñānacakṣuṣām
mahātmā kāraṇe nālpe kṛṣṇo dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
bhrātrā jyeṣṭhena dharmajño virodhaṃ gantum arhati
yathaiva mama mātuḥ sa varaṃ prādād adhokṣajaḥ
tathaiva tasyāḥ putrāṇāṃ jyeṣṭhānāṃ soḍhum arhati
yathaivopendratāṃ yātaḥ svayam icchañ janārdanaḥ
tathaiva bhrātur indrasya saṃmānaṃ kartum arhati
jyaiṣṭhyam etena devena nārabdhaṃ kiṃ purātane
athedānīm apīcchet sa jyeṣṭho 'stu madhusūdanaḥ
suniścitaṃ balaripum īkṣya nārado
visarjitas tridaśavareṇa dharmavit
yayau purīṃ yaduvṛṣabhābhirakṣitāṃ
kuśasthalīṃ dhṛtimatimāṃs tapodhanaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
athaitya dvārakāṃ ramyāṃ nārado munisattamaḥ
dadarśa puruṣaśreṣṭhaṃ nārāyaṇam ariṃdamam
svaveśmani sukhāsīnaṃ sahitaṃ satyabhāmayā
virājamānaṃ vapuṣā sarvatejotigāminā
tam evārthaṃ mahātmānaṃ cintayantaṃ dṛḍhavratam
kevalaṃ yojayantaṃ ca vākyamātreṇa bhāminīm
dṛṣṭvaiva nāradaṃ devaḥ pratyutthāya adhokṣajaḥ
pūjayām āsa ca tadā vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā
sukhopaviṣṭaṃ viśrāntaṃ prahasya madhusūdanaḥ
vṛttāntaṃ paripapraccha pārijātataruṃ prati
athovāca muniḥ sarvaṃ vistareṇa tapodhanaḥ
indrānujāyendravākyaṃ nikhilaṃ janamejaya
śrutvā kṛṣṇas tu tat sarvaṃ nāradaṃ vākyam abravīt
amarāvatīṃ purīṃ yāsye so 'haṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
ity uktvā nāradenaiva sahitaḥ sāgaraṃ yayau
saṃdideśa tatas tatra vivikte nāradaṃ hariḥ
mahendrabhavanaṃ gatvā vadasvādya tapodhana
abhivādya mahātmānaṃ madvākyam amarottamam
na yuddhe pramukhe śakra sthātum arhasi me prabho
pārijātasya nayane niścitaṃ tvam avehi mām
evam uktas tu kṛṣṇena nāradas tridivaṃ gataḥ
ācacakṣe ca kṛṣṇoktaṃ devendrasyāmitaujasaḥ
tato bṛhaspateḥ śakraḥ śaśaṃsa balanāśanaḥ
śrutvā bṛhaspatir devam uvāca kurunandana
aho dhig brahmasadanaṃ mayi yāte śatakrato
durnītam idam ārabdham atra bhedo hi dāruṇaḥ
anākhyāya kathaṃ nāma bhavatā bhuvaneśvara
mamaitat kṛtyam ārabdhaṃ deva kenāpi hetunā
atha vā bhavitavyena karmajena pramuhyate
jagadvṛtraghna na vidhiḥ śakyaḥ samativartitum
sahasaiva tu kāryāṇām prārambho na praśasyate
tad etat sahasārabdhaṃ kāryaṃ dāsyati lāghavam
bṛhaspatiṃ mahātmānaṃ mahendras tv abravīd vacaḥ
evaṃ gate 'dya yat kāryaṃ tad bhavān vaktum arhati
tam uvācātha dharmātmā gatānāgatatattvavit
adhomukhaś cintayitvā bṛhaspatir udāradhīḥ
yatasva sahaputreṇa yodhayasva janārdanam
tathā śakra kariṣyāmi yathā nyāyyaṃ bhaviṣyati
bṛhaspatis tv evam uktvā kṣīrodaṃ sāgaraṃ gataḥ
ācaṣṭa munaye sarvaṃ kaśyapāya mahātmane
tac chrutvā kaśyapaḥ kruddho bṛhaspatim abhāṣata
avaśyaṃ bhāvyam etad bhoḥ sarvathā nātra saṃśayaḥ
icchataḥ sadṛśīṃ bhāryāṃ maharṣer devaśarmaṇaḥ
apadhyānakṛto doṣaḥ pataty eṣa śatakratoḥ
asya doṣasya śāntyartham ārabdhaś ca mune mayā
udavāsaḥ sa doṣaś ca prāpta eva sudāruṇaḥ
tad gamiṣyāmi mātrāsya sahādityā tapodhana
ubhau tau vārayiṣyāmi daivaṃ saṃvadate yadi
bṛhaspatis tu dharmātmā mārīcam idam abravīt
prāptakālaṃ tvayā tatra bhavitavyaṃ tapodhana
tatheti kaśyapaś coktvā saṃprasthāpya bṛhaspatim
jagāmārcayituṃ devaṃ rudraṃ bhūtagaṇeśvaram
tatra somaṃ mahātmānam ānarca vṛṣabhadhvajam
varārtho kaśyapo dhīmān adityā sahitaḥ prabhuḥ
tuṣṭāva ca tam īśanaṃ mārīcaḥ kaśyapas tadā
vedoktaiḥ svakṛtaiś caiva stavaiḥ stavyaṃ jagadgurum
urukramaṃ viśvakarmāṇam īśaṃ
jagatsraṣṭāraṃ dharmadṛśyaṃ pareśam
sarveśaṃ tvāṃ dhṛtimaddhāma divyaṃ
viśveśvaraṃ bhagavantaṃ namasye
yo devānām adhipaḥ pāpahartā
tataṃ viśvaṃ yena jaganmayatvāt
āpo garbho yasya śubhā dharitryo
viśveśvaraṃ taṃ śaraṇam ahaṃ prapadye
śālāvṛkān yo yatirūpo nijaghne
dattān indreṇa praṇudo 'hitānām
virūpākṣaṃ sudarśanaṃ puṇyayoniṃ
viśveśvaraṃ yāmi mūrdhnā prapadye
bhuṅkte ya eko vibhur jagato viśvam agryaṃ
dhāmnāṃ dhāma sukṛtitvān na dhṛṣyaḥ
puṣyāt sa māṃ mahasā śāśvatena
somapānāṃ marīcipānāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
atharvāṇaṃ suśirasaṃ bhūtayoniṃ
kṛtinaṃ vīraṃ dānavānāṃ ca bādham
viyajjuṣṭaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ vaikṛtaṃ ca
viśveśvaraṃ śaraṇaṃ yāmi devam
jagajjālaṃ vitataṃ yatra viśvaṃ
viśvātmānaṃ prītidevaṃ natānām
yad ūrdhvagaṃ ratham āsthāya yāti
viśveśvaraḥ sa sumanā me 'stu nityam
antaścaraṃ rocanaṃ cāruśākhaṃ
mahābalaṃ dharmanetāram ādyam
sahasranetraṃ śatavartmānam ugraṃ
mahādevaṃ viśvasṛjaṃ namasye
śociṣkeśaṃ śamanaṃ śāntapāpaṃ
śarvaṃ śaṃbhuṃ śaṃkaraṃ bhūtanātham
dhuraṃdharaṃ gopatiṃ candracihnaṃ
hṛṣīkāṇām ayanaṃ yāmi mūrdhnā
āśuḥśaśinaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ roruvāṇaṃ
kṛtaṃ dharmaṃ vitathaṃ nāśuśeṣam
vasuṃdharaṃ samṛḍīkaṃ samarthaṃ
dhṛtavrataṃ śūladharaṃ prapadye
anantavīryaṃ dhṛtakarmāṇam ādyaṃ
yajñasyejaṃ yajatāṃ cātiyājyam
havirbhujaṃ bhuvanānāṃ sadaiva
jyeṣṭhaṃ dvijaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ prapadye
paraṃ guṇebhyaḥ pṛśnigarbhasvarūpaṃ
yaśaḥśṛṅgaṃ vyūhanaṃ kāntarūpam
nabho vṛṇvānaṃ puruṣaṃ satyadhāma
saṃmohanaṃ duṣkṛtināṃ namasye
yuktoṃkāraṃ suśirasaṃ cārukarma
dṛḍhavrataṃ dṛḍhadhanvānam ājau
śūraṃ vettāraṃ dhanuṣo 'strātirekaṃ
patiṃ paśūnāṃ śamanaṃ namasye
eko 'rātiś caiva bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ
sarvātithir yo hi juṣaty arighnaḥ
aruṃtudo 'nuttamaḥ saṃvibhāgī
vibhājako māṃ bhagavān pātu devaḥ
ya eko yāti jagatāṃ viśvam īśo
ya eko 'dān marutāṃ prāṇam agryam
yenānṛśaṃsyāc chāśvataṃ sāma juṣṭaṃ
sa māṃ juṣyāt sukṛtī śreyase saḥ
brahmāsṛjad yo bhuvanottamottamaṃ
tṛpto vidvān brāhmaṇaḥ ṣaḍguṇasya
sraṣṭāraṃ taṃ vyāhṛtisthaṃ samagraṃ
sa māṃ pāyād bahurūpair ihāṅgaiḥ
vyañjano 'jano 'tha vidvān samagraḥ
spṛśiḥ śaṃbhuḥ prāṇadaḥ kṛttivāsāḥ
raso dhruvaḥ pavamānasya bhartā
sapatnīśaḥ śaṃkaraḥ sāradhātā
tryambakaṃ puṣṭidaṃ vo bruvāṇaṃ
dharmaṃ viprāṇāṃ varadaṃ yajvanāṃ ca
varād varaṃ raṇajetāram īśaṃ
devaṃ devānāṃ śaraṇaṃ yāmi rudram
āsyaṃ devānām antakaṃ duṣkṛtīnāṃ
trivṛtsomaṃ vṛkṣahaṃ karmasākṣim
bhūtāyanaṃ bhūtapatiṃ guṇajñaṃ
guṇākāraṃ śaraṇaṃ yāmi rudram
anuddhataṃ yajñakartāram antaṃ
madhyaṃ cādyaṃ jagato 'sāmyarūpam
devavrateṣu bahudhā gītam īśam
abhi triviṣṭapaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāmi rudram
mahājinaṃ vratinaṃ mekhalālaṃ
sutoṣaṇaṃ krodhadhanaṃ vipāpam
bhūtaṃ kṣetrajñaṃ guṇinaṃ vā kapardinaṃ
nato 'smīśaṃ vandanaṃ vandanānām
devaṃ devānāṃ pāvanaṃ pāvanānāṃ
kṛtiṃ kṛtīnāṃ mahato mahāntam
śatātmānaṃ saṃstutaṃ gopatīnāṃ
patiṃ devaṃ śaraṇaṃ yāmi rudram
antaścaraṃ puruṣaṃ guhyasaṃjñaṃ
prabhāsvantaṃ praṇavaṃ dhīpradīpam
hetuṃ paraṃ paramasyākṣarasya
śubhaṃ devaṃ guṇinaṃ saṃnato 'smi
prasūtir ubhayor na prasūtiś ca sūkṣmaḥ
pṛthag bhūtebhyo na pṛthak caikabhūtaḥ
svayaṃbhūtaḥ pātu māṃ sarvasāraḥ
pradaḥ svādaḥ saṃmadaḥ pātu ratnam
āsannaḥ sannataraḥ sādhakānāṃ
śraddhāvatāṃ śrāddhavṛttipraṇetā
patir gaṇānāṃ mahatāṃ satkṛtīnāṃ
pāyān meśaḥ pūraṇaḥ ṣaḍguṇānām
antar bahir vṛjinānāṃ nihantā
svayaṃ kartā bhūtabhāvī vikurvan
dhṛtāyudhaḥ sukṛtinām uttamaujāḥ
praṇudyān me vṛjinaṃ devadevaḥ
yenoddhṛtās traipurā māyino vai
dagdhā ghoreṇa vitathāntāḥ śareṇa
mahat kurvanto vṛjinaṃ devatānāṃ
sa mām īśaḥ pātu viśvasya dhātā
bhāgīyasāṃ bhāgamato 'ntam icchan
makho dākṣo yena kṛtto 'nvadhāvat
vidvān yajñasyādir athāntaḥ sa devaḥ
pāyād īśo māṃ dakṣayajñāntahetuḥ
anyo dhanyaḥ saṃkṛtaś cottamaś ca
jagat sṛṣṭvā yo 'tti sarvātiguhyam
sa māṃ mukhapramukhe pātu nityaṃ
vicinvānaḥ prathamaḥ ṣaḍguṇānām
guṇatraikālyaṃ yasya devasya nityaṃ
sattvodreko yasya bhāvāt prasūtaḥ
gopto goptṝṇāṃ sādano duṣkṛtīnām
ādyo viśvasya dhāvamānasya kruddhaḥ
dhāmno yasya harir agro 'tha viśvo
brahmā putraiḥ sahitaś ca dvijāś ca
parābhūtā bhuvane yasya somo
juṣatv eṣa śreyase sādhugoptā
yasmād bhūtānāṃ bhūtir anto 'tha madhyaṃ
dhṛtir bhūtir yaś ca guhā śrutiś ca
guhābhūteṣu puruṣeśvarasya
mahātmanaḥ sa mṛḍavedyasya tasya
yal liṅgāṅkaṃ tryambakaḥ sarvam īśo
bhagāṅkaṃ yat tad dhy umā sarvadhātrī
nānyat tṛtīyaṃ jagatīhāsti kiṃcin
mahādevāt sarvasarveśvaro 'sau
iti saṃstūyamānas tu bhagavān vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
darśayām āsa dharmātmā kaśyapaṃ dharmabhṛdvaram
uvāca cainaṃ deveśaḥ prasannenāntarātmanā
yena saṃstauṣi kāryeṇa tvaṃ taj jāne prajāpate
indropendrau mahātmānau devau prakṛtim eṣyataḥ
pārijātaṃ tu dharmātmā nayiṣyati janārdanaḥ
apadhyāto mahendro hi muninā devaśarmaṇā
asyākāṅkṣat purā bhāryāṃ tapodīptasya kaśyapa
gamyatāṃ tatra dharmajña dākṣāyaṇyā saha tvayā
adityā śakrasadanaṃ śreyas te putrayor dhruvam
iti haravacanaṃ niśamya vidvān
kamalabhavātmajasūnur aprameyaḥ
tridaśagaṇaguruṃ praṇamya rudraṃ
muditamanāḥ svam atho gṛhaṃ jagāma
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
atha viṣṇur mahātejā muhūrtābhyudite ravau
mṛgayāvyapadeśena yayau raivatakaṃ girim
āropyaikarathe devaḥ sātyakiṃ narapuṃgavam
pradyumnam anugaccheti proktvā kurukulodvaha
raivataṃ ca giriṃ devo gatvā dārukam abravīt
madīyaṃ ratham etaṃ taṃ tvaṃ gṛhītvehaiva dāruka
pratipālaya māṃ saumya dinārdhaṃ cārayan harīn
rathenaiva praveṣṭāhaṃ dvārakāṃ sūtasattama
iti saṃdiśya bhagavān āruroha jayodyataḥ
tārkṣyaṃ sasātyakir dhīmān aprameyaparākramaḥ
pṛthag rathena kauravya pradyumnaḥ śatrusūdanaḥ
ākāśagāminā rājan pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛṣṇam anviyāt
nimeṣāntaramātreṇa nandanaṃ kānanaṃ hariḥ
devodyānaṃ yayau dhīmān pārijātajihīrṣayā
dadarśa yatra bhagavān devayodhān durāsadān
nānāyudhadharān vīrān nandanasthān adhokṣajaḥ
teṣāṃ saṃpaśyatām eva pārijātaṃ mahābalaḥ
utpāṭyārpayām āsa pārijātaṃ sātāṃ gatiḥ
garuḍaṃ pakṣirājānam ayatnenaiva bhārata
upasthito vigrahavān pārijātaś ca keśavam
sāntvito vāsudevena pārijātaś ca bhārata
uktaś ca vṛkṣa mā bhais tvaṃ keśavena mahātmanā
taṃ prasthitaṃ taruṃ dṛṣṭvā pārijātam adhokṣajaḥ
amarāvatīṃ purīṃ śreṣṭhāṃ tataś cakre pradakṣiṇam
te tu nandanagoptāraḥ pārijātaṃ drumottamam
hriyateti mahendrāya gatvā nṛpa śaśaṃsire
athairāvatam āruhya niryayau pākaśāsanaḥ
jayantena rathasthena pṛṣṭhato 'nugataḥ prabhuḥ
pūrvam abhyāgataṃ dvāraṃ keśavaṃ śatrusūdanam
dṛṣṭvovāca pravṛttaṃ bhoḥ kim idaṃ madhusūdana
praṇamya garuḍastho 'tha keśavaḥ śakram abravīt
vadhvās te puṇyakārthāya nīyate 'yaṃ varadrumaḥ
tam uvāca tataḥ śakro mā maivaṃ puṣkarekṣaṇa
ayodhayitvā na tarur nayitavyas tvayācyuta
praharasva mahābāho prathamaṃ mayi keśava
pratijñā saphalā te 'stu muktvā kaumodakīm api
tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śarais tīkṣṇair devarājagajottamam
bibhedāśanisaṃkāśaiḥ prahasann iva bhārata
vivyādha garuḍaṃ vajrī divyaiḥ śaravarais tathā
bāṇāṃś ca cchedayām āsa keśavasya tarasvinaḥ
yān yān mumoca devendras tāṃs tāṃś ciccheda mādhavaḥ
mādhavena prayuktāṃś ca ciccheda balavṛtrahā
mahendrasya ca śabdena dhanuṣaḥ kurunandana
śārṅgasya ca ninādena mumuhuḥ svargavāsinaḥ
tayor vartati saṃgrāme garuḍasthaṃ mahābalaḥ
pārijātaṃ jayanto 'tha hartum abhyudito balī
pradyumnam atha kaṃsaghno vārayeti tam abravīt
tatas taṃ vārayām āsa raukmiṇeyaḥ pratāpavān
jayanto jayatāṃ śreṣṭho raukmiṇeyam atheṣubhiḥ
sarvagātreṣu vihasann ājaghāna rathe sthitaḥ
rathastha eva rathinaṃ kāmas tu kamalekṣaṇaḥ
aindrim abhyardayām āsa bāṇair āśīviṣopamaiḥ
sa saṃnipātas tumulo babhūva kurunandana
jayantasya ca vīrasya raukmiṇeyasya cobhayoḥ
kṛtapratikṛtaṃ yuddhe cakratus tau mahābalau
mahendropendratanayau jagaty astrabhṛtāṃ varau
devāś ca munayaś caiva dadṛśur vismayānvitāḥ
taṃ saṃgrāmaṃ mahāghoraṃ siddhāś caiva sacāraṇāḥ
tatas tu pravaro nāma devadūto mahābalaḥ
pārijātaṃ punar hartum iyeṣa kurunandana
sakhā sa devarājasya mahāstravid ariṃdamaḥ
avadhyo varadānena brahmaṇaḥ kurunandana
brāhmaṇas tapasā siddho jambudvīpād divaṃ gataḥ
svaśaktyā nṛpa saṃyātaḥ sakhitvaṃ balaghātinaḥ
tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya kṛṣṇaḥ sātyakim abravīt
rathastha eva pravaraṃ śarair vāraya sātyake
na tv eva nirdayaṃ bāṇā moktavyāḥ sātyake tvayā
asya brāhmaṇacāpalyaṃ soḍhavyaṃ khalu sarvathā
tataḥ ṣaṣṭyā tatheṣūṇāṃ garuḍasthaṃ dvijas tadā
ājaghāna mahābāho sātyakiṃ pravaro bhṛśam
śiner naptā tatas tasya kṣipataḥ sāyakān nṛpa
ciccheda puruṣavyāghro vacanaṃ cedam abravīt
brāhmaṇo nābhihantavyas tiṣṭha vipra svavartmani
avadhyā yādavānāṃ hi svaparādhe 'pi hi dvijāḥ
pravaras tu prahasyainam uvāca kurunandana
alaṃ kṣāntyā nṛṇāṃ śūra yudhya sarvātmanā raṇe
jāmadagnyasya rāmasya śiṣyo 'ham api yādava
nāmataḥ pravaro nāma sakhā śakrasya dhīmataḥ
na devā yoddhum icchanti manyanto madhusūdana
ānṛṇyaṃ sauhrdasyāham adya gantāsmi mādhava
tatas tayos tadā raudraḥ saṃgrāmo vavṛdhe nṛpa
astrair divyair naravyāghra śaineyadvijamukhyayoḥ
dyauś cacāla tadā rājan dyucarāś ca sahasraśaḥ
tasmin vartati saṃgrāme teṣām atimahātmanām
nātiśiṣye raṇe kārṣṇir aindram astrabhṛtāṃ varaṃ
aindriḥ kārṣṇiṃ mahātmānaṃ māyinaṃ śūrasaṃmatam
hanta gṛhṇa pratīccheti tāv ubhau yodhasattamau
yuyudhāte naraśreṣṭha parasparajayaiṣiṇau
atha śārṅgāyudhasutaṃ śacīputraḥ pratāpavān
vibhāṣyābhyahanad rājan divyenāstreṇa satvaraḥ
so 'straṃ tad atidīpyantam āpatantaṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
tastambhe bāṇajālena tad adbhutam ivābhavat
tatas tad dīpyamānaṃ tu papāta raṇamūrdhani
raukmiṇeyasya kauravya ghoraṃ dānavamardanam
tenāstreṇa ratho dagdhaḥ pradyumnasya mahātmanaḥ
nādahat tat tu ghoraṃ taṃ raukmiṇeyaṃ janādhipa
dahaty agniṃ na khalv agnir uddhato 'pi viśāṃ pate
dagdhād rathān mahābāhū raukmiṇeyo 'pacakrame
atha nārāyaṇasuto viratho rathināṃ varaḥ
sthito dhanuṣmān ākāśe jayantam idam abravīt
mahendraputra divyaṃ tvaṃ yad astraṃ muktavān asi
nāham idṛśarūpāṇāṃ śakyo hantuṃ śatair api
prayatnaṃ kuru śikṣāyāṃ yatnaṃ me 'dya pradarśaya
nāsti me 'tiśayaṃ kartā saṃgrāme 'maranandana
āsīn me sādhvasaṃ dṛṣṭvā rathasthaṃ tvāṃ dhṛtāyudham
bibhemi tava nedānīṃ yuddhe dṛṣṭabalābalaḥ
manasā smaryatām eṣa pārijātas tvayā taruḥ
śakyaṃ na khalu hastābhyāṃ spraṣṭavyo yas tvayā hy asau
ratho māyāmayo dagdhas tvayā yo hy astratejasā
īdṛśāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi sraṣṭuṃ śakto 'smi māyayā
evam ukto jayantaś ca mumocāstraṃ mahābalaḥ
tapasopacitaṃ tena svayam evātitejasā
tat pradyumno mahāvegaṃ śarajālair avārayat
catvāry astrāṇi divyāni mumocaivāparāṇi saḥ
dikṣu sarvāsu rurudhus tany astrāṇy atha bhārata
raukmiṇeyaṃ mahātmānam antarikṣe ca pañcamam
maholkāsadṛśān bāṇān astrāṇy amarasattamaḥ
mumoca tāni ghorāṇi pradyumnaṃ prati sarvataḥ
tāni sarvāṇi bāṇaughaiḥ kārṣṇir astrāṇy avārayat
jayantaṃ cāparair bāṇair vivyādha niśitais tadā
tato nādaḥ samutsṛṣṭo dyucaraiḥ puṇyakarmabhiḥ
dṛṣṭvā sthairyaṃ ca śaighryaṃ ca pradyumnasya mahātmanaḥ
pravarasyāpi bāṇena śitena śinipuṃgavaḥ
cicchedeṣvasanaṃ vīro hastāvāpaṃ ca bhārata
tato 'nyat sa tu jagrāha mahat tad dhanur uttamam
mahendradattaṃ pravaro mahāśanisamasvanam
sa tena vīro mahatā dhanuṣā viprasattamaḥ
śarān mumoca viśikhān arkaraśminibhāṃs tadā
cakarta ca dhanuś citraṃ śaineyasyāmitaujasaḥ
vivyādha sarvagātreṣu bāṇair api ca sātyakim
dhanur ādāya śaineyas tato 'nyat kurunandana
dṛḍhaṃ bhārasahaṃ dhīmān vivyādha pravaraṃ raṇe
uccakartatur anyonyaṃ varmaṇī tau śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
gātrebhyaś caiva māṃsāni marmabhidbhiḥ śarottamaiḥ
athāṣṭadhārabāṇena punar iṣvasanaṃ dvidhā
ciccheda pravaro vīras tribhiś cainam atāḍayat
anyad iṣvasanaṃ taṃ tu grahītumanasaṃ dvijaḥ
gadayā tāḍayām āsa kṣiptayā laghuhastavat
so 'siṃ carma ca jagrāha sātyakiḥ prahasann iva
na jagrāha dhanur dhīmān gadayābhihato bhṛśam
tataḥ śaraśatāny eva mumoca pravaras tadā
vihastam iva vijñāya sātyakiṃ yadunandanam
pradyumno 'sya dadau khaḍgaṃ nirmalākāśasaṃnibham
tasya ciccheda bhallena nistriṃśaṃ pravaras tadā
tsarudeśe 'pātayac ca pravaraḥ prahasann iva
vyadhamac ca tathā carma śitair bāṇair ajihmagaiḥ
ājaghāna ca śaktyainaṃ hṛdi vipro nanāda ca
taṃ viklavam iva jñātvā pārijātajihīrṣayā
tārkṣyābhyāśe rathenaiva sa tasthau pravaras tadā
taṃ pakṣapuṭavegena cikṣepa garuḍas tadā
gavyūtim ekaṃ sarathaḥ sa papāta mumoha ca
taṃ jayanto nipatyātha patitaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ nṛpa
samāśvāsya rathaṃ śīghraṃ samāropitavāṃs tadā
śaineyam api muhyantaṃ patantaṃ ca muhur muhuḥ
āśvāsayānaḥ pradyumnaḥ pitṛvyaṃ pariṣasvaje
taṃ hi pasparśa hastena savyena madhusūdanaḥ
nīrujaḥ spṛṣṭamātreṇa sātyakiḥ samapadyata
pradyumno dakṣiṇe pārśve vāme tu śinipuṃgavaḥ
tasthatuḥ pārijātasya yuddhaśauṇḍatarāv ubhau
jayantaḥ pravaraś caiva rathenaikena bhārata
saṃpatantau mahendreṇa prahasyoktau mahātmanā
nāsannam abhigantavyaṃ garuḍasya kathaṃcana
balavān eṣa patatāṃ rājā ca vinatāsutaḥ
dakṣiṇe caiva savye ca pārśve mama dhṛtāyudhau
ubhau sthitau yudhyamānaṃ mām eveha prapaśyatam
evam uktau sthitau vīrau tataḥ śakrasya pārśvayoḥ
dadṛśāte yudhyamānau devarājajanārdanau
athendro garuḍaṃ bāṇair mahāśanisamasvanaiḥ
vivyādha sarvagātreṣu mahāstraprabhavais tadā
sa tān bāṇān agaṇayan vainateyaḥ pratāpavān
sasārābhimukho vīraḥ śakranāgam ariṃdamaḥ
ubhau tau sahasā rājan balinau gajapakṣiṇau
prayuddhau vīryasaṃpannau mahāprāṇau durāsadau
radanaiḥ pannagaripuṃ kareṇa śirasā tadā
airāvato gajapatir ājaghāna nadaṃs tadā
tathā nakhāṅkuśais tīkṣṇair vainateyo balotkaṭaḥ
tathā pakṣanipātaiś ca śakranāgaṃ jaghāna ha
muhūrtaṃ sumahān āsīt saṃpāto gajapakṣiṇoḥ
vismāpanīyo jagataḥ prekṣakāṇāṃ bhayāvahaḥ
mūrdhny athairāvataṃ tārkṣyas tāḍayām āsa bhārata
nakhāṅkuśakarālena caraṇena mahābalaḥ
sa prahārābhisaṃtapto nipapāta triviṣṭapāt
pāriyātre giriśreṣṭhe dvīpe 'smiñ janamejaya
patantam api taṃ śakro na mumoca mahābalaḥ
kāruṇyād atha sauhārdāt pūrvābhyupagamād api
kṛṣṇo 'py anvagamac cainaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ prabhavāvyayaḥ
pārijātavatā dhīmān garuḍena mahābalaḥ
sa tasthau parvataśreṣṭhe pāriyātre tu vṛtrahā
airāvate samāśvaste saṃgrāmo vavṛdhe punaḥ
śarair āśīviṣaprakhyair astrayuktaiḥ sutejitaiḥ
anyonyaṃ kuruśārdūla śakrakeśavayor mahān
tato vajrāyudho vajram āśaniṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ
mumoca garuḍe rājann airāvaṇaripau nṛpa
vajrāśaninipātāṃs tān sehe śakrasya nāgahā
avadhyo balināṃ śreṣṭho nisargeṇa tapobalāt
mumoca pakṣam ekaikaṃ mānayann aśaniṃ tadā
vajraṃ ca devarājño 'tha bhrātuḥ kaśyapasaṃbhavaḥ
ākramyamāṇas tārkṣyeṇa nyamajjan nṛpate giriḥ
viveśa dharaṇīṃ rājañ śīryamāṇaḥ samantataḥ
cukūja bahumānena kṛṣṇasya sa tu parvataḥ
tam adrākṣīt tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ kiṃcic cheṣam adhokṣajaḥ
taṃ muktvā garuḍenātha tasthau devo vihāyasi
pradyumnaṃ ca tadovāca sarvakṛl lokabhāvanaḥ
ito dvāravatīṃ gatvā ratham ānaya māciram
sadārukaṃ mahābāho mattejobalam āśritaḥ
vaktavyo balabhadraś ca rājā ca kukurādhipaḥ
śvo jitvendram āgamiṣye dvārakām iti mānada
tathety uktvā tu dharmātmā pradyumnaḥ pitaraṃ vibhuḥ
gatvā yathoktam uktvā ca yādaveśabalāv ubhau
nāḍikāntaramātreṇa punas taṃ deśam āyayau
dārukeṇa samāyuktaṃ ratham asthāya bhārata
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tam āruhya rathaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ pāriyātraṃ giriṃ yayau
yatrairāvatam āsthāya sthitaḥ surapatiḥ prabhuḥ
pāriyātro giriśreṣṭho dṛṣṭvāyāntaṃ janārdanam
śāṇapādasamo bhūtva praviveśa vasuṃdharām
priyārthaṃ vāsudevasya prabhāvajño mahātmanaḥ
tasya prīto hṛṣīkeśaḥ parvatasya janādhipa
tataḥ prayāntaṃ yuddhārtham acyutaṃ kurunandana
sapārijāto garuḍaḥ pṛṣṭhato 'nuyayau balī
pradyumnaḥ sātyakiś cāpi garuḍasthau mahābalau
gatāv ubhau rakṣaṇārthaṃ pārijātam ariṃdamau
tatas tv astaṃ gataḥ sūryaḥ pravṛttā rajanī nṛpa
upasthitaṃ punar yuddhaṃ śakrakeśavayos tadā
suprahārāhataṃ dṛṣṭvā viṣṇur airāvataṃ gajam
nātikalyaṃ mahātejā devarājānam abravīt
garuḍābhihataḥ pūrvaṃ nātikalyo gajottamaḥ
airāvato mahābāho rātriś ca samupohyate
śvaḥ prabhāte punaḥ kāmaṃ pravartasva yathecchasi
evam astv iti kṛṣṇaṃ tu devarājo 'bravīt prabhuḥ
uvāsa puṣkarābhyāśe devarājaḥ puraṃdaraḥ
vrajaṃ girimayaṃ kṛtvā dharmātmā nṛpasattama
brahmā tato jagāmātha kaśyapaś ca mahān ṛṣiḥ
aditiś caiva sarve ca devā munaya eva ca
sādhyā viśve ca kauravya nāsatyāv aśvinau tathā
ādityāś caiva rudrāś ca vasavaś ca janeśvara
nārāyaṇaś ca putreṇa sātyakena ca bhārata
sahovāsa girau ramye pāriyātre prahṛṣṭavat
yaḥ sa śāṇapramāṇo 'sya bhaktyā samabhavan nṛpa
varaṃ prādāt tatas tasya parvatasya mahādyutiḥ
śāṇapāda iti khyāto bhaviṣyasi mahāgire
puṇyenārdhena tulyo hi puṇyo himavataḥ śubhaḥ
evam eva ca bhūyiṣṭho bhava parvatasattama
meruṇā spardhamāno hi bahucitramṛgāyutaḥ
tathā dattvā varaṃ tasya parvatasya tu keśavaḥ
dadhyau gaṅgāṃ saricchreṣṭhāṃ namaskṛtya vṛṣadhvajam
athāyayau viṣṇupadī smṛtā kṛṣṇena bhārata
saṃpūjya tāṃ tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ snātvā snānam adhokṣajaḥ
udakaṃ ca grahāyātha bilvaṃ ca harir avyayaḥ
devam āvāhayām āsa rudraṃ sarvasureśvaram
tataḥ prāpto mahādevaḥ somaḥ sapravaro vibhuḥ
tasthāv upari bilvasya tathā gaṅgodakasya ca
taṃ pārijātakusumair arcayām āsa keśavaḥ
tuṣṭāva vāgbhir īśeśaṃ sarvakartāram īśvaram
rudro devas tvaṃ rudanād rāvaṇāc ca
rorūyamāṇo drāvaṇāc cādidevaḥ
bhaktaṃ bhaktānāṃ vatsalaṃ vatsalānāṃ
kīrtyā yuṅkṣveśādya prabhavāmy antareṇa
grāmyāraṇyānāṃ tvaṃ patis tvaṃ paśūnāṃ
khyāto devaḥ paśupatiḥ sarvakarmā
nānyas tvattaḥ paramo devadeva
jagatpatiḥ suravīrārihantā
yasmād īśo mahatām īśvarāṇāṃ
bhavān ādyaḥ prītidaḥ prāṇadaś ca
tasmād dhi tvām īśvaraṃ prāhur īśaṃ
santo vidvāṃsaḥ sarvaśāstrārthatajjñāḥ
bhūtaṃ yasmāj jagad atyantadhīra
tvatto 'vyaktād akṣarād akṣareśa
tasmāt tvām āhur bhava ity eva bhūtaṃ
sarveśvarāṇāṃ mahatām atyudāram
yāsmāj jitair abhiṣikto 'si sarvair
devāsuraiḥ sarvabhūtaiś ca deva
maheśvaraṃ viśvakarmāṇam āhus
tvāṃ vai sarve tena devādhideva
pūjyo devaiḥ pūjyase nityadā vai
śaśvac chreyaḥkāṅkṣibhir varadāmeyavīrya
tasmād vikhyāto bhagavān devadevaḥ
satām iṣṭaḥ sarvabhūtātmabhāvī
bhūmis trayāṇāṃ deva yasmāt pratiṣṭhā
mune lokānāṃ bhāvano 'meyakīrtiḥ
tryambaketi prathamaṃ tena nāma
tavāprameyeti tridaśeśanātha
śarvaḥ śatrūṇāṃ śāsanād aprameyas
tathā bhūyaḥ śāsanāc ceśvareśa
sarvavyāpitvāc chaṃkaratvāc ca sadbhiḥ
śabdasyeśānaḥ śrīkarārkāgryatejāḥ
saṃsaktānāṃ nityadā yat karoṣi
śamaṃ bhrātṛvyān yad vyanaiṣīḥ samastān
tasmād devaḥ śaṃkaro 'sy aprameyaḥ
sadbhir dharmajñaiḥ kathyase sarvanātha
dattaḥ prahāraḥ kuliśena pūrvaṃ
taveśāna surarājñātivīrya
kaṇṭhe nailyaṃ tena te yat pravṛttaṃ
tasmāt khyātas tvaṃ nīlakaṇṭheti kalyaḥ
yal liṅgāṅkaṃ yac ca loke bhagāṅkaṃ
sarvaṃ soma tvaṃ sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ ca
prāhur viprās tvāṃ guṇinaṃ tattvavijñās
tathā dhyeyām ambikāṃ bhūtadhātrīm
vedair gītā sā hi tattvaṃ prasūtā
yajño dīkṣāṇāṃ yogināṃ cātirūpaḥ
nātyadbhutaṃ tvatsamaṃ deva bhūtaṃ
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhava devātha nāsti
ahaṃ brahmā kapilo 'thāpy anantaḥ
putrāḥ sarve brahmaṇaś cātivīrāḥ
tvattaḥ sarve devadeva prasūtā
evaṃ sarveśaḥ kāraṇātmā tvam īḍyaḥ
iti saṃstūyamānas tu bhagavān govṛṣadhvajaḥ
prasārya dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ nārāyaṇam athābravīt
manīṣitānām arhānāṃ prāptis te 'stu surottama
pārijātaṃ ca hartāsi mā bhūt te manasā vyathā
yathā mainākam āśritya tapas tvam akaroḥ prabho
tathā mama varaṃ kṛṣṇa saṃsmṛtya sthairyam āpnuhi
avadhyas tvam ajeyaś ca mattaḥ śūrataras tathā
bhavitāsīty avocaṃ yat tat tathā na tad anyathā
yaś ca stavena māṃ bhaktyā stoṣyate 'marasattama
tvayā kṛtena dharmajña dharmabhāk sa bhaviṣyati
samare ca jayaṃ viṣṇo prāpya pūjāṃ tathottamām
bilvodakeśvaro nāma bhavitāham ihānagha
deśe tvayā sthāpito vai devasiddhopayācanaḥ
ihasthopoṣito vidvān bhaktimān mama keśava
trirātram īpsitāṃl lokān gamiṣyati janārdana
avandhyā nāma deśe 'smin gaṅgā caiva bhaviṣyati
gaṅgāsnānasamaṃ snānaṃ mantrato bhavitā tathā
ṣaṭpuraṃ nāma nagaraṃ dānavānāṃ janārdana
atrāntardharaṇīdeśe tac cākramya mahābalāḥ
ete daityā durātmāno jagato devakaṇṭakāḥ
channā vasanti govinda sānāv asya mahāgireḥ
avadhyā devadevānāṃ vareṇa brahmaṇo 'nagha
mānuṣāntaritas tasmāt tvam etāñ jahi keśava
evam uktvā mahādevas tatraivāntaradhīyata
pariṣvajya mahātmānaṃ vāsudevaṃ janādhipa
tato yāte mahādeve prabhātāyāṃ narādhipa
tasyāṃ niśāyāṃ govindo bhūyaḥ parvatam abravīt
tavādhaḥ parvataśreṣṭha nivasanti mahāsurāḥ
tvayā ruddho hi tanmārgo jagato hitakāmyayā
nirgamiṣyanti te naiva mayā ruddhā mahābalāḥ
dvāre niruddhe tatraiva vinaṅkṣyanti mamājñayā
tvayi saṃnihitaś cāhaṃ bhaviṣyāmi mahāgire
adhiṣṭhāya mahāghorān nivatsyāmi ca parvata
āruhya mūrdhni madrūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā parvatasattama
gosahasrapradānasya phalaṃ prāpsyanti śāśvatam
tvatto 'śmabhiś ca pratimāṃ kārayitveha bhaktitaḥ
śuśrūṣiṣyanti ye nityaṃ mama yāsyanti te gatim
iti taṃ parvataṃ kṛṣṇo varado 'nugṛhītavān
tadāprabhṛti deveśas tatra saṃnihito 'cyutaḥ
pāṣāṇaiḥ pratimāṃ tatra kārayitvā ca kaurava
śuśrūṣanti kṛtātmāno viṣṇulokābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tatho rathavaraṃ kṛṣṇaḥ āruhya mahātmanāḥ
bilvodakeśvaraṃ devaṃ namaskṛtya yayau nṛpa
mahendram āhvayām āsa rathastho madhusūdanaḥ
satkṛtaṃ puṣkarābhyāśe sarvair devagaṇaiḥ saha
tataḥ śakro jayanto 'tha haribhir yuktam uttamam
āruroha rathaṃ devaḥ sarvakāmapradaḥ satām
tayo rathasthayor yuddham abhavat kurunandana
devayor daivayogena pārijātakṛte tadā
tato 'hanad raṇe viṣṇur bāṇaiḥ śatrubalārdanaḥ
sainyāni devarājasya bāṇajālair ajihmagaiḥ
upendraṃ na mahendro 'tha naiva viṣṇuḥ sureśvaram
tāḍayām āsatur vīrau śastraiḥ śaktāv ubhau prabho
ekaikam aśvaṃ daśabhir mahendrasya janārdanaḥ
vivyādha bāṇair niśitair astrayuktair janeśvara
sainyāny api ca devendraḥ śarair amarasattamaḥ
chādayām āsa rājendra ghorair astrābhimantritaiḥ
sa ca bāṇasahasraiś ca kṛṣṇo gajam avākirat
garuḍaṃ ca mahātejā balabhid dharivāhanaḥ
bhūmiṣṭhābhyāṃ rathābhyāṃ tau tad ahaḥ śatrudāraṇau
yuyudhāte mahātmānau nārāyaṇasurādhipau
cakampa vasudhā kṛtsnā naur jalastheva bhārata
diśāṃ dāhena digdeśāḥ saṃvṛtāś ca samantataḥ
celur girivarāś caiva petuś ca śataśo drumāḥ
petuś ca dharaṇīpṛṣṭhe martyā dharmaguṇānvitāḥ
nirghātāḥ śataśaś cānye petus tatra narādhipa
ūhuś ca saritaḥ sarvāḥ pratisroto viśāṃ pate
viṣvag vātā vavuś caiva petur ulkāś ca niṣprabhāḥ
muhur muhur bhūtasaṃghā rathanādena mohitāḥ
prajajvāla jale caiva vahnir janapadeśvara
yuyudhuś ca grahaiḥ sārdhaṃ grahā nabhasi sarvataḥ
jyotīṃṣi śataśaḥ petuḥ svargāc ca dharaṇītale
diśāṃ gajāḥ prakupitā nāgāś ca dharaṇītale
gardabhāruṇasaṃsthānaiś channābhraiś cāvṛtaṃ nabhaḥ
vinadadbhir mahārāvair ulkāśoṇitavarṣibhiḥ
na bhūr na dyaur na gaganaṃ narendravṛṣabhābhavan
svasthāni suravīrau tau dṛṣṭvā yuddhagatau tadā
jepur munigaṇā mantrāñ jagato hitakāmyayā
brāhmaṇāś ca mahātmāno vyatiṣṭhaṃs teṣu satvarāḥ
tato brahmā mahātejāḥ kaśyapaṃ vākyam abravīt
gaccha vadhvā sahādityā putrau vāraya suvrata
sa tatheti tadā devam uktvā padmanabhaṃ muniḥ
jagāma ratham āsthāya tasthau naravarāntike
sthitaṃ tu kaśyapaṃ drṣṭvā sahādityā tadāntarā
ubhau rathābhyāṃ dharaṇīm avatīrṇau mahābalau
nyastaśastrau ca tau vīrau vavandatur ariṃdamau
pitarau dharmatattvajñau sarvabhūtahite ratau
ubhau grahāya hastābhyām aditis tv abravīd vacaḥ
asodarāv ivaivaṃ kim anyonyaṃ hantum icchatha
svalpam arthaṃ puraskṛtya pravṛttam atidāruṇam
sadṛśaṃ neti paśyāmi sarvathā mama putrayoḥ
śrotavyaṃ yadi mātuś ca pituś caiva prajāpateḥ
nyastaśastrau sthitau bhūtvā kurutaṃ vacanaṃ mama
tathety uktvā ca tau devau snātukāmau mahābalau
gaṅgāṃ jagmatur evātha prajalpantau parasparam
śakra uvāca
tvaṃ prabhur lokakṛt kṛṣṇa rājye 'haṃ sthāpitas tvayā
sthāpayitvā kathaṃ nāma punar mām avamanyase
bhrātṛtvam upagamyaivaṃ jyeṣṭhatvaṃ pratipūjya ca
kathaṃ kamalapatrākṣa nirvāṇaṃ kartum arhasi
snātau tu jāhnavītoye punar abhāgatau nṛpa
yatrāditiḥ kaśyapaś ca mahātmānau dṛḍhavratau
priyasaṃgamanaṃ nāma taṃ deśaṃ munayo 'vadan
yatra tau saṃgatau cobhau pitṛbhyāṃ kamalekṣaṇau
tataḥ śakrasya kauravya prāptā vāsājiraṃ tadā
yatra devagaṇāḥ sarve sametā dharmacāriṇaḥ
tato yayur vimānair tu devāḥ sarve triviṣṭapam
ṛddhyā paramayā yuktās teṣām evānurūpayā
kaśyapaś cāditiś caiva tathā śakrajanārdanau
vimānam ekam āruhya gatā rājaṃs triviṣṭapam
te śakrasadanaṃ prāptā ramyaṃ sarvaguṇānvitam
ūṣur ekatra kauravya muditā dharmacāriṇaḥ
śacī tu kaśyapaṃ patnyā sahitaṃ dharmavatsalā
upācaran mahātmānaṃ sarvabhūtahite ratā
tatas tasyāṃ prabhātāyāṃ rajanyām abravīd dharim
aditir dharmatattvajñā sarvabhūtahitaṃkaram
upendra dvārakaṃ gaccha pārijātaṃ nayasva ca
vadhvā saṃprāpayasvemaṃ puṇyakaṃ hṛdayepsitam
puṇyake satyayā prāpte punar eṣa tvayā taruḥ
nandane puruṣaśreṣṭha sthāpyaḥ sthāne yathocite
evam astv iti kṛṣṇena devamātā yaśasvinī
uktā dharmaguṇair yuktā yādavena mahātmanā
tato 'bhivādya pitaraṃ mātaraṃ ca janārdanaḥ
mahendraṃ saha śacyā ca pratasthe dvārakāṃ prati
dadau kṛṣṇāya paulomī niyogāt kurunandana
sarvāsām eva kṛṣṇasya bhāryāṇāṃ dharmacāriṇī
divyānāṃ sarvaratnānāṃ vāsasāṃ ca manasvinī
nānārāgaviraktānāṃ sadaivārajasām api
bhāryāṇāṃ ca sahasrāṇi yāni ṣodaśa mādhave
pratigṛhya mahātejāḥ prayayau dvārakāṃ prati
saṃpūjayamāno dyutimān khecaraiḥ puṇyakarmabhiḥ
sasātyakiḥ saputraś ca prāpto raivatakaṃ girim
sa tatra sthāpayitvā ca pārijātaṃ varadrumam
sātyakiṃ preṣayām āsa dvārakāṃ dvāramālimīm
kṛṣṇa uvāca
pārijātam ihānītaṃ mahendrasadanān mayā
nivedaya mahābāho bhaimānāṃ bhaimavardhana
adya dvāravatīṃ caiva pārijātaṃ mahādrumam
praveśayiṣye nagare śobhā prakriyatāṃ śubhā
ity uktaḥ satyako gatvā tathoktvā punar āgataḥ
kumārair nāgaraiḥ sārdhaṃ sāmbaprabhṛtibhiḥ prabho
tato 'grataḥ pārijātam āropya garuḍe tadā
pradyumno dvārakāṃ ramyāṃ viveśa rathināṃ varaḥ
śaibyādihayayuktena rathenānuyayau hariḥ
tasyānu rathamukhyena satyakaḥ sāmba eva ca
ye tv anye nṛpa vārṣṇeyā yānair bahuvidhais tathā
yayuḥ prahṛṣṭās tat karma pūjayanto mahātmanaḥ
satyakād vistaraṃ śrutvā yādavā nāgarās tathā
vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmur aprameyasya karmaṇaḥ
taṃ divyakusumaṃ vṛkṣaṃ dṛṣṭvānartanivāsinaḥ
rājan na tatṛpur hṛṣṭāḥ paśyamānā mahodayam
tam adbhutam acintyaṃ ca madakelikilāṇḍajam
vṛkṣottamaṃ paśyatāṃ vai vṛddhānām agamaj jarā
ye tv andhacakṣuṣaḥ sarve te 'bhavan divyacakṣuṣaḥ
virogā rogiṇaś cāsan ghrātvā gandhaṃ vanaspateḥ
lapantaḥ kokilāḥ śvetāḥ śrutvānartanivāsinaḥ
babhūvur hṛṣṭamanaso vavanduś ca janārdanam
nānāvidhāni tūryāṇi geyāni madhurāṇi ca
śuśruvus tasya vṛkṣasya nātidūragatā narāḥ
yo yaṃ saṃkalpayām āsa gandhaṃ hṛdyaṃ naras tadā
sa tadaiva tam ājaghre pārijātasamudbhavam
tataḥ praviśya ramyāṃ tu dvārakāṃ yadunandanaḥ
vasudevaṃ mahātmānaṃ dadṛśe devakīṃ tathā
kukurādhipatiṃ caiva balaṃ bhrātaram eva ca
vṛddhāṃś ca yādavānāṃ ye mānārhān amaropamān
visarjya tān vai bhagavān anādinidhano 'cyutaḥ
saṃpūjya ca yathānyāyaṃ svam eva bhavanaṃ gataḥ
sa satyabhāmayā vāsaṃ viveśa madhusūdanaḥ
pārijātaṃ taruśreṣṭḥaṃ grahāya gadapūrvajaḥ
sā devī pūjayām āsa prahṛṣṭā vāsavānujam
pratijagrāha taṃ cāpi pārijātaṃ mahādrumam
manīṣitena sa tarur alpo bhavati bhārata
mahāṃś ca vāsudevasya tad adbhutam ivābhavat
kadācid dvārakāṃ sarvāṃ pracchādayati bhārata
kadācid dhastadhāryas tu bhavaty aṅguṣṭhasaṃnibhaḥ
nananda satyā kauravya devī prāpya manoratham
puṇyakārthaṃ tu saṃbhārān saṃbhartum upacakrame
yāni dravyāṇi kauravya jambudvīpe tu kānicit
yogyāni tāni kṛṣṇena saṃhṛtāni mahātmanā
muniṃ tadā saṃsmṛtavān sa nāradaṃ
janārdanaḥ sarvaguṇānvitaṃ vaśī
pratigrahārthaṃ vratakasya satyayā
yathopadiṣṭasya puraṃdarānujaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
atha kṛṣṇasya kauravya dhyātamātras tapodhanaḥ
ājagāma muniśreṣṭho nārado vadatāṃ varaḥ
taṃ pūjayitvā vidhivad vāsudevo viśāṃ pate
pratigrahārthaṃ vidhivac chrīmān abhinyamantrayat
tataḥ kāle ca saṃprāpte snātaṃ devo mahāmunim
saṃpūjya mālyair gandhaiś ca bhojayām āsa bhārata
sārvakāmikam annādyaṃ sarvabhūtakṛd avyayaḥ
satyayā priyayā sārdhaṃ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
puṣpadāmāvasajyātha kaṇṭhe kṛṣṇasya bhāvanī
babandha kṛṣṇaṃ subhagā pārijāte vanaspatau
adbhir dadau nāradāya tato 'nujñāpya keśavam
devī dhenusahasraṃ ca kāñcanasya ca parvatam
hiraṇyarūpyamiśrasya maṇiratnaprabhasya ca
tilamiśrasya ca tathā dhānyair anyair yutasya ca
pratigṛhya tu tat sarvaṃ nārado munisattamaḥ
prahṛṣṭo vadatāṃ śreṣṭho bhuktvā keśavam abravīt
bhoḥ keśava madīyas tvam adbhir datto 'si satyayā
sa tvaṃ mām anugacchasva kuru yad yad bravīmy aham
prathamaḥ kalpaḥ ity evam abravīn madhusūdanaḥ
vrajantam anuvavrāja nāradaṃ ca janārdanaḥ
parihāsaṃ bahuvidhaṃ kṛtvā munivaras tadā
tiṣṭhasva gacchāmīty uktvā parihāsavicakṣaṇaḥ
apanīya tataḥ kaṇṭhāt puṣpadāmainam abravīt
kapilāṃ gāṃ savatsāṃ bho niṣkrayārthaṃ prayaccha me
kṛṣṇājinaṃ tilaiḥ pūrṇaṃ prayaccha ca sakāñcanam
eṣo 'tra niṣkrayaḥ kṛṣṇa vihito vṛṣaketunā
tathety uktvā hṛṣīkeśas tathā cakre janādhipa
sa uvāca muniśreṣṭhaṃ rahite madhusūdanaḥ
varaṃ varaya dharmajña yas te nārada kāṅkṣitaḥ
taṃ te dātāsmi dharmajña parā prītir hi me tvayi
nārada uvāca
nityam evāstu me prīto bhavān viṣṇo sanātana
tvatprabhāvāc ca sālokyaṃ vrajeyaṃ te mahāmate
ayonijo bhaveyaṃ ca nārāyaṇa satāṃ gate
bhaveyaṃ brāhmaṇaś caiva punarjātyantareṣv aham
evam astv iti taṃ devo viṣṇuḥ provāca bhārata
tutoṣa ca tato dhīmān nārado munisattamaḥ
ṣoḍaśa strīsahasrāṇi viṣṇor atulatejasaḥ
nimantritāni kauravya satyayā harikanyayā
tāsāṃ dadau saṃniyogam ekaikaṃ harivallabhā
śacyā yo vāsudevasya purā datto narādhipa
pārijāto vasaṃs tatra tataḥ pravavṛdhe tadā
ājñayā vāsudevasya nāradena mahātmanaḥ
nimantritā gaṇāḥ sarve keśavena mahātmanā
vibhūtiṃ pārijātasya dadṛśuḥ kurunandana
pāṇḍavāṃś cānayām āsa sahaiva pṛthayā hariḥ
draupadyā ca mahātejās tathaiva ca subhadrayā
śrutaśravāṃ ca sasutāṃ bhīṣmakaṃ sasutaṃ tathā
anyān api ca kauravya mitrasaṃbandhibāndhavān
reme ca saha pārthena phālgunena janārdanaḥ
sāntaḥpuro mahātejāḥ paramarddhyāvasan nṛpa
saṃvatsare tato yāte keśihāmarasaṃnibhaḥ
pārijātaṃ punaḥ svargam anayat sarvabhāvanaḥ
tatrāditiṃ kaśyapaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā svapitarau prabhuḥ
śakreṇa sahito dhīmān aprameyaparākramaḥ
tam uvācāditir mātā praṇataṃ madhusūdanam
saubhrātram astu vām evaṃ nityaṃ cāmarasattama
manorathaṃ mamaitaṃ tvaṃ pūrayasva janārdana
tathety evābravīt kṛṣṇas tato mātaram ātmavān
āmantrayitvā pitarau devarājānam abravīt
vāsudevo mahātejāḥ kālaprāptam idaṃ vacaḥ
mahādevena deveśa saṃdiṣṭo 'smi mahātmanā
antarbhūmitale vadhyān asurān prati mānada
tad ito daśarātreṇa hantāham asurottamān
tatropariṣṭāt sthātavyaṃ pravaṇena mahātmanā
jayantena ca vīreṇa dānavānāṃ jighāsayā
eko 'tra mānuṣo devo devaputras tathāparaḥ
avadhyāḥ kila te devair brahmaṇo varadarpitāḥ
asmābhiḥ kila hantavyā mānuṣatvam upāgataiḥ
tatheti kṛṣṇaṃ sa hariḥ prītarūpas tadābravīt
sasvajāte 'tha tau devāv anyonyaṃ janamejaya
dadau kirīṭaṃ kṛṣṇāya śakro 'mṛtasamudbhavam
prītātmā kuruśārdūla kuṇḍaladvayam eva ca
janamejaya uvāca
puṇyakānāṃ mamotpattiṃ kathayasva dvijottama
dvaipāyanaprasādena sarvaṃ hi viditaṃ tava
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
umayā puṇyakavidhir narendrotpāditaḥ purā
śṛṇu yena vidhānena loke djarmabhṛtāṃ vara
svargān nīte pārijāte kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā
yayau dvāravatīṃ dhīmān nārado munisattamaḥ
devāsure nṛpaśreṣṭha saṃgrāme samupasthite
ṣaṭpurasya vadhe ghore mahādevājñayānagha
kṛṣṇena sahitaṃ vipraṃ nāradaṃ dharmavittamam
āsīnaṃ paripapraccha rukmiṇī bhaiṣmakī nṛpa
tatra jāmbavatī devī satyamhāmā ca bhāminī
gāndhārarājaputrī ca yogayuktā narādhipa
devyaś ca nṛpa kṛṣṇasya bahvyo 'nyā vai samāgatāḥ
kulaśīlaguṇopetā dharmaśīlāḥ pativratāḥ
rukmiṇy uvāca
mune dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha sarvajñānabhṛtāṃ vara
utpattiṃ puṇyakānāṃ tvaṃn vaktum arhasy aśeṣataḥ
vidhiṃ ca phalayojaṃ ye dānakālaṃ tathaiva ca
kautūhalaṃ naḥ paramaṃ tac chindhi dvipadāṃ vara
nārada uvāca
śṛṇu vaidarbhi dharmajñe sapatnībhiḥ sahānaghe
puṇyakānāṃ vidhiḥ prokto yathā devyomayā purā
cacāromā vrataṃ devi puṇyakānāṃ śucivratā
vratāvasāne 'tha tayā sakhyo devi nimantritāḥ
adityādyāḥ sutāḥ sarvā dakṣasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ
paulomī ca śacī devī khyātā like pativratā
rohiṇī ca mahābhāgā somasyadayitā satī
phalgunī ca tahtā pūrvā revatī ca visāṃ pate
tathā śatabhiṣā caiva maghā ca kurunandana
etābhir hi mahādevī pūrvam ārādhitā satī
gaṅgā sarasvatī caiva celagaṅgā ca nimnagā
tathā vaitaraṇī caiva gaṇḍakī yā ca bhārata
anyāś ca sarito ramyā lopāmudrā ca bhārata
satyaś cānyā jagaddevi dhārayanti hi tāḥ śubhāḥ
śubhāś ca girinandinyo vahnikanyāś ca suvratāḥ
svāhā vahnipriyā devī sāvitrī ca yaśasvinī
ṛddhiḥ kuberakāntā ca jaleśamahiṣī tathā
bhāryā pitṛpateś caiva vasupatnyas tathaiva ca
hrīḥ śrīr dhṛtis tathā kīrtir āśā meghā ca suvratā
prītir matiś ca khyātiś ca saṃyatiś ca tapodhanāḥ
devyaḥ satyas tathaivānyāḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ
tāsāṃ vratāvasāne ca pūjāṃ cakre 'mbikā tadā
tilaratnamayaṃ dattvā parvataṃ sarvadhānyavat
vāsobhir bahubhir mukhyair nānārāgaiḥ sumadhyame
pratigṛhya tu tāṃ pūjāṃ dattāṃ devyā tapodhanāḥ
upaviṣṭāḥ kathāś citrāḥ kurvantyo bhartṛdevatāḥ
puṇyakārthaṃ kathās tāsām āsan devī śaśaṃsa yāḥ
vidhiṃ ca puṇyakasyātha satīnāṃ bhartṛdevate
tāsāṃ matena sādhvīnāṃ sarvāsāṃ somanandinī
paryapṛcchad umāṃ devīṃ puṇyakānāṃ vidhiṃ varam
umā tāsāṃ priyārthaṃ tu puṇyakāny abravīt tadā
samakṣaṃ mama vaidarbhi sarvabhūtahite ratā
mamaiva comayā dattaḥ sa tadā ratnaparvataḥ
pratigṛhya mayā caiva kṛto brāhmaṇāc chubhe
umā tv arundhatīṃ sādhvīm āmantrya yad abhāṣata
śṛṇu kalyāṇi vakṣyāmi sarvābhiḥ sahitā śubhe
puṇyakānāṃ vidhiṃ kṛtsnaṃ yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ
yathā caiva mayā dṛṣṭas tata eṣa vidhiḥ śubhe
umovāca
sarvajñāhaṃ yadā bhartuḥ prasādena śaucismite
tadā purā mayādiṣṭo dṛṣṭaḥ puṇyavidhiḥ śubhaḥ
sanātanaḥ puṇyavidhir iti buddhyāvagamyatām
mahādevaprasādena mayā dṛṣṭas tv arundhati
puṇyakāni ca sarvāṇi cīrṇavaty asmy anindite
anujñayā bhagavato bhartuḥ śarvasya dhīmataḥ
satītvaṃ dharmacaraṇaṃ yasyā nityamakhaṇḍitam
puṇyakānāṃ vidhis tasyāḥ purāṇe parikīrtitaḥ
dānopavāsapuṇyāni sukṛtāny apy arundhati
niṣphalāny asatīnāṃ hi puṇyakāni tathā śubhe
yā vañcayanti bhartāraṃ yoniduṣṭāś ca yāḥ striyaḥ
yoniduṣṭāt puṇyaphalaṃ nāśnanti nirayaṃgamāḥ
sādhvyo jagad dhārayanti suśīlāḥ patidevatāḥ
ananyā dharmanityāś ca satāṃ panthānam āśritāḥ
avāgduṣṭāḥ śauciyuktā dhṛtimatyāḥ śubhavratāḥ
satataṃ sādhuvādinyo dhārayanti jagat khalu
vyādhitaḥ patito vāpi dīno vāpi katkhaṃcana
na tyaktavyaḥ striyā bhartā dharma eṣa sanātanaḥ
akāryakāriṇaṃ vāpi patitaṃ vāpi nirguṇam
strī patiṃ tārayaty eva tathātmānaṃ śubhānane
yoniduṣṭastriyo nāsti prāyaścittaṃ hataiva sā
vāgduṣṭe vihitaṃ sadbhiḥ prāyaścittaṃ purātane
bhartuś chandena kartavyaṃ vratakaṃ sarvadā striyā
upavāso 'pi vā satye kāṇkṣantyā sukṛtāṃ gatim
kalpāntarasahasreṣu na strī sā labhate gatim
tiryagyonisahasreṣu pacyate yoniviplavāt
yadi syān nāma mānuṣyaṃ strī labhed asatī satī
caṇḍālayonau durmedhā jāyate kukkurāśanā
bhartā devaḥ sadā strīṇāṃ sadbhir dṛṣṭas tapodhane
yasyā hi tuṣyate bhartā sā satī dharmacāriṇī
kautūhalahatānāṃ tu striṇāṃ loko na śobhanaḥ
bhartary eva mano yāsāṃ sadbhāvena vyavasthitam
karmaṇā manasā vācā patiṃ nāticaranti yāḥ
tāsāṃ puṇyaphalaṃ saumye puṇyakaiḥ samudāhṛtam
puṇyakānāṃ vidhiṃ kṛtsnaṃ svarlokaṃ prati śobhane
nibodha saha sarvābhir dṛṣṭo yas tapasā mayā
snātvā strī pratar utthāya patiṃ vijñāpayet satī
upavāsārtham atha vā vratakāryaṃ dhṛtavrate
śvaśurābhyāṃ ca caraṇau satataṃ saṃnamasya ca
grahāyaudambaraṃ pātraṃ sakuśaṃ sākṣataṃ tathā
gośṛṅgaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ sicya pratigṛhṇīta taj jalam
tato bhartuḥ satī dadyāt snātasya prayatasya ca
ātmano 'tha niṣektavyaṃ tataḥ śirasi taj jalam
trailokye sarvatīrtheṣu snānam etad udāhṛtam
upavāseṣu kartavyam etad dhi vratakeṣu ca
snānam etad dhi sāmānyaṃ strīṇāṃ puṃsāṃ ca bhāvini
arundhati mayā dṛṣṭaṃ tapasā haratejasā
aśalyaviddhaṃ śayanam āsanaṃ ca tathāvidham
svayaṃ prakṣālanaṃ cāpi pādayor anuśabditam
aśruprapāto roṣaś ca kalahaś ca kṛtaḥ sati
upavāsād vratād vāpi sadyo bhraṃśayati striyaḥ
śuklam eva sadā vāsaḥ praśastaṃ candrasaṃbhave
antarvāsaṃ coparaṃ caiva upavāse vrate tathā
pādukāryaṃ trṇaiḥ kāryaṃ sarvadā vratake sati
upavāse 'pi ca vidhir eṣa eva prakīrtitaḥ
añjanaṃ rocanaṃ cāpi gandhān sumanasas tathā
vratake copavāse ca nityam eva vivarjayet
dantakāṣṭaṃ śiraḥsnānam udvartanam athāpi vā
vivarjitaṃ mṛdā sarvaḥ śaucarthas tu vidhīyate
bilvāmṛtaphalair nityaṃ śrīphalaiś ca samācaret
prakṣālanaṃ vai śirasaḥ sadā mṛnmiśritair jalaiḥ
śiraso 'bhyañjanaṃ saumye naivam etat praśasyate
na pādayor na gātrasya sneheneti sthitiḥ smṛtā
goyānam uṣṭrayānaṃ ca kharayānaṃ ca varjitam
nagnasnānaṃ ca satataṃ vrate cāpy upavāsake
nadījalaṃ prasravajaṃ praśastaṃ somanandini
śubhe taḍāgavāpy ādau vistīrṇe jalajāyute
gatvā snānaṃ praśastaṃ tu sadaive khalu sarvathā
alābhe tv avaruddhā strī ghaṭasnānaṃ samācaret
navaiś ca kumbhaiḥ snātavyaṃ vidhir eṣa purātanaḥ
snānaṃ ca kāryaṃ śirasā tapaḥphalam avāpnuyāt
umovāca
vidhinaitena kṛtsnena strī sadā bhatṛdevatā
caret saṃvatsaraṃ dāntā ṣaṇmāsān māsam eva vā
striyo hy āvāhayet sādhvīr ekādaśa samādhinā
svayaṃ caiva vidhir dṛṣṭo vratakānāṃ vidhiḥ śubhaḥ
adbhir dadyāt satī sarvā yā mūlavratinī bhavet
tāsāṃ tu niṣkrayo deyo deśakālānurūpataḥ
tato māsāntaśuklasya tithau ca navamī tathā
ārādhayitvā kartavyaṃ vratakasyāpavarjanam
upavāsam ahorātraṃ vratakasyāpi niścitā
ādau cānte ca kurvīta vratakasyāpi siddhaye
kṣurakarma tato bhartur ātmanaś caiva kārayet
utsādanaṃ na snānaṃ ca tasminn ahani saṃsmṛtam
tato vivāhavat snānaṃ vihitaṃ puṇyake śubhe
maṇḍanaṃ caiva vihitaṃ mālyadhāraṇam eva ca
kumbhais tu snāpyamānemaṃ sādhvī mantram udīrayet
bhartuḥ pādau namaskṛtya manasā vātha vā girā
āpo devyo ṛṣīṇāṃ hi viśvadhātryo
divyā mādantyā yāḥ śaṃkarā dharmadhātryaḥ
hiraṇyavarṇāḥ pāvakāḥ śivatamena
rasena śreyase māṃ juṣantu
apām eṣa smṛto mantraḥ sarvatrānyatra me śṛṇu
mantraṃ purāṇavihitaṃ strīṇāṃ sarvāṅgaśobhane
śubhāvyayā guṇinī yuktadharmā
bhartrā sākaṃ mama dāsyā vateṇyā
mā karmaṇā manasā vāpi vācā
bhartur bhaveyaṃ ruśatī syāṃ vaśaṃgā
sapatnīnām adhi nityaṃ bhaveyaṃ
suputrā syāṃ subhagā cārurūpā
saṃpannahastā guṇavādinī ca
sarvāmanā syāṃ na daridrā bhaveyam
patiś ca me syāt sumukho matpratīkṣo
nityaṃ madbhaktaḥ syāmn manmatir madgatiś ca
prītiś ca nau syāc cakravākānurūpā
manovirāgo na bhavet sādhu ca syāt
lokān sādhvānām uttamānāṃ vrajeyaṃ
yābhiḥ sarvaṃ dhāryate viśvarūpam
ubhe ule yāḥ śubhāḥ pāvayanti
pitur bhartuś ca patibhaktyorjitāś ca
bhūmir vāyur jalam ākāśam agnir
antaḥkṣetrajñaḥ prakṛtir yo mahāṃś ca
ahaṃkāraś ca mama sākṣye niyuktāḥ
smareyur me niścayaṃ ca vrataṃ ca
yair ārabdho dehināṃ bhautiko 'yaṃ
vidhiḥ sattvādyair bhūtayuktaiḥ sabījaiḥ
santv ete me sākṣiṇaḥ sarvasaṃsthā
vrate cāsmin niścaye cāpi vṛtte
candrādityau puṇyasākṣī yamaś ca
diśaḥ sarvā daśa cātmā ca me 'yam
santv ete vai sākṣiṇaḥ sarva eva
vrate cāsmin niścaye cāpi nityam
mantrair etaiḥ purāṇoktaiḥ sarvadravyabhimantraṇam
vratacaryāprabhṛti vai purāṇe samudāhṛtam
snātvātha vāsasī dadyād bhartuḥ kartya svayaṃ śubhe
athātmakartitaṃ na syāc chubhe vighnena kenacit
vāso 'nyad eva dadyāc ca śvetaṃ mukhyaṃ navaṃ śuci
svakartitaṃ sūtratantuṃ vāsasā tena miśrayet
tato dvijaṃ śuciṃ dāntaṃ jñānavijñānakovidam
bhojayec ca yathāśakti saha bhartrā sumadhyame
brāhmaṇasyāpi dātavyaṃ vāsoyugmaṃ mahāmate
śayyā yānaṃ gṛhaṃ dhānyaṃ dāsīdāsaṃ tathaiva ca
alaṃkāraḥ śaktitaś ca ratnaparvata eva ca
sarvadhānyasamunmiśras tilaiś ca saviśeṣataḥ
vāsobhiś ca praticchanno nānāvarṇair arundhati
hastyaśvājarathāś caiva deyā gaur eva ca dhruvam
lavaṇapratimāṃ dadyān navanītasya cāparām
guḍasya madhunaś caiva suvarṇasya ca śobhanām
tathaiva sarvagandhānāṃ rasānāṃ pṛthag eva ca
tathā sumanasāṃ dadyād rūpasyaudumbarasya ca
phalānāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ vāsasām api nandini
citrapratikṛtiṃ caiva yāṃś cānyān apy abhīpsyati
śilāpratikṛtiṃ caiva dadhno 'tha payasas tathā
sarpiṣā dūrvayā caiva yāṃś cānyān apy abhīpsati
kāladeśānurūpaṃ ca deyaṃ vibhavataḥ sati
alpaṃ vā bahulaṃ vāpi bhartuś chandena sarvadā
tilapātraṃ pradātavyaṃ na deyaṃ na tu śobhane
gaus tv avaśyaṃ pradātavyā kapilā kāṃsyam eva ca
kṛṣṇājinaṃ ca subhage satilaṃ vāsasānvitam
ādarśaś caiva kūrcaś ca tathājinam anindite
etad dattvā sarvakāmān āpnoti varavarṇinī
purodhikā putravatī subhagā rūpabhāvinī
mṛṣṭahastā dhanāḍhyā ca strī bhavaty amalekṣāṇā
icchayā labhate caiva kanyāṃ rūpaguṇānvitām
bhavanti subhagāś cāḍhyās tathaiva ca purodhikāḥ
putravatyo dhanāḍhyāś ca śīlavatyaś ca nityadā
arundhati kṛtaṃ hy etan mayaiva prathamaṃ yataḥ
umāvratakam ity evaṃ khyātam atra mahītale
etad evottamaṃ strīṇāṃ vrataṃ tasmāt samācaret
sarvakāmān avāpnoti strī dattvaivam anindite
etad vratakarāje ca devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ
purābhiṣiktavān saumye priyārthaṃ mama sarvakṛt
vratakasyāvasāne tu deyaṃ bhojyaṃ ca nityadā
strīṇāṃ pradeyāḥ kāmāś ca sadṛśāḥ kāladeśayoḥ
ekaikasya pradātavyaṃ vratakaṃ varavarṇini
chandato brāhmaṇānāṃ tu deyam annaṃ sadakṣiṇam
pāyasaṃ tatra dātavyaṃ vratake nānyad iṣyate
nātra prāṇivadhaḥ kāryaḥ purāṇe niyatā śrutiḥ
atha dvitīyaṃ vakṣyāmi vratakaṃ somasaṃbhave
mahādevaprasādeva dṛṣṭavaty asmi yac chubhe
sarvāḥ putraphalāḥ nāryaḥ sadbhir etad udāhṛtam
tasmād anviṣyatī dadyāt saputrakarakāñ śubhe
jyeṣṭhāṣāḍhau śubhau māsau puroktaṃ vidhim ācaret
atha vā jyeṣṭham evaikam āṣāḍhaṃ vā samācaret
tato māsadvaye pūrṇe māse vā varavarṇini
saputrakarakān dadyāt phāṇitapratipūritān
sarpiṣaḥ payasaś caiva dadhno 'tha madhuno 'naghe
jalasya ca tathā dadyāt pūrayitvā śaśiprabhe
ekasmai jñānavṛddhāya suvratāya jitātmane
saputrakarakān dadyād yāvanto manasaḥ priyāḥ
icched duhitaraṃ ced dhi strīnāmnā kārayet tataḥ
kiṃcid dravyaṃ sutākāmāt sutāṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayam
gaur vātha kāñcanaṃ vāpi dakṣiṇārthaṃ praśasyate
viprasyācchādanaṃ deyam avaśyaṃ tu śucismite
yajñopavītaṃ vratake dadyān nārī śucivratā
saputrakarakāṇāṃ tu vidhinaivaṃ vipaścitā
apatyākhyānayogena brāhmaṇebhyaḥ śucismite
saṃvatsaraṃ susaṃpūrṇaṃ vratadharmānupālinī
karakān api dadyāc ca pūrṇe saṃvatsare śubhe
anujñayā sadā bhartuḥ satyavādiny arundhati
suvarṇasūtraṃ viprāya kaumudyāṃ dātum arhati
yajñopavītaṃ viprasya vrataṃ saṃsthāpya kāmikam
