yajñopavītaṃ karakaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ ca svaśaktitaḥ
prayacchantī satī strībhiḥ sarvān kāmān samaśnute
na ca saṃbhakṣayet kiṃcin nārī dhānyam atho phalam
puṣpaṃ vā nopayuñjīta yāvad evaṃ samācaret
ekabhaktena dharmajñe sā tryahaṃ kṣantum arhati
brāhmaṇāya tato deyaṃ bhartuś ca tadanantaram
evaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ kṛtvā subhagā rūpaśālinī
bhavaty avidhavā caiva strī dhanasya tatheśvarī
vārtākāni na khāded yā strī pūrṇaṃ parivatsaram
na sā putravināśaṃ hi paśyatīty avagamyatām
śaśakaṃ mṛgamāṃsaṃ ca nityam eva vivarjayet
nāpnoti maraṇaṃ nārī prāpnoti patidevatām
alābuṃ varjayen nārī tathaivopodikām api
kalambūṃ kāñcanaṃ dadyād yā bhartuḥ sukham icchati
pūrṇe saṃvatsare dadyād ekaikaṃ śākam ādṛtā
sudakṣiṇaṃ putravatī bhavaty eṣā purodhikā
svayaṃ prakṣālayānā strī svapādāv evam āditaḥ
pratiṣṭhāṃ labhate nityam udvegaṃ nādhigacchati
divā yā sūryapūtena vartayet strī pativratā
evaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ pūrṇaṃ rātrāv annaṃ vivarjayet
sā jīvaputrā subhagā bhavaty amaravarṇinī
adhitiṣṭhati sarvāś ca sapatnyo nātra saṃśayaḥ
pūrṇe saṃvatsare dadyāt sauvarṇaṃ sūryam uttamam
brāhmaṇāyābhirūpāya daridrāya yaśasvine
phalāni vātha puṣpāṇi bhakṣāṇy api ca suvratā
dadyād anastamitake caritavratakā tathā
athkāstaṃgamite sūrye bhuṅkte strī niyatā satī
candranakṣatrapūtāni bhojyāni varavarṇinī
sā dadyāt kāñcanaṃ candraṃ nakṣatrtāṇi grahān api
abhirūpāya viprāya vāsaś ca lavaṇānvitam
candraśītalagātrī sā bhavaty amaravarṇini
subhagā darśanīyā ca putravaty api bhāmini
paurṇamāsyāṃ tu satataṃ prāpte somodaye 'ṅganā
arghyaṃ dadyāt sumanasā sākṣataṃ sakuśaṃ tathā
yāvakaṃ ca baliṃ dadyād dadhinā saha saṃyutam
evaṃ yā kurute nityaṃ sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt
adṛṣṭvā yā tu nāśnāti sūryaṃ nārī pativratā
durdine vātha vā vyabhre sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt
kāñcanaṃ śaktito dadyāt sā viprāya manasvinī
subhagā darśanīyā ca bhavaty amaravarṇinī
umovāca
niveṣṭavyaṃ śarīraṃ yair vratakaiḥ puṇyair api
arundhati pravakṣyāmi sahaitabhir vare śṛṇu
kṛṣṇāṣṭamīṃ yā kṣipati syād vā mūlaphalāśinī
brāhmaṇāyaikam aśanaṃ dattvā bhartṛdevatā
śuklavastrā śubhācārā gurudaivatapūjakā
evaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ kṛtvā tato dadyād dvijātaye
govājarajjusukṛtaṃ cāmaraṃ balvajaṃ tathā
dakṣiṇāpūrvam iṣṭānnaṃ śaktyā vāpi śucismite
urmimantaḥ svarālāgrāḥ śroṇideśāvalambanaḥ
tasyā bhavanti keśās tu bhavatīṣṭā hi bhartare
śiro nirveṣṭukāmā tu gomayena śiraḥ satī
prakṣālayen malaṃ dhātryā bilvena śrīphalena ca
gomūtraṃ ca sadā prāśec chiraḥsnānaṃ ca miśrayet
kṛṣṇāṃ caturdaśīṃ tv etat kartavyaṃ varavarṇini
bhavaty avidhavā caiva subhagā vijvarā tathā
śirorogair naiva cāsyāḥ śarīram abhitapyate
darśanīyaṃ lalāṭaṃ yā kāṅkṣati strī śucismite
tithiṃ pratipadaṃ nityaṃ sā kṣaped ekabhojanā
payasā ca tathāśnīyād yāvat saṃvatsaro gataḥ
brāhmaṇasya tato dadyāt paṭṭaṃ rūpyamayaṃ śubham
lalāṭaṃ rūpasaṃpannam āpnoti strī sumadhyamā
satataṃ strī dvitīyāyāṃ bhruvor icchet surūpatām
anantaropavāsane śākabhaktāśanā satī
tataḥ saṃvatsare pūrṇe brāhmaṇaṃ svasti vācayet
phalaiḥ pariṇataiḥ saumye māsāṇāṃ dakṣiṇānvitaiḥ
lavaṇena ca bhadraṃ te ghṛtapātreṇa cānaghe
ātmanaḥ śobhanau karṇāv icchantī strī sumadhyamā
nakṣatre śravaṇe prāpte dhruvaṃ bhuñjīta yāvakam
tataḥ saṃvatsare pūrṇe karṇau dadyād dhiraṇmayau
ghṛte prakṣipya viprāya payasā sahitau śubhe
nāsām icchel lalāṭāntām avyaṅgāṃ vyādhivarjitām
tilagulmaṃ sadā siñced yāvat puṣped dhi rakṣitaḥ
anantaropavāsena sektavyaḥ salilaiḥ sadā
tasmād ādāya puṣpāṇi ghṛte prakṣipya dāpayet
svakṣī bhaveyam iti yā strī kāṅkṣaty amṛtodbhave
anantaraṃ vai bhuñjānā payasā vā ghṛtena vā
tataḥ saṃvatsare pūrṇe padmapatrāṇi paṇḍitā
tathaivotpalapatrāṇi nyaset kṣīre śucismite
plavamānāni viprāya tato dadyāt satī sati
kṛṣṇasārasamānākṣī tad dattva bhavati sma vai
icched oṣṭhau cārurūpau yā strī dharmaguṇānvitā
sā mṛṇmayena tu pibed udakaṃ vatsaraṃ satī
ayācitena bhuñjīta navamyāṃ dharmabhāginī
tataḥ saṃvatsare pūrṇe vidrumaṃ dātum arhati
tena bimbaphalābhoṣṭhī strī bhavaty eva śobhane
subhagāyavapuḥputradhanāḍhyā gomatī tathā
yā cārurūpān iccheta dantān amaravarṇini
śuklāṣṭamīṃ na sāśnīyād bhaktadvayam aninditā
tataḥ saṃvatsare pūrṇe dadyād rūpyamayān satī
dantān prkṣipya dharmajñe payasy atiguṇodite
tena sā tilapuṣpābhān dantān āpnoti sā satī
saubhāgyam api cāpnoti saputratvaṃ tathānaghe
sarvam eva mukhaṃ kāntam icched yā rucirānane
sā paurṇamāsyām aśnātu prāpte candrodaye śubhe
yāvakaṃ payasā siddhaṃ dattvā viprāya bhāminī
tataḥ saṃvatsare pūrṇe candraṃ rūpyamayaṃ śubham
padme phulle tu vinyasya brāhmaṇān svasti vācayet
pūrṇacandramukhī tena dānena strī śubhe bhavet
stanāv icchati yā nārī tṛṇarājaphalopamau
ayācitaṃ daśamyāṃ sā nityam aśnīta vāgyatā
saṃvatsare tataḥ pūrṇe dve bilve kāñcane śubhe
sadakṣiṇe brāhmaṇāya prayacchatu dhṛtātmane
saubhāgyaṃ param āpnoti bahūn putrāṃs tathaiva ca
sadonnatau stanau sā strī bibharty amaravarṇini
śātodāratvam icchantī kṣaped ekānnabhojinī
pañcamyāṃ tu na bhoktavyaṃ annaṃ toyena nityadā
tataḥ saṃvatsare pūrṇe dadyāj jatilatāṃ śubhe
phullāṃ sadakṣiṇāṃ dhanye brāhmaṇāya dhṛtāmane
hastāv icchati yā nārī rūpayuktau sumadhyame
dvādaśīṃ sā kṣaped evaṃ śākaiḥ sarvair aninditaiḥ
saṃvatsare tataḥ pūrṇe raukme padme dadātu sā
brāhmaṇāyābhirūpāya tathā padmadvayaṃ śubhe
śroṇīṃ viśālām anvicchet strī kṣapetv eva suvratā
trayodaśīm ekabhaktam aśnātv evam ayācitam
tataḥ saṃvatsare pūrṇe lavaṇaṃ saṃprayacchatu
prajāpatimukhākāraṃ kṛtvā tajjñā varānane
kāñcanaṃ caiva dātavyaṃ tadākārasya sarvadā
añjanena ca dharmajñe śanakair avacūrṇayet
ratnāni caiva pūrṇāni vāso raktaṃ ca dāpayet
tena śroṇīm abhimatāṃ strī saumye pratipadyate
madhurāṃ vācam icchantī varjayel lavaṇaṃ satī
saṃvatsare vā māsaṃ vā dāpayel lavaṇaṃ tataḥ
sadakṣiṇaṃ brāhmaṇāya paraṃ mādhuryam icchatī
śukavākyāc chataguṇaṃ bhavaty amaravarṇini
gūḍhagulphaśirau pādāv icchantyā somanandini
ṣaṣṭhyāṃ ṣaṣṭhyāṃ varārohe bhoktavyaṃ satilaudanam
agnir vā brāhmaṇo vāpi na spraṣṭavyaḥ padā sadā
padā yadā spṛśet taṃ ca vandeta tapasānvitā
pādena caiva pādaṃ na prakṣālayitum arhati
etair nityavratair yuktā dharmajñā patidevatā
kūrmau rukmamayau dadyād brāhmaṇāya pativrate
tau vācayed brāhmanāya sthāpayitvā ghṛte 'naghe
padme cādhomukhe kṛtvā dadyād viprāya nandini
raktair dravyair miśrayitvā kāñcanenābhyalaṃkṛtau
sarvam eva tu yā gātram icchaty atimanoharam
trirātraṃ puṣpakāle sā karoti patidevatā
kaumudyām atha vāṣāḍhyāṃ māghyāṃ cāśvayuje tathā
mātaraṃ pitaraṃ caiva manyate yadi daivatam
ghṛtaṃ ca nityaṃ viprebhyo dadātu lavaṇaṃ tathā
saṃmārjanaṃ gṛhe caiva karotu patidevatā
upalepanaṃ ca dharmajñe balikarma ca mānini
vāgduṣṭā caiva mā śubhre bhavatv ātmārthapaṇḍitā
paryaśnātu ca sā kaṃcid api śākaṃ yaśasvini
baliṃ sṛjatv atathyaṃ ca parityajatu bhāmini
bāndhavān saguṇān icched ekabhaktena nityadā
saptamīṃ saptamīṃ nityaṃ kṣapet strī patidevatā
tataḥ saṃvatsare pūrṇe vṛkṣaṃ dadyād dhiraṇmayam
sadakṣiṇaṃ brāhmaṇāya śubhabandhumatī bhavet
karañje dīpakaṃ dadyāt sadā yā pramadā vare
pūrṇe saṃvatsare dadyāt sauvarṇaṃ dīpakaṃ tathā
rucyā sā strī bhaved bhartur iṣṭā putravatī tathā
sapatnīnām adhi tathā dīpavaj jvalate śubhe
yā śeṣabhojinī nityaṃ naiva ca syād aruṃtudā
na ca syād vyaśanā saumye nityaṃ ca patidevatā
śaucānvitā ca satataṃ na ca rūkṣābhibhāṣiṇī
śvaśrūśvaśurayor nityaṃ śuśrūṣaniratā satī
kiṃ tasyā vratakaiḥ kāryaṃ kiṃ vā syād upavāsakaiḥ
yā bhartur devatā nityaṃ satyadharmaguṇānvitā
vidhavā strī tu yā syād daivayogāt satī sati
tasyā vakṣyāmi yo dharmaḥ purāṇoktaḥ sumadhyame
patiṃ sṃakalpayitvā sā citrasthaṃ vātha mṛnmayam
tasya pūjāṃ sadā kuryāt satāṃ dharmam anusmaret
tata evābhyanujñāṃ ca nityaṃ yācate suvratā
vratake copavāse ca bhojane ca viśeṣataḥ
bhartṛlokān vrajaty evaṃ na ced vyuccarate patim
śāṇḍilī sūryavad bhāti satataṃ patidevatā
adyaprabhṛti sarveṣāṃ devānāṃ caiva yoṣitaḥ
drakṣyanti puṇyakavidhiṃ paurāṇo yaḥ sanātanaḥ
muniś ca nāradaḥ kṛtsnaṃ paurāṇaṃ jñāsyate vidhim
upavāsasya dharmātmā vratakānāṃ tathaiva ca
aditiś cāpi sendrāṇī tvaṃ ca somasute vare
pravartane vratakānāṃ puṇyakānāṃ ca sarvadā
kīrtanīyāḥ satīnāṃ hi bhaviṣyatha guṇānvitāḥ
upavāsavratavidhiṃ yathāvad iha kṛtsnaśaḥ
prādurbhāveṣu sarveṣu viṣṇor bhāryā mahātmanaḥ
jñāsyanti puṇyakavidhiṃ nityam eva sanātanam
saviśeṣaṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ strīdharmeṣu praśasyate
patibhaktir aduṣṭatvam avāgduṣṭatvam eva ca
nārada uvāca
evam uktās tu tāḥ sādhvyo mahādevyā tapodhanāḥ
jagmur hṛṣṭā mahādevīṃ praṇipatya harapriyām
aditir vratakaṃ cakre śṛṇu yad dharmacāriṇī
umāvratavidhiḥ sarvaḥ pūrvoddiṣṭas tayā kṛtaḥ
pārijāte nibadhyātha mama dattas tu kaśyapaḥ
aditivratakaṃ nāma tad dattaṃ satyabhāmayā
tad eva vratakaṃ dattaṃ sāvitryā dharmanityayā
tair eva yuktaiḥ saṃyuktam idaṃ tv abhyadhikaṃ kṛtam
saṃdhyākāle ca saṃprāpte sthāne sthāne tathaiva ca
pūjanaṃ vā namaskāro japaś ca dviguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ
sāvitryā vratakaṃ kṛtvā tathādityā vrataṃ satī
bhartuḥ kulaṃ pitṛkulaṃ tathātmānaṃ ca tārayet
indrāṇī vratakaṃ cakre tathaivomā yathāvidhi
raktaṃ abhyadhikaṃ vāso bhojanaṃ caiva sāmiṣam
caturthe divase cāpi puṇyakārthavidhiḥ punaḥ
ahorātropavāsaś ca deyaṃ kumbhaśataṃ tathā
gaṅgayā vratakaṃ dattaṃ tad evaumaṃ yaśaskari
snānam abhyadhikaṃ kāryaṃ pratyūṣasyātmano jale
anyatra vā jale māgha śuklapakṣe haripriye
etad gaṅgāvrataṃ nāma sarvakāmapradaṃ smṛtam
sapta sapta ca saptātha kulāni harivallabhe
strī tārayati dharmajñā gaṅgāvratakacāriṇī
deyaṃ kumbhasahasraṃ tu gaṅgāyā vratake śubhe
tāraṇaṃ pāraṇaṃ caiva tad vrataṃ sārvakāmikam
yamabhāryā cakārātha vrataṃ yāmarathaṃ śubham
hemante tat tukartavyam ākāśe harivallabhe
imāni caiva vākyāni brūyād ākāśam āsthitā
snātā śucisamācārā namaskṛtya patiṃ śubhe
carāmy ahaṃ yāmarathaṃ himaṃ pṛṣṭhena dhāraye
pativratā jīvaputrā bhaveyaṃ ca purodhikā
sapatnīś cādhitiṣṭheyaṃ paśyeyaṃ caiva mā yamam
sabhartṛputrā jīveyaṃ ciraṃ sumukham eva ca
patilokaṃ ca gaccheyaṃ bhaveyaṃ nandinī tathā
sucelā mṛṣṭahastā ca svajaneṣṭā guṇānvitā
evaṃ kṛtvā tato vipraṃ madhunā svasti vācayet
tilair api tathā kṛṣṇaiḥ pāyasena tu bhojayet
evaṃ vratāni devībhiḥ kṛtāny amaravarṇini
mahādevyā puroktāni rudrapatnyā haripriye
ahaṃ bravīmi tapasā madīyena samanvitā
sarvā drakṣyatha puṇyāni vratakāni tathaiva ca
paurāṇāny umayā devyā yāni dṛṣṭāni vai purā
kalyāṇaguṇayuktāni pāvanāni śubhāni ca
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
rukmiṇī vratakaṃ cakre dṛṣṭvā vratakavistaram
umāyā varadānena dṛṣṭvā divyena cakṣuṣā
umāvrateṣu sarveṣu vṛṣadānaṃ tathādhikam
ratnamālāpradānaṃ ca tathānnaṃ sārvakāmikam
tathā jāmbavatī cakre puromāvratakaṃ tathā
dadāv abhyadhikaṃ sā tu ratnavṛkṣaṃ manoharam
satyā dadau tathaivātha puromāvratakaṃ yathā
pītam abhyadhikaṃ vāsas tayā dattam umāvrate
rohiṇyātha ca phālgunyā maghayā ca purātane
vratāni khalu dattāni bahūni kulavardhane
dadau śatabhiṣā caiva vratakaṃ puṇyalakṣaṇam
yena nakṣatramukhyatvaṃ jagāma kurunandana
janamejaya uvāca
vaiśaṃpāyana dharmajña vyāsaśiṣya tapodhana
pārijātasya haraṇe ṣaṭpuraṃ parikīrtitam
nivāso 'suramukhyānāṃ dāruṇānāṃ tapodhana
teṣāṃ vadhaṃ muniśreṣṭha kīrtayasvāndhakasya ca
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tripure nihate vīre rudreṇākliṣṭakarmaṇā
tatra pradhānā bahavo babhūvur asurottamāḥ
śarāgninā na dagdhāste rudreṇa tripurālayāḥ
ṣaṣṭiḥ śatasahasrāṇi na nyūnāny adhikāni ca
te jñātivadhasaṃtaptāś cakrur vīrāḥ purā tapaḥ
jambumārge satām iṣṭe maharṣigaṇasevite
ādityābhimukhāvīrāḥ sahasrāṇāṃ śataṃ samāḥ
vāyubhakṣā nṛpaśreṣṭha stuvantaḥ padmasaṃbhavam
teṣām udumbaraṃ rājan gaṇa ekaḥ samāśritaḥ
vṛkṣaṃ tatrāvasan vīra te kurvanto mahat tapaḥ
kapitthaṃ vṛkṣam āśritya kecit tatroṣitāḥ purā
sṛgālavāṭīṃ tv aparre cerur ugraṃ tathā tapaḥ
vaṭamūle tathā cerus tapaḥ kauravanandana
adhīyantaḥ pare brahma vaṭaṃ gatvāsurātmajāḥ
teṣāṃ tuṣṭaḥ prajākartā naradeva pitāmahaḥ
varaṃ dātuṃ suraśreṣṭhaḥ prāpto dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
varaṃ varayatety uktās te rājan padmayoninā
te neṣur varadānaṃ tu dviṣantas tryambakaṃ vibhum
icchanti 'pacitiṃ gantuṃ jñātīnāṃ kurunandana
tān uvāca tato brahmā sarvajñaḥ kurunandana
viśvasya jagataḥ kartuḥ saṃhartuś ca mahātmanaḥ
kaḥ śakto 'pacitiṃ gantum māstu vo 'tha vṛthā śramaḥ
anādimadhyanidhanaḥ somo devo maheśvaraḥ
tam astūya sukhaṃ svarge vastum icchanti ye 'surāḥ
te neṣus tatra kecit tu durātmāno mahāsurāḥ
atheṣur apare rājann asurā bhavyabhāvanāḥ
neṣur ye sudurātmānas tān uvāca tāmaḥ
varayadhvaṃ varaṃ vīrā rudrakrodham kṛte 'surāḥ
te ūcuḥ sarvadevānām avadhyāḥ syāma he vibho
purāṇi ṣaṭ ca no deva bhavantv antar mahītale
sarvakāmasamṛddhārthaṃ ṣaṭpuraṃ cāstu naḥ prabho
vayaṃ ca ṣaṭpuragatās vasema ca sukhaṃ vibho
rudrāc ca no bhayaṃ na syād yena no jñātayo hatāḥ
nihataṃ tripuraṃ dṛṣṭvā bhītāḥ sma tapasāṃ nidhe
pitāmaha uvāca
asurā bhavatāvadhyā devānāṃ śaṃkarasya ca
na bādhiṣyatha ced viprān satpathasthān satāṃ priyān
vipropaghātaṃ mohāc cet kariṣyatha kathaṃcana
nāśaṃ yāsyatha viprā hi jagataḥ paramā gatiḥ
nārāyaṇād dhi bhetavyaṃ kurvadbhir brāhmaṇāhitam
sarvabhūteṣu bhagavān hitaṃ dhatte janārdanaḥ
te gatā asurā rājan brahmaṇā ye visarjitāḥ
ye 'pi bhaktā mahādevam asurā dharmacāriṇaḥ
svaṃ hi darśanaṃ teṣāṃ dadau tripuranāśanaḥ
śvetaṃ vṛṣabham āruhya somaḥ sapravaraḥ prabhuḥ
uvāca cedaṃ bhagavān asurān sa satāṃ gatiḥ
vairaṃ utsṛjya dambhaṃ ca hiṃsāṃ cāsurasattamāḥ
mām eva cāśritās tasmād varaṃ sādhu dadāmi vaḥ
yair dīkṣitāḥ stha munibhiḥ satkriyāparamair dvijaiḥ
saha tair gamyatāṃ svargaḥ prīto 'haṃ vaḥ sukarmaṇā
iha ye caiva vatsyanti tāpasā brahmavādinaḥ
api kāpitthikāvṛkṣe teṣāṃ lokā yathā mama
iha māsāntapakṣāntau yaḥ kariṣyati mānavaḥ
vānaprathena vidhinā pūjayan māṃ tapodhanaḥn
varṣāṇāṃ sa sahasraṃ tu tapasāṃ prāpsyate phalam
kṛtvā trirātraṃ vidhival lapsyate cepsitaṃ gatim
arkadvīpe nivasato dviguṇaṃ tad bhaviṣyati
nīce deśe ca bhadraṃ vo varam etaṃ dadāmy aham
śvetavāhananāmānaṃ yaś ca māṃ pūjayiṣyati
sarvato bhayacitto 'pi gatiṃ sa mama yāsyati
audumbarān vāṭamūlān dvijān kāpitthikān api
tathā sṛgālavāṭīyān dharmātmāno dṛḍhavratān
munīṃś ca brahmavāṭīyān saviśeṣeṇa ye narāḥ
pūjayiṣyanti satataṃ te yāsyantīpsitāṃ gatim
ity uktvātha mahādevo bhagavāñ śvetavāhanaḥ
tair eva sahitaḥ sarvai rudralokaṃ jagāma vai
jambūmārgaṃ gamiṣyāmi jambūmārge vasāmy aham
evaṃ saṃkalpamāno 'pi rudraloke mahīyate
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
etasminn eva kāle tu caturvedaṣaḍaṅgavit
brāhmaṇo yājñyavalkasya śiṣyo dharmaguṇānvitaḥ
brahmadatteti vikhyāto vipro vājasaneyivān
aśvamedhaḥ kṛtas tena vasudevasya dhīmataḥ
sa sāṃvatsaradīkṣāyāṃ dīkṣitaḥ ṣaṭpurālayaḥ
āvartāyāḥ śubhe tīre sunadyā munijuṣṭayā
sakhā tu vasudevasya sahādhyāyī dvijottamaḥ
upādhyāyaś ca kauravya kṣīrahotā mahātmanaḥ
vasudevas tatra yāto devakyā sahitaḥ prabho
yajamānaṃ ṣaṭpurasthaṃ yathā śakro bṛhaspatim
tat satraṃ brahmadattasya bahvannaṃ bahudakṣiṇam
upāsanti muniśreṣṭhā mahātmāno dṛḍhavratāḥ
vyāso 'haṃ yājñavalkyaś ca sumantur jaiminis tathā
dhṛtimāñ jājaliś caiva devalādyāś ca bhārata
ṛddhyānurūpayā yuktaṃ vasudevasya dhīmataḥ
yatrepsitān dadau kāmān devakī dharmacāriṇī
vāsudevaprabhāvena jagat sraṣṭuṃ mahīpate
tasmin satre vartamāne daityāḥ ṣaṭpuravāsinaḥ
nikumbhādyāḥ samāgamya tam ucur varadarpitāḥ
kalpyatāṃ yajñabhāgo naḥ somaṃ pāsyāmahe vayam
kanyāś ca brahmadatto no yajamānaḥ prayacchatu
bahvyaḥ santy asya kanyāś ca rūpavatyo mahātmanaḥ
āhūya tāḥ pradātavyāḥ sarvathaiva hi naḥ śrutam
ratnāni ca brahmadatto viśiṣṭāni dadātu naḥ
anyathā tu na yaṣṭavyaṃ vayam ājñāpayāmahe
etac chrutvā brahmadattas tān uvāca mahāsurān
yajñabhāgo na vihitaḥ purā vo 'surasattamāḥ
kathaṃ sattre somapānaṃ śakyaṃ dātuṃ mayā hi vaḥ
pṛcchatheha muniśreṣṭhān vedabhāṣyārthakovidān
kanyā hi mama yā deyās tāś ca saṃkalpitā mayā
antarvedyāṃ pradātavyāḥ sadṛśānām asaṃśayam
ratnāni tu prayacchāmi sāntvenāhaṃ vicintya vai
balān naiva pradāsyāmi devakīputram āśritaḥ
nikumbhādyās tu ruṣitāḥ pāpāḥ ṣaṭpuravāsinaḥ
yajñavāṭaṃ vilulupur jahruḥ kanyāś ca tās tathā
taṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃpravṛttaṃ tu dadhyāv ānakaduṃdubhiḥ
vāsudevaṃ mahātmānaṃ balabhadraṃ gadaṃ tathā
viditārthas tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pradyumnam idam abravīt
gaccha kanyāparitrāṇaṃ kuru putrāśu māyayā
yāvad yāvanasainyena ṣaṭpuraṃ yāmy ahaṃ prabho
sa yayau ṣaṭpuraṃ vīraḥ pitur ājñākaras tadā
nimeṣāntaramātreṇa gatvā kāmo mahābalaḥ
kanyās tā māyayā dhīmān ājahre sa mahābalaḥ
māyāmayīś ca kṛtvānyā nyastavān rukmiṇīsutaḥ
mā bhair iti ca dharmātmā devakīm uktavāṃs tadā
māyāmayīs tu tā hatvā sutā hy asya durāsadāḥ
ṣaṭpuraṃ viviśur daityāḥ parituṣṭā nārādhipa
karma cāsārya te tatra vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā
yad viśiṣṭaṃ bahuguṇaṃ tad abhūc ca narādhipa
etasminn antare prāptā rājānas tatra bhārata
satre nimantritāḥ pūrvaṃ brahmadattena dhīmatā
jarāsaṃdho danta vaktraḥ śiśupālas tathaiva ca
pāṇḍavā dhārtarāṣṭrāś ca mālavānāṃ gaṇās tathā
rukmī caivāhvṛtiś caiva nīlo nādhrama eva ca
vindānuvindāv āvantyau ślayaḥ śakunir eva ca
rājānaś cāpare vīrā mahātmāno dṛḍhāyudhāḥ
āvāsitā nātidūre ṣaṭpurasya ca bhārata
tān dṛṣṭvā nāradaḥ śrīmān acintayad aninditaḥ
kṣatrasya yādavānāṃ ca bhaviṣyati samāgamaḥ
atra hetur ayaṃ yuddhe tasmāt tat prayatāmy aham
evaṃ saṃcintayitvā sa nikumbhabhavanaṃ gataḥ
pūjitaḥ sa nikumbhena dānavaiś ca tathāparaiḥ
upaviṣṭaḥ sa dharmātmā nikumbham idam abravīt
kathaṃ virodhaṃ yadubhiḥ kṛtvā svasthair ihāsyate
yo brahmadattaḥ sa kṛṣṇaḥ sa hi tasya pituḥ sakhā
śatāni pañca bhāryāṇāṃ brahmadattasya dhīmataḥ
ānītā vasudevasya sutasya priyakāmyayā
śatadvayaṃ brahmaṇīnāṃ rājanyānāṃ tathā śatam
vaiśyānāṃ śataṃ ekaṃ ca śādrīṇāṃ śatam eva ca
tābhiḥ śuśrūṣito dhīmān durvāsa dharmavittamaḥ
tena tāsāṃ varo datto muninā puṇyakarmaṇā
ekaikas tanayo rānn ekekā duhitā tathā
rūpeṇānupamāḥ sarvā varadānena dhīmataḥ
kanyā bhavanti tanayās tasyāsure punaḥ punaḥ
saṃgame saṃgame vīra bhartṛbhiḥ śayane saha
sarvaṃ puṣpamayaṃ gandhaṃ sravanti ca varāṅganāḥ
sarvadā yauvane nyastāḥ sarvāś caiva pativratāḥ
sarvaguṇair apsarasāṃ gītanṛtyaguṇodayaṃ
jānanti sarvā daiteya varadānena dhīmataḥ
putrāś ca rūpasaṃpannāḥ śāstrārthakuśalās tathā
sve sve sthitā varṇadharme yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ
tāḥ kanyā bhaimamukhyānāṃ dattāḥ prāyeṇa dhīmatā
avaśeṣaṃ śataṃ tv ekaṃ yad ānītaṃ kila tvayā
tadarthe yādavān vīrān yodhayiṣyasi sarvathā
sāhāyyārthe tu rājāno vriyantāṃ hetupūrvakam
brahmadattasutārthaṃ ca rātnāni vividhāni ca
dīyantāṃ bhūmipālānāṃ sāhāyyārthaṃ mahātmanām
ātithyaṃ kriyatāṃ caiva ye sameṣyanti vai nṛpāḥ
evam ukte tathā cakrur asurās te 'tihṛṣṭavat
labdhvā pañcaśataṃ kanyā ratnāni vividhāni ca
yathārheṇa narendrais tā vibhaktā bhaktivatsalāḥ
ṛte pāṇḍusutān vīrān vāritā nāradena te
nimeṣāntaramātreṇa tatra gatvā mahātmnanā
tuṣṭais tair asurā hy uktā rājan bhūmipasattamaiḥ
sarvakāmasamṛddhārthkair bhavadbhiḥ khagamaiḥ svayam
arcitāḥ sma yathānyāyaṃ kṣatraṃ suraripus tadā
kṣatraṃ nārcitapūrvaṃ hi divyair vīrair bhavadvidhaiḥ
nikumbho 'thābravīd dhṛṣṭaḥ kṣatraṃ suraripus tadā
anuvarṇayitvā kṣatrasya mahātmyaṃ satyam eva ca
yuddhaṃ no ripubhiḥ sārdhaṃ bhaviṣyati nṛpottamāḥ
sāhāyyaṃ dattam iccchāmo bhavadbhis tatra sarvathā
evam astv iti tān ūcuḥ kṣatriyāḥ kṣīṇakilbiṣāḥ
pāṇḍaveyān ṛte vīrāñ śrutārthān nāradād vibho
kṣatriyāḥ saṃniviṣṭās te yuddhārthaṃ kurunandana
patnyas tu brahmadattasya yajñavāṭaṃ gatā api
kṛṣṇo 'pi senayā sārdhaṃ prayayau ṣaṭpuraṃ vibhuḥ
mahādevasya vacanam udvahan manasā nṛpa
sthāpayitvā dvāravatyāṃ āhukaṃ pārthivaṃ tadā
sa tayā senayā sārdhaṃ paurāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā
yajñyavāṭasyāvidūre devo niviviśe vibhuḥ
deśe pravarakalyāṇe vasudevapracoditaḥ
dattāgulmāpratisaraṃ kṛtvā taṃ vidhivat prabhuḥ
pradyumnam aṭane śrīmān rakṣārthaṃ viniyujya ca
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
muhūrtābhyudite sūrye janacakṣuṣi nirmale
balaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sātyakiś ca tārkṣyam āruruhur mudā
baddhagodhāṅgulitrāṇā daṃśitā yuddhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
bilvodakeśvaraṃ devaṃ namaskṛtyāsurottamam
āvartāyā jale snātvā rudreṇa varadattayā
gaṅgāyāḥ kuruśārdūla rudravākyena puṇyayā
pradyumnam agre sainyasya viyati sthāpya mānada
rakṣārthaṃ yajñavāṭasya pāṇḍavān viniyujya ca
śeṣāṃ senāṃ guhādvāri bhagavān viniyujya ca
jayantam atha sasmāra pravaraṃ ca satāṃ gatiḥ
tāv āpetatur evātha svayaṃ cāpaśyatāṃ tathā
viyaty eva niyuktau tau pradyumna iva bhārata
tataḥ kṛṣṇasya vacanād āhato raṇaduṃdubhiḥ
jalajā murajāś caiva vādyāny apy aparāṇi ca
mākaro racito vyūhaḥ sāmbena ca gadena ca
sāraṇaś coddhavaś cobhau bhojo vaitaraṇas tathā
anādhṛṣṭiś ca dharmātmā vipṛthuḥ pṛthur eva ca
kṛtavarmā ca daṃṣṭre dve vicakṣur arimardanaḥ
sanatkumāro dhkarmātmā cārudeṇṣaś ca bhārata
aniruddhasahāyau tau pṛṣṭhānīkaṃ rarakṣatuḥ
śeṣā yādavasenā tu vyūhamadhye vyavasthitā
rathair aśvair narair nāgair ākulā kulavardhana
ṣaṭpurād api niṣkrāntā dānavā yuddhadurmadāḥ
āruhya meghanādāṃś ca gardabhān api hastinaḥ
makarāñ śiśumārāṃś ca hayān api ca bhārata
mahiṣān atha khaḍgāṃś ca drutān api ca kacchapān
etair eva rathair yuktair vividhāyudhapāṇayaḥ
kirīṭāpīḍamukuṭair aṅgadair api maṇḍitāḥ
nānardamānair vividhais tūryair nemisvanākulaiḥ
pradhmāyamānaiḥ śaṅkhaiś ca mahkkāmbudasamasvanaiḥ
tāsām asurasenāsām udyatānāṃ janeśvara
nikumbho niryayau agre devānām iva vāsavaḥ
bhūmiṃ dyāṃ ca vavṛdhire dānavās te balotkaṭāḥ
nadanto vividhān nādān kṣveḍantaś ca punaḥ punaḥ
rājasenāpi saṃyattā cedirājapurogamā
asurāṇāṃ sahāyārthaṃ niścitā janamejaya
duryodhanabhrātṛśataṃ cedirājānugāgragam
sthitaṃ narair naravyāghra gandharvanagarupamaiḥ
kaṭhinā nādino vīrā drupadasyandanās tathā
rukmī caivāhvṛtiś caiva tasthatur niścitau raṇe
tālavṛkṣapratīkāśe dhunvānau dhanuṣī śubhe
śalyaś ca śakuniś cobhau bhagadattaś ca pārthivaḥ
jarāsaṃdhas trijgartaś ca virāṭaś ca sahottaraḥ
yuddhārtham udyatā vīrā nikumbhādyā jayaiṣiṇaḥ
yuyutsamānā yadubhir devair iva mahāsurāḥ
tato nikumbhaḥ samare śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥ
mamarda samare senāṃ bhaimnānāṃ bhīmadarśanām
senāpatir anādṛṣṭir mamṛṣe tan na yādavaḥ
mamarda ghorair bāṇaughaiś citrapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥ
na ratho 'suramukhyasya dadṛśe na ca vājinaḥ
na dhvajo na nikumbhaś ca sarvaṃ bāṇābhisaṃvṛtam
sa parītya tato vīro nikumbho māyināṃ varaḥ
astambhayad anāvṛṣṭiṃ māyayā bhaimasattamam
stambhayitvānayad vīraṃ guhāṃ ṣaṭpurasaṃjñitām
ruddhvā cābhyagamad vīraṃ māyābalam upāśritaḥ
punar eva nikumbhas tu kṛtavarmāṇam āhave
anayac cārudeṣṇaṃ ca bhojaṃ vaitaraṇaṃ tathā
sanatkumāraṃ tārkṣyaṃ ca tathaiva niśaṭholmukau
bahūṃś caivāparān bhojān māyābalasamāśritaḥ
na tasya dadṛśe deho māyācchanno janeśvara
nayato yādavān ghorān guhāṃ ṣaṭpurasaṃjñitām
tad dṛṣṭvā kadanaṃ ghoraṃ bhaimānāṃ bhītivardhanam
cukopa bhagavān kṛṣṇo balaḥ satyaka eva ca
saviśeṣaṃ tathā kāmaḥ sāmbaś ca paravīrahā
aniruddhaś ca durdharṣo bhaimāś ca bahavo 'pare
tataḥ śārṅgāyudhaḥ śārṅgaṃ kṛtvā sajyaṃ nareśvara
dānaveṣu pravṛtteṣu tṛṇeṣv iva hutāśanaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā dānavā devam abhidudruvur īśvaram
śalabhāḥ kālapāśārtāḥ pradīptam iva pāvakam
samutsṛjya śataghnīś ca parighāṃś ca sahasraśaḥ
śūlāni cāgnitulyāni pradīptāṃś ca paraśvadhān
parvatāgrāṇi vṛkṣāṃś ca ghorāś ca vipulāḥ śilāḥ
utkṣipya ca gajān mattān rathān api hayān api
nārāyaṇāgnis tān sarvān dadāha prahasann iva
bāṇārciṣā mahātejā jagaddhitakaro hariḥ
śāradaṃ varṣaṇaṃ yadvat sahed vīra gavāṃ patiḥ
tadvad yaduvṛṣaḥ sehe bāṇavarṣam ariṃdamaḥ
na sehire 'surā bāṇān nārāyaṇadhanuścyutān
varṣaṃ parjanyavihitaṃ vālukāsetavo yathā
na śekuḥ pramukhe sthātuṃ kṛṣṇasyāsurasattamāḥ
vyāditāsyasya siṃhasya vṛṣabhā iva bhārata
te vadhyamānāḥ kṛṣṇena divam ācakramus tadā
jīvitāśāṃ vahantas tu nārāyaṇabhayārditāḥ
tān ākāśagatān aindrir jayantaḥ pravaras tadā
nijaghnatuḥ śarair ghorair jvalanārciḥsamaprabhaiḥ
nipetur asurāṇāṃ tu śirāṃsi dharaṇītale
tṛṇarājaphalānīva muktāni śikharāt taroḥ
nipetur bahavaś cchinnā daityānāṃ vasudhātale
kālenopahatā vīra pañcavaktrā ivoragāḥ
raukmiṇeyas tataḥ sṛṣṭvā ghorāṃ māyāmayīṃ guhām
adṛśyaniṣkramāṃ vīraḥ kṣatraṃ prakṣeptum udyataḥ
gadena saha dharmātmā sāraṇena śaṭhena ca
sāmbena cāparaiś cāpi pūrvaṃ yena praveśitāḥ
pramathya tarasā karṇaṃ yatantaṃ raṇamūrdhani
jagrāha balavān kārṣṇiḥ prasphurantaṃ tatas tataḥ
vinadya ca guhāṃ vīro ghorāṃ māyāmayīṃ nṛpa
duryodhanaṃ ca rājānaṃ virāṭadrupadāv api
śakuniṃ caiva śalyaṃ ca nīlaṃ cāpi nadīsutam
vindānuvindau rājānau jarāsaṃdhaṃ ca bhārata
trigartān mālavāṃś caiva vasātīṃś ca mahābalān
dhṛṣṭadyumnādikāṃś caiva pañcālām astrakovidām
tathāhvṛtim uvācedaṃ mātulaṃ rukmim eva ca
śiśupālaṃ ca rājānaṃ bhagadattaṃ ca bhārata
saṃbamdhaṃ ca gurutvaṃ ca mānayāmi narādhipāḥ
guhām imāṃ ghorarūpāṃ yena prakṣepayāmi vaḥ
bilvodakeśvareṇāham ājñaptaḥ śūlapāṇinā
prakṣeptavyā narendrās te guhāyām iti dhīmatā
āśritya śāmbarīṃ māyāṃ nikumbhena mahātmanā
prakṣiptān yādavāṃś caiva mākṣayiṣyāmi sarvathā
ity ukte śiśupālas tu rājā senapatis tathā
śarais tatarda tān bhaimān pradyumnaṃ saviśeṣataḥ
bilvodakeśvaraṃ devaṃ raukmiṇeyo namasya ca
ārambhan nṛpatiṃ baddhuṃ śiśupālaṃ mahābalam
tataḥ pāśasahasrāṇi grahāya pravarottamaḥ
śailādir abravīd vīraṃ raukmiṇeyaṃ mahābalam
bilvodakeśvaro devaḥ prāha tvāṃ yadunandana
sarvaṃ kuru yathā rātryāṃ proktas tvaṃ bhaima māyayā
kanyārthaṃ ratnalubdhāṃs tu badhānemān narādhipān
pāśais tvam eva moktuṃ ca pramāṇaṃ yadunandana
asurāṃs tu mahābāho niḥśeṣān kartum arhasi
evam eva ca vaktavyas tvayā vīra janārdanaḥ
tataḥ sa bhagadattaṃ ca śiśupālaṃ ca bhūmipam
āhvṛtiṃ caiva rumiṃ ca śeṣāṃś cānyān narādhipān
babandha haradattais taiḥ pāśair uttamavīryavān
māyāmayīṃ guhāṃ caiva nināya kurunandana
baddhvā ca raukmiṇeyo 'tha niḥśvasanta ivoragān
aniruddhaṃ cakārātha rakṣitāraṃ svam ātmajam
teṣāṃ niravaśeṣeṇa babandha yadunandanaḥ
senapatiṃ kṣatriyāṃś ca kośādhyakṣāṃś ca bhārata
hastyaśvarathavṛndāṃś ca cakāra ca tathātmasāt
avyagras tu tato hantum asurān udyataḥ prabho
saṃnaddha eva covāca brahmadattaṃ dvijottamam
viśrabdhaṃ vartatāṃ karma mā bhaiḥ paśya dhanaṃjayam
na devebhyo nāsurebhyo nānyebhyo dvijasattama
bhayaṃ hi vidyate tasya goptāro yasya pāṇḍavāḥ
na cāsurais tava sutāḥ spṛṣṭāḥ khalv api tejasā
yajñavaṭe nirīkṣyaitān māyayā nihitā mayā
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
rudreṣu bhūmipāleṣu sānugeṣu viśāṃ pate
āviveśāsurāṃś caiva kaśmalaṃ janamejaya
diśaḥ prasasrus te vārā vadhyamānāḥ samantataḥ
kṛṣṇānantaprabhṛtibhir yadubhir yuddhadurmadaiḥ
nikumbhas tān athovāca ruṣito dānavottamaḥ
bhittvā pratijñāṃ kiṃ mohād bhayārtā yātha vihvalāḥ
hīnapratijñāḥ kāṃl lokān prayāsyatha palāyitāḥ
agatvāpacitiṃ yuddhe jñātīnāṃ kṛtaniścayāḥ
phalaṃ jitveha bhoktavyaṃ ripūn samarakarkaśān
hatena cāpi śūreṇa vastavyaṃ tridive sukham
palāyitvā grḥaṃ gatvā kasya drakṣyatha he mukham
dārān vakṣyatha kiṃ cāpi dhig dhik kiṃ kiṃ na lajjatha
evam uktā nivṛttās te lajjamānā nṛpāsurāḥ
dviguṇena ca vegena yuyudhur yadubhiḥ saha
utsave yuddhaśauṇḍānāṃ nānāpraharaṇair nṛpa
ye yānti yajñavāṭaṃ tu tān nihati dhanaṃjayaḥ
yamau bhīmaś ca rājā ca dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
dyāṃ prayātāj jaghānaindriḥ pravaraśca dvijottamaḥ
athāsurāsṛktoyāḍhyā keśaśaivalaśāḍvalā
cakrakūrmarathāvartā gajaśailānuśobhinī
dhvajakuntatarucchannā stanitotkruṣṭaśabdinī
govindaśailaprabhavā bhīrucittapramāthinī
asṛgbudbudaphenāṣhyā asimatsyataraṃgiṇī
susrāva śoṇitanadī nadīva jalād āgame
tāṃ dṛṣṭvaiva nikumbhas tu vardhamānāṃś ca śātravān
hatān sarvān sahāyāṃś ca vīryād evotpapāta ha
sa vārito jayantena pravareṇa ca bhārata
śaraiḥ kuliśasaṃkāśair nikumbho raṇakarkaśaḥ
saṃnivṛtyātha daṣṭauṣṭaiḥ parigheṇa durāsadaḥ
pravaraṃ tāḍayām āsa sa papāta mahītale
aindris taṃ patitaṃ bhūmau bāhubhyāṃ parṣasvaje
viditvā caiva saprāṇaṃ hitvāsuram abhidrutaḥ
abhidrutya nikumbhaṃ ca nistriṃśena jaghana ha
parigheṇāpi daiteyo jayantaṃ samatāḍayat
tatakṣa bahulaṃ gātraṃ nikumbhasyaindrir āhave
sa cintayām āsa tadā vadhyamāno mahāsuraḥ
kṛṣṇena saha yoddhavyaṃ vairiṇā jñātighātinā
śrāvayāmi kim ātmānam āhave śakrasūnunā
evaṃ sa niścayaṃ kṛtvā tattraivāntaradhīyata
jagāma caiva yuddhārthaṃ yatra kṛṣṇo mahābalaḥn
taṃ dṛṣvairāvataskandham āsthito balanāśanaḥ
draṣṭum abhyāgato yuddhaṃ jahṛṣe saha daivataiḥ
sāghu sādhv iti putraṃ ca parituṣṭaḥ sa sasvaje
pravaraṃ cāpi dharmātmā sasvaje mohavarjitam
devaduṃdubhayaś cāpi praṇedur vāsavājñayā
jayamānaṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā jayantaṃ raṇadurjayam
dadarśātha nikumbhas tu keśavaṃ raṇadurjayam
arjunena sthitaṃ sārdhaṃ yajñavāṭāvidūrataḥ
sa nādaṃ sumahat kṛtvā pakṣirājam atāḍayat
parigheṇa sughoreṇa balaṃ sātyakim eva ca
nārāyaṇaṃ cārjunaṃ ca bhīmaṃ cātha yudhiṣṭhiram
yamau ca vasudevaṃ ca sāmbaṃ kāmaṃ ca vīryavān
yuyudhe māyayā daityaḥ śīghrakārī ca bhārata
na cainaṃ dadṛśuḥ sarve sarvaśastraviśāradāḥ
yadā tu naiva paśyanti tadā bilvodakeśvaram
dadhyau devaṃ hṛṣīkeśaḥ pramathānāṃ gaṇeśvaram
tatas te dadṛśuḥ sarve prabhāvād atitejasaḥ
bilvodakeśvarasyāśu nikumbhaṃ māyināṃ varam
kailāsaśikharākāraṃ grasantam iva dhiṣṭhitam
āhvayantaṃ raṇe kṛṣṇaṃ vairiṇaṃ jñātināśanam
sajjagāṇḍīva evātha pārthas tasya ratheṣubhiḥ
parighaṃ caiva gātreṣu vivyādhainam athāsakṛt
te bāṇās tasya gātreṣu parighaś ca janādhipa
bhagnāḥ śilāśitāḥ sarve nipetuḥ kuñcitāḥ kṣitau
viphalān astrayuktāṃs tān dṛṣṭvā bāṇān dhanaṃjayaḥ
papraccha keśavaṃ vīraḥ kim etad iti bhārata
parvatān api bhindanti mama vajropamāḥ śarāḥ
kim idaṃ devakīputra vismayo 'tra mahān mama
tam uvāca tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ prahasann iva bhārata
mahadbhūtaṃ nikumbho 'yaṃ kaunteya śṛṇu vistaram
purā gatvottarakurūṃs tapaś cakre mahāsuraḥ
śataṃ varṣasahasrāṇāṃ devaśatrur durāsadaḥ
athainaṃ chandayām āsa vareṇa bhagavān haraḥ
sa vavre trīṇi rūpāṇi navadhyāni surāsuraiḥ
tam uvāca mahādevo bhagavān vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
mama vā brāhmaṇānāṃ vā viṣṇor vāpriyam ācaran
bhaviṣyasi harer vadhyo na tv anyasya mahāsura
bramaṇyo 'haṃ ca viṣṇuś ca viprā naḥ paramā gatiḥ
sa eṣa sarvaśastrāṇām avadhyaḥ pāṇḍunandana
trideho 'tipramāthī ca varadattaś ca dānavaḥ
bhānumatyāpahataṇe deho 'syaiko hato mayā
avadhyaṃ ṣaṭpuraṃ deham idam asya durātmanaḥ
ditiṃ śuśrūṣati tv eko deho 'sya tapasānvitaḥ
anyas tu deho ghoro 'sya yenāvasati ṣaṭpuram
etat te sarvam akhyātaṃ nikumbhacaritaṃ mayā
tvarayāsya vadhe vīra kathā paścād bhaviṣyati
tayoḥ kathayator evaṃ kṛṣṇayor asuras tadā
guhāṃ ṣaṭpurasaṃjñāṃ tāṃ viveśa taṇadurjayaḥ
anviṣya tasya bhagavān viveśa madhusūdanaḥ
tāṃ ṣaṭpuraguhāṃ ghrāṃ durdharṣāṃ kurunandana
candrasūryaprabhāhīnāṃ jvalantīṃ svena tejasā
sukhaduḥkhoṣṇaśītāni prayacchantīṃ yathepsitam
yatra praviśya bhagavān apaśyata janādhipān
yuyudhe saha ghoreṇa nikumbhena janādhipa
kṛṣṇasyānu praviṣṭās tu balādyā yādavās tathā
praviṣṭāś ca tataḥ sarve pāṇḍavāś ca mahātmanaḥ
sametās tu praviṣṭās te kṛṣṇasyānumatena vai
yuyudhe sa tu kṛṣṇena raukmiṇeyaḥ pracoditaḥ
anayad yādavān sarvān yān ayaṃ baddhavān purā
te muktā raukmiṇeyena prāptā yatra janārdanaḥ
prahṛṣṭamanasaḥ sarve nikumbhavadhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
rājāno vīra muñceti punaḥ kāmam athābruvan
mumoca cātha tān vīro raukmiṇeyo pratāpavān
adhomukhamukhāḥ sarve baddhamaunā narādhipāḥ
lajjayābhiplutā vīrās tasthur naṣṭaśriyas tathā
nikumbham appi govindaḥ prayatantaṃ jayaṃ prati
yodhayām āsa bhagavān ghoram ātmaripuṃ hariḥ
parigheṇāhataḥ kṛṣṇo nikumbhena bhṛśaṃ vibho
gadayā cāpi kṛṣṇena nikumbhas tāḍito bhṛśam
tāv ubhau moham āpannau suprahārahatau tadā
tataḥ pravyathitān dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavāṃś cātha yādavān
jepur muṇigaṇās tatra kṛṣṇasya hitakāmyayā
tuṣṭuvuś ca mahātmānaṃ vedaproktais tathā stavaiḥ
tataḥ pratyāgataprāṇo bhagavān keśavas tadā
dānavaś ca punar vīrau udyatau samaraṃ prati
vṛṣabhāv iva nardantau gajāv iva ca bhārata
śālāvṛkāv iva kruddhau praharantau raṇotkaṭau
atha kṛṣṇaṃ tadovāca nṛpa vāg aśarīriṇī
cakreṇa śamasyasvainaṃ devabrāhmaṇakaṇṭakam
iti hovāca bhagavān devo bilvodakeśvaraḥ
dharmaṃ yaśaś ca vipulaṃ prāpnuhi tvaṃ mahābala
tathety uktvā namaskṛtvā lokanāthaḥ satāṃ gatiḥ
sudarśanaṃ mumocātha cakraṃ daityakulāntakam
tan nikumbhasya ciccheda śiraḥ pravarakuṇḍalam
nārāyaṇabhujotsṛṣṭaṃ sūryamaṇḍalavarcasam
tat papāta śiras tasya bhūmau jvalitakuṇḍalam
meghamatto gireḥ śṛṅgān mayūra iva bhūtale
nikumbhe nihate tasmin devo bilvodakeśvaraḥ
tutoṣa ca naravyāghra jagattrāsakare vibho
papāta puṣpavṛṣṭiś ca śakrasṛṣṭā nabhastalāt
devaduṃdubhayś caiva praṇedur arināśana
nananda ca jagat kṛtsnaṃ munayaś ca viśeṣataḥ
daityakanyāś ca bhagavān yadubhyaḥ śataśo dadau
kṣatriyāṇāṃ ca bhagavān sāntvayitvā punaḥ punaḥ
ratnāni ca vicitrāṇi vāsāṃsi pravarāṇi ca
rathānāṃ vājiyuktānāṃ ṣaṭsahasrāṇi keśavaḥ
adadāt pāṇdaveyebhyaḥ prītātmā gadapūrvajaḥ
tad eva cātha pravaraṃ saṭpuraṃ puravardhanaḥ
dvijāya brahmadattāya dadau tārkṣyavaradhvajaḥ
sattre samāpte ca tadā śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
visarjayitvā tat kṣatraṃ pāṇḍavāṃś ca mahābalaḥ
bilvodakeśvarasyātha samājam akarot prabhuḥ
māṃsasūpasamākīrṇaṃ bahvannaṃ vyañjanākulam
niyuddhakuśalān mallān devo mallapriyas tadā
yodhayitvā dadau bhūri vittaṃ vastrāṇi cātmavān
mātāpitṛbhyāṃ sahito yadubhiś ca mahābalaḥ
abhivādya brahmadattaṃ yayau dvāravatīṃ purīm
sa viveśa purīṃ ramyāṃ hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākulām
puṣpacitrapathāṃ vīro vandyamāno naraiḥ pathi
imaṃ yaḥ ṣaṭpuravadhaṃ vijayaṃ cakrapāṇinaḥ
śṛṇuyād vā paṭhed vāppi sa yuddhe jayam āpnuyāt
aputro labhate putram adhano labhate dhanam
vyādhito mucyate rogād baddhaś cpay atha bandhanāt
idaṃ puṃsavanaṃ proktaṃ gaubhādhānaṃ ca bhārata
śrāddheṣu paṭhitaṃ samyag akṣayyakaraṇaṃ smṛtam
idam amaravarasya bhārate
prathitabalasya jayaṃ mahātmanaḥ
satatam iha hi yaḥ paṭhen naraḥ
sugatim ito vrajate gatajvaraḥ
maṇikanakavicitrapāṇipādo
niratiśayārkaguṇo 'rihādimadhyaḥ
caturudadhiśayaś caturvidhātmā
jayati jagatpuruṣaḥ sahasranāmā
janamejaya uvāca
śruto 'yaṃ ṣaṭpuravadho ramyo munivarottama
puroktam andhakavadhaṃ vaiśaṃpāyana kīrtaya
bhānumatyāś ca haraṇaṃ nikumbhasya vadhaṃ tathā
prabrūhi vadatāṃ śreṣṭha paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
ditir hateṣu putreṣu viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
tapasārādhayām āsa mārīcaṃ kaśyapaṃ purā
tapasā kālayuktena tathā śuśrūṣayā muneḥ
ānukūlyena ca tathā mādhuryeṇa ca bhārata
parituṣṭaḥ kaśyapas tu tām uvāca tapodhanām
parituṣṭo 'haṃ te bhadre varaṃ varaya suvrate
ditir uvāca
hataputrāsmi bhagavan devair dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
avaśyaṃ putram icchāmi devair amitavikramam
kaśyapa uvāca
avadhyas te suto devi dākṣāyaṇi bhaved iti
devānāṃ saṃśayo nātra kaścit kamalalocane
devadevam ṛte rudraṃ tasya na prabhavāmy aham
ātmā tatas te putreṇa rakṣitavyo hi sarvathā
anvālabhata tāṃ devīṃ kaśyapaḥ satyavāg atha
aṅgulyodaradeśe tu sā putraṃ suṣuve tataḥ
sahasrabahuṃ kauravya sahasraśirasaṃ tathā
dvisahasrekṣaṇaṃ caiva tāvaccaraṇam eva ca
sa vrajaty andhavad yasmād anandho 'pi hi bhārata
tam andhako 'yaṃ nāmneti procus tatranivāsinaḥ
avadhyo 'smīti lokān sa sarvān bādhati bhārata
haraty api ca ratnāni sarvāṇy ātmabalāśrayāt
vāsayaty ātmavīryeṇa nigṛhyāpsarasāṃ guṇān
sa veśmany ūrjito 'tyarthaṃ sarvalokabhayaṃkaraḥ
paradārāpaharaṇaṃ pararatnavilopanam
cakāra satataṃ mohād andhakaḥ pāpaniścayaḥ
trailokyavijayaṃ kartum udyataḥ satu bhārata
sahāyair asuraiḥ sārdhaṃ bahubhiḥ sarvadharṣibhiḥ
taṃ śrutvā bhagavāñ śakraḥ kaśyapaṃ pitaraṃ bravīt
andhakenedam ārabdham īdṛśam munisattama
ājñāpaya vibho kāryam asmākaṃ samanantaram
yavīyasaḥ kathaṃ nāma soḍhavyaṃ syān mune mayā
iṣṭaputre prahartavyaṃ kathaṃ nāma mayā vibho
ihātrabhavatī kuryān manyuṃ mayi hate sute
devendravacanaṃ śrutvā kaśyapo 'bravīn muniḥ
vārayiṣyāmi devendra sarvathā bhadram astu te
andhakaṃ vārayām āsa dityā saha tu kaśyapaḥ
trailokyavijayād vīra kṛcchrakṛcchreṇa bharata
vārito 'pi sa duṣṭātmā bādhaty eva divaukasaḥ
tais tair upāyair duṣṭātmā pramathya ca tathā parān
babhañja kānane vṛkān udyānāni ca durmatiḥ
uccaiḥśravaḥsutān aśvān balād apy ānayad divaḥ
nāgān diśāgajasutān divyān āpi ca bhārata
balād dharati devānāṃ paśyatāṃ baladarpitaḥ
devān āpyāyante tu ye yajñais tapasā balāt
teṣāṃ cakāra vidhvaṃsaṃ duṣṭātmā devakaṇṭakaḥ
nejur yajñais trayo varṇās tepur naiva tapāṃsy api
andhakasya bhayād rājan yajñavighnāni kurvataḥ
tasyecchayā vāti vāyur ādityaś ca tapaty uta
candramāś ca sanakṣatro dṛśyate naiva vā punaḥ
na bhajanti vimānāni vihāyasy prabhāṃ prabho
andhakasyātighorasya baladṛptasya durmateḥ
niroṃkāravaṣaṭkāraṃ jagad vīra tadābhavat
andhakasyātighorasya bhayāt kurukulodvaha
kurūn athottarān pāpo drāvayām āsa bhārata
bhadrāśvān ketumālāṃś ca jambudvīpāṃs tathaiva ca
mānayanti ca taṃ devā dānavāś ca durāsadāḥ
bhūtāni ca tathānyāni samarthāny api sarvathā
ṛṣayo vadhyamānās tu sametā brahmavādinaḥ
acintayann andhakasya vadhaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
teṣāṃ bṛhaspatir madhye dhīmān idam athābravīt
nāsya rudrād ṛte mṛtyur vidyate ca kathaṃcana
tathā vare dīyamāne kaśyapenāpi śabditaḥ
nāhaṃ rudrāt paritrātuṃ śakta ity eva dhīmatā
tad upāyaṃ cintayāmaḥ śarvo yena sanātanaḥ
jānīyāt sarvabhūtāni pīḍyamānāni śaṃkaraḥ
viditārtho hi bhagavān avaśyaṃ jagataḥ prabhuḥ
aśrupramarjanaṃ devaḥ kariṣyati satāṃ gatiḥ
vrataṃ hi devadevasya bhavasya jagato guroḥ
santo 'sadbhyo rakṣitavyā brāhmaṇās tu viśeṣataḥ
te vayaṃ nāradaṃ sarve prayāmaḥ śaraṇaṃ dvijaṃ
upāyaṃ vetsyate tatra vayasyo hi bhavasya saḥ
bṛhaspativacaḥ śrutvā sarve te 'tha tapodhanāḥ
devā ūcuḥ
trāṇārthaṃ nāradaṃ procus tāṃs tatheti sa coktavān
ṛṣiṣv atha prayāteṣu tat kāryaṃ nārado muniḥ
vicārya manasā vidvān iti kāryaṃ sa dṛṣṭavān
sa devadevaṃ bhagavān draṣṭuṃ munir athāyayau
mandāravanamadhyastho yatra nityaṃ vṛṣadhvajaḥ
sa tatra rajanīm ekām uṣitvā munisattamaḥ
mandārāṇāṃ vane ramnye dayitaḥ śūlapāṇinaḥ
ājagāma punaḥ svargaṃ labdhvānujñāṃ vṛṣadhvajāt
mandārapuṣpaiḥ sukṛtāṃ mālām ābadhya bhārata
grathitāṃ saviśeṣāṃ tāṃ sarvagandhottamottamām
saṃtānamālyadāmaṃ ca sarvais taiḥ kusumaiḥ kṛtam
tac ca kaṇṭhe samāsajya mahāgandhaṃ nārādhipa
āyayāv andhako yatra durātmā baladarpitaḥ
andhakas tv atha taṃ dṛṣṭvā gandham āghrāya cottamam
saṃtānakānāṃ sraṅmālāṃ mahāgandhāṃ mahāmuneḥ
kuto 'yaṃ puṣpajātir vā kamanīyā tapodhana
gandhān varṇāñ śubhāṃs tān hi bhoḥ puṣyati muhur muhuḥ
svarge saṃtānakusumāny ativartanti sarvathā
kaḥ prabhus tasya deśasya yaḥ sa sukṛtavān mune
ācakṣya yady anugrāhyā vayaṃ te devatātithe
tam uvāca muniśreṣṭhaḥ prahasann iva bhārata
grahāya dakṣiṇe haste mahatas tapaso nidhiḥ
mandaraḥ parvataśreṣṭho vīra kāmagamaṃ vanam
tatra caivaṃvidhaṃ puṣpaṃ bhoḥ sṛṣṭiḥ śūlapāṇinaḥ
na tu tatra vanaṃ kaścid acchandena mahātmanaḥ
praveṣṭuṃ labhate tad dhi rakṣanti pramathottamāḥ
nānāpraharaṇā ghorā nānāveṣā durāsadāḥ
avadhyāḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ mahādevābhirakṣitāḥ
nityaṃ prakrīḍate tatra somaḥ sapravaro haraḥ
mandāradrumaṣaṇḍeṣu sarvātmā sarvabhāvanaḥ
tapoviśeṣair ārādhya haraṃ tribhuvaneśvaram
śakyaṃ mandārapuṣpāṇi prāptuṃ kaśyapavaṃśaja
strīratnamaṇiratnāni yāni cānyāni cāpy atha
kāṅkṣitāni phalanti sma te drumā haravallabhāḥ
na tatra sūryaḥ somo 'tha tapaty atulavikrama
svayaṃprabhaṃ taruvanaṃ tad bho duḥkhavivarjitam
tatra gandhāḥ sravanty anye ratnāny anye mahādrumāḥ
vāsāṃsi vividhāny anye sugandhāni mahābala
bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ ca peyaṃ ca coṣyaṃ lehyaṃ tathaiva ca
tarubhyaḥ sravate tebhyo vividhaṃ manasepsitam
pipāsā vā bubhukṣā vā glāniś cintāpi vānagha
na mandāravane vīra bhavatīty upadhāryatām
na te varṇayituṃ śakyā guṇā varṣaśatair api
guṇā ye tatra vartante svargād bahuguṇottarāḥ
atīva vijayel lokān samahendrān na saṃśayaḥ
ekāham api yas tatra vased vai ditijottama
svargasyāpi hi tat svargaṃ sukhānām api sat sukham
babhūva jagataḥ sarvam iti me dhīyate manaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
andhako nāradavacaḥ śrutvā tattvena bhārata
mandaraṃ parvataṃ gantuṃ mano dadhre mahāsuraḥ
so 'surān sumahātejāḥ samānīya mahābalaḥ
jagāma mandaraṃ kruddho mahādevālayaṃ tadā
taṃ mahābhrapraticchannaṃ mahauṣadhisamākulam
nānāsiddhasamākīrṇaṃ maharṣigaṇasevitam
candanāgaruvṛkṣāḍhyaṃ saraladrumasaṃkulam
kiṃnarodgītaramyaṃ ca bahunāgakulākulam
vātoddhūtair vanaiḥ phullair nṛtyantam iva ca kvacit
prasrutair dhātubhiś citrair viliptam iva ca kvacit
pakṣisvanaiḥ sumadhurair nadantam iva ca kvacit
haṃsaiḥ śucipadaiḥ kīrṇaṃ saṃpatadbhir itas tataḥ
mahābalaiś ca mahiṣaiś caradbhir daityanāśanaiḥ
candrāṃśuvimalaiḥ siṃhair bhūṣitaṃ himasaṃcayam
mṛgarājaśatākīrṇaṃ mṛgavṛndaniṣevitam
sa mandaraṃ giriṃ prāha rūpiṇaṃ baladarppitaḥ
vetsi tvaṃ hi yathāvadhyo varadānād ahaṃ pituḥ
mama caiva vaśe sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram
pratiyoddhuṃ na māṃ kaścid icchaty api gire bhayāt
pārijātavanaṃ cāsti tava sānau mahāgire
sarvakāmapradaiḥ puṣpair bhūṣitaṃ ratnam uttamam
tad ācakṣvopabhokṣyāmi tad vanaṃ tava sānujam
kiṃ kariṣyasi kruddhas tvaṃ mano hi tvarate mama
trātāraṃ nānupaśyāmi mayā khalv arditasya te
ity ukto mandaras tena tatraivāntarhito 'bhavat
tato 'ndhako 'tiruṣito varadānena darpitaḥ
mumoca nādaṃ sumahad idaṃ vacanam abravīt
mayā nāma yācyamāno yasmān na bahu manyase
ahaṃ cūrṇīkaromi tvāṃ balaṃ parvata paśya me
evam uktvā gireḥ śṛṅgam utpāṭya bahuyojanam
niṣpipeṣa gires tasya śṛṅge 'thānyatra vīryavān
saha tair asuraiḥ sarvair varadānena darpitaḥ
taṃ pracchannanadījālaṃ bhajyamānaṃ mahāgirim
viditvā bhagavān rudraś cakārānugrahaṃ gireḥ
saviśeṣataraṃ vīra mattadvipamṛgāyutam
nadījālair bahutarair ācitaṃ citrakānanam
nabhaścyutaiḥ purā yadvat tadvad eva virājate
atha devaprabhāvena śṛṅgāṇy utpāṭitāni tu
kṣiptāni cāsurān eva ghnanti ghorāṇi bhārata
kṣiptvā ye prapalāyante śṛṅgāṇi tu mahāsurāḥ
śṛṅais tais taiḥ sma vadhyante parvatasya janādhipa
ye svasthās tv asurās tatra tiṣṭhanti girisānuṣu
śṛṅgais te tasya vadhyante mandarasya mahāgireḥ
tato 'ndhakas tadā dṛṣṭvā senāṃ tāṃ sūditāṃ tathā
ruṣitaḥ sumahānādaṃ naditvedaṃ tadābravīt
āhvayaitaṃ vanaṃ yasya yuddhārtham upatiṣṭhatu
kiṃ tvayācala yuddhena hatāḥ sma cchadmanā raṇe
evam ukte tv andhakena vṛṣabheṇa maheśvaraḥ
saṃprāptaḥ śūlam udyamya devo 'ndhakajighāṃsayā
pramathānāṃ gaṇair dhīmān vṛto vai bahulocanaḥ
tathā bhūtagaṇaiś caiva dhīmān bhūtagaṇeśvaraḥ
pracakampe tataḥ kṛtsnaṃ trailokyaṃ ruṣite hare
sindhavaś ca pratisrotam ūhuḥ prajvalitodakāḥ
jagmur diśo 'gnidāhaṃ ca sarvato haratejasā
yuyudhuś ca grahāḥ sarve viparītā janādhipa
celuś ca girayas tatra kāle kurukulodvaha
pravavarṣātha parjanyaḥ sadhūmāṅgāravṛṣṭimān
uṣṇabhāś candramāś cāsīt sūryaḥ śītaprabhas tathā
na brahma vividus tatra munayyo brahmavādinaḥ
vaḍavāḥ suṣuvur gāś ca gāvo 'śvān api cānagha
petur vṛkṣāś ca medinyām acchinna bhasmasātkṛtāḥ
bādhante vṛṣabhā gāś ca gāvaś cāruruhur vṛṣān
rākṣasā yātudhānāś ca piśācāś cāpi sarvaśaḥ
viparītaṃ jagad dṛṣṭvā mahādevas tathā gatam
mumoca bhagavāñ śūlaṃ pradīptāgnisamaprabham
tat papāta harotsṛṣṭam andhakorasi durdharam
bhasmasāc cākarod raudram andhakaṃ sādhukaṇṭakam
tato devagaṇāḥ sarve munayaś ca tapodhanāḥ
śaṃkaraṃ tuṣṭuvuś caiva jagacchatrau nibarhite
devaduṃdubhayo neduḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ha
trailokyaṃ virvṛtaṃ cāsīn narendra vigatajvaram
prajagur devagandharvā nanṛtuś cāpsarogaṇāḥ
jepuś ca brāhmaṇā vedān ījuś ca kratubhis tathā
grahāḥ prakṛtim āpedur ūhur nadyo yathā purā
na jajvāla jale vahnir āśāḥ sarvāḥ prasedire
mandaraḥ parvataśreṣṭhaḥ pureva virarāja ha
śriyā paramayā juṣṭaḥ sarvatejaḥsamucchrayāt
reme somaś ca bhagavān pārijātavane haraḥ
supracārān surān kṛtvā śakrādīn dharmataḥ prabhuḥ
janamejaya uvāca
mune 'ndhakavadhaḥ śrāvyaḥ śruto 'yaṃ khalu bho mayā
śāntis trayāṇāṃ lokānāṃ kṛtā devena dhīmatā
nikumbhasya hataṃ dehaṃ dvitīyaṃ cakrapāṇinā
yadarthaṃ ca yathā caiva tad bhavān vaktum arhati
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
śraddadhānasya rājendra vaktavyaṃ bhavato 'nagha
caritaṃ lokanāthasya harer amitatejasaḥ
dvāravatyāṃ nivasato viṣṇor atulatejasaḥ
samudrayātrā saṃprāptā tīrthe piṇḍārake nṛpa
ugraseno narapatir vasudevaś ca bhārata
nikṣiptau nagarādhyakṣau śeṣāḥ sarve vinirgatāḥ
pṛthag balaḥ pṛthag dhīmāl lokanātho janārdanaḥ
goṣṭhyaḥ pṛthak kumārāṇāṃ nṛdevāmaratejasām
gaṇikānāṃ sahasrāṇi niḥsṛtāni narādhipa
kumaraiḥ saha vārṣṇeyai rūpavadbhiḥ svalaṃkṛtaiḥ
daityādhivāsaṃ nirjitya yadubhir dṛḍhavikramaiḥ
veśyā niveśitā vīra dvāravatyāṃ sahasraśaḥ
sāmānyās tāḥ kumārāṇāṃ krīḍānāryo mahātmanām
icchābhojyā guṇair eva rājanyā veśayoṣitaḥ
sthitir eṣā hi bhaimānāṃ kṛtā kṛṣṇena dhīmatā
strīnimittaṃ bhaved vairaṃ mā yadunām iti prabho
revatyā caikayā sārdhaṃ balo reme 'nukūlayā
cakravākānurāgeṇa yaduśreṣṭhaḥ pratāpavān
kādambarīpānakalo bhūṣito vanamālayā
cikrīḍa sāgarajale revatyā sahito balaḥ
ṣoḍaśa strīsahasrāṇi jale jalajalocanaḥ
ramayām āsa govindo vaiśvarūpyeṇa sarvakṛt
aham iṣṭā mayā sārdhaṃ jale vasati keśavaḥ
iti tā menire sarvā nārāyaṇaparāḥ striyaḥ
sarvāḥ suratacihnāṅgyaḥ sarvāḥ suratatarpitāḥ
mānam ūhuś ca tāḥ sarvā govinde bahumānajam
aham iṣṭaham iṣṭeti snigdhe parijane tadā
nārāyaṇās triyaḥ sarvā mudā śaślāghire śubhāḥ
karajadvijacihnāni kucādharagatāni tāḥ
dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā jahṛṣire darpaṇeṣv aṅgalakṣaṇam
gotram uddiśya kṛṣṇasya jagire kṛṣṇayoṣitaḥ
pibantya iva kṛṣṇasya nayanair vadanāmbujam
kṛṣṇārpitamanodṛṣṭyaḥ kāntā nārāyaṇastriyaḥ
manoharatarā rājann abhavann ekaniścayāḥ
ekārpitamanodṛṣṭyo nerṣyā tāś cakrire 'ṅganāḥ
nārāyaṇena devena tarpyamāṇamanorathāḥ
śirāṃsi garvitāny ūhuḥ sarvā niravaśeṣataḥ
vāllabhyaṃ keśavamayaṃ vahantyaś cārudarśanāḥ
tābhis tu saha cikrīḍa sarvābhir harir ātmavān
vaiśvarūpyeṇa vidhinā samudre vimale jale
uvāha sarvagandhāḍhyaṃ svacchaṃ vāri mahodadhiḥ
toyaṃ cālavaṇaṃ vīra vāsudevasya śāsanāt
gulphadaghnaṃ jānudaghnam ūrudaghnam athāpi vā
nāryas tāḥ stanadaghnaṃ vā jalaṃ samabhikāṅkṣitam
siṣicuḥ keśavaṃ patnyo dhārā iva mahodadhim
siṣeca taśca govindo meghaḥ phullalatā iva
avalambyāparāḥ kaṇṭhe hariṃ hariṇalocanāḥ
upagūhasva māṃ vīra patāmīty abruvan striyaḥ
kāścit kāṣṭhamayais teruḥ plavaiḥ sarvāṅgaśobhanāḥ
krauñcabarhiṇanāgānām ākārasadṛśaiḥ striyaḥ
makarākṛtibhiś cānyā mīnābhair api cāparāḥ
bahurūpākṛtidharaiḥ pupluvuś cāparāḥ striyaḥ
stanakumbhais tathā terūḥ kumbhair iva tathāparāḥ
samudrasalile ramye harṣayantyo janārdanam
rarāma saha rūkmiṇyā jale tasmin mudā yutaḥ
yenaiva kāryayogena ramaty amarasattamaḥ
tat tad eva hi tāś cakrur mudā nārāyaṇastriyaḥ
tanuvastrāvṛtās tanvyo lilāyantyas tathāparāḥ
cikrīḍur vāsudevasya jale jalajalocanāḥ
yasyā yasyās tu yo bhāvas tāṃ tāṃ tenaiva keśavaḥ
anupraviśya bhāvajño nināyātmavaśaṃ vaśī
hṛṣīkeśo 'pi bhagavān hṛṣīkeśaḥ sanātanaḥ
babhūva vaiśvarūpyeṇa kāntāvaśagataḥ prabhuḥ
kulaśīlasamo 'smākaṃ yogyo 'yam iti menire
vaiśvarūpyeṇa vartantam aṅganās tā janārdanam
dakṣā dākṣiṇyayuktaṃ taṃ smitapūrvābhibhāṣiṇam
kṛṣṇaṃ bhāryāś cakamire bhaktyā ca bahu menire
pṛthag goṣṭhyaḥ kumārāṇāṃ prakāśaṃ strīgaṇaiḥ saha
alaṃcakrur jalaṃ vīrāḥ sāgarasya guṇākarāḥ
gītanṛtyavidhijñānāṃ tāsāṃ strīṇāṃ janeśvara
tejasāpy āhṛtānāṃ te dākṣaṇyāt tasthire vaśe
śṛṇvantaś cārugītāni tathā svabhinayāny api
tūryāṇy uttamanārīṇāṃ mumudur yadupuṃgavāḥ
pañcacūḍās tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ kauberyaś ca varāpsarāḥ
māhendrīś cānayām āsa vaiśvarūpyeṇa hetunā
tāḥ provācāprameyātmā sāntvayitvā jagat prabhuḥ
upasthitāś ca praṇatāḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭās tathā
krīḍāyuvatyo bhaimānāṃ praviśadhvam aśaṅkitāḥ
matpriyārthaṃ varārohā ramayadhvaṃ ca yādavān
darśayadhvaṃ guṇān sarvān nṛtyagītai rahaḥsu ca
tathābhinayayogeṣu vādyeṣu vividheṣu ca
evaṃ kṛte vidhāsyāmi śreyo vo manasepsitam
maccharīrasamā hy ete sarve niravaśeṣataḥ
śirasājñāṃ tu tāḥ sarvāḥ pratigṛhya hares tadā
krīḍāyuvatyo viviśur bhaimānām apsarovarāḥ
tābhiḥ praviṣṭamātrābhir dyotitaḥ sa mahārṇavaḥ
saudāminībhir nabhasi ghanavṛnda ivānagha
tā jale sthalavat sthitvā jaguś cāthāpy avādayan
cakruś cābhinayaṃ samyak svargāvāsa ivāṅganāḥ
gandhair mālyaiś ca tā divyair vastraiś cāyatalocanāḥ
helābhir hāsabhāvaiś ca jahrur bhaimamanāṃsy atha
kaṭākṣair iṅgitair hāsaiḥ kalaroṣaiḥ prasāditaiḥ
manonukūlair bhaimānāṃ samājahrur manāṃsi tāḥ
utkṣipyotkṣipya cākāśaṃ vātaskandhān bahūṃś ca tān
madirāvaśagā bhaimā mānayanti varāpsarāḥ
kṛṣṇo 'pi teṣāṃ prītyarthaṃ vijahre viyati prabhuḥ
sarvaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ sārdhaṃ strīsahasrair mudānvitaḥ
prabhāvajñās tu te vīrāḥ kṛṣṇasyāmitatejasaḥ
na jagmur vismayaṃ bhaimā gāmbhīryaṃ paramāsthitāḥ
kecid raivatakaṃ gatvā punar āyānti bhārata
gṛhān anye vanāny anye kāṅkṣitāny arimardana
apeyaḥ peyasalilaḥ sāgaraś cābhavat tadā
ājñayā lokanāthasya viṣṇor atulatejasaḥ
adhāvan sthalavac cāpi jale jalajalocanāḥ
gṛhya haste tathā nāryo yuktā majjaṃs tathāpi ca
bhakṣyabhojyāni peyāni coṣyaṃ lehyaṃ tathaica ca
bahuprakāraṃ manasā dhyāte teṣāṃ bhavaty uta
amlānamālyadhāriṇyas tāḥ striyas tān aninditān
rahaḥsu ramayāṃ cakruḥ svarge devaratānugāḥ
naubhir gṛhaprakārābhiś cikrīḍur aparājitāḥ
snātānuliptamuditāḥ sāyāhne 'ndhakavṛṣṇayaḥ
āyatāś caturasrāś ca vṛttāś ca svastikās tathā
prāsādā nauṣu kauravya vihitā viśvakarmaṇā
kailāsamandaracchandā merucchandās tathaiva ca
tathā nānāvayaśchandās tathehāmṛgarūpiṇaḥ
vaidūryatoraṇaiś citrāś citrābhir maṇibhaktibhiḥ
masāragalvarkamayaiś citrabhaktiśatair api
prakrīḍagaruḍacchandāś citrā kanakarītibhiḥ
krauñcacchandāḥ śukacchandā gajacchandās tathāpare
karṇadhārair gṛhītās tā nāvaḥ kārtasvarojjvalāḥ
salilaṃ śobhayām āsuḥ sāgarasya mahormimat
samucchritaiḥ sitaiḥ potair yānapātrais tathaiva ca
naubhiś ca jhillikābhiś ca śuśubhe varuṇālayaḥ
purāṇy ākāśagāmīni gandharvāṇām itas tataḥ
babhramuḥ sāgarajale bhaimayānāni bhārata
nandanacchandayukteṣu yānapātreṣu bhārata
nandanapratimaṃ sarvaṃ vihitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
udyānāni sabhā vṛkṣā dīrghikāḥ syandanāni ca
niveśitāni svalpāni tādṛśāny eva sarvathā
svargacchandeṣu cānyeṣu samāsāt svargasaṃnibhāḥ
nārāyaṇājñayā vīra vihitā viśvakarmaṇā
vaneṣu ruruvur hṛdyaṃ madhuraṃ caiva pakṣiṇaḥ
manoharataraṃ caiva bhaimānām atitejasām
devalokodbhavāḥ śvetā vilepuḥ kokilās tadā
madhurāṇi vicitrāṇi yadūnāṃ kāṅkṣitāni ca
candrāṃśusamarūpeṣu harmyapṛṣṭheṣu barhiṇaḥ
nanṛtur madhurārāvāḥ śikhaṇḍigaṇasaṃvṛtāḥ
patākā yānapātrāṇāṃ sarvāḥ pakṣigaṇāyutāḥ
bhramarair upagītāś ca sragdāmāsaktavāsibhiḥ
nārāyaṇājñayā vṛkṣāḥ puṣpāṇi mumucur bhṛśam
ṛtavaś cānurūpāṇi vihāyasigatās tadā
vavau manoharo vāto ratikhedaharaḥ sukhaḥ
rajobhiḥ sarvapuṣpāṇāṃ yuktaś candanaśaityabhṛt
śītoṣṇam icchatāṃ tatra babhūva vasudhāpate
vāsudevaprasādena bhaimānāṃ krīḍatāṃ tadā
na kṣutpipāsā na glānir na cintā śoka eva ca
āviveśa tadā bhaimān prabhāvāc cakrapāninaḥ
apraśāntamahātūryā gītanṛtyopaśobhitāḥ
babhūvuḥ sāgarakrīḍā bhaimānām atitejasām
bahuyojanavistīrṇaṃ samudraṃ salilāśayam
rūdhvā cikrīḍur indrābhā bhaimāḥ kṛṣṇābhirakṣitāḥ
paricchadasyānurūpaṃ yānapātraṃ mahātmanaḥ
nārāyaṇasya devasya vihitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
ratnāni yāni trailaukye viśiṣṭāni viśāṃ pate
kṛṣṇasya tāni sarvāṇi yānapātre 'titejasaḥ
pṛthak pṛthaṅ nivāsāś ca strīṇāṃ kṛṣṇasya bhārata
maṇivaidūryacitrāntāḥ kārtasvaravibhūṣitāḥ
sarvartukusumākīrṇāḥ sarvagandhādhivāsitāḥ
yadusiṃhāḥ śubhair juṣṭāḥ śakunaiḥ svargavāsibhiḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
reme balaś candanapaṅkadigdhaḥ
kādambarīpānakalaḥ pṛthuśrīḥ
raktekṣaṇo revatim āśrayitvā
pralambabāhuḥ skhalitaprayātaḥ
nīlāmbudābhe vasane vasānaś
candrāṃśugauro madirāvilākṣaḥ
rarāja rāmo 'mbudamadhyam etya
saṃpūrṇabimbo bhagavān ivenduḥ
vāmaikakarṇāmalakuṇḍalaśrīḥ
smeraṃ manojñābjakṛtāvataṃsaḥ
tiryakkaṭākṣaṃ priyayā mumoda
rāmo mukhaṃ cārvabhivīkṣamāṇaḥ
athājñayā kaṃsanikumbhaśatror
udārarūpo 'psarasāṃ gaṇaḥ saḥ
draṣṭuḥ mudā revatim ājagāma
balālayaṃ svargasamānam ṛddhyā
tāṃ revatīṃ cāpy atha vāpi rāmaṃ
sarvā namaskṛtya varāṅgayaṣṭyaḥ
vādyānurūpaṃ nanṛtuḥ sugātryaḥ
samantato 'nyā jagire ca samyak
cakrus tathaivābhinayena labdhaṃ
yathāvad eṣāṃ priyam arthayuktam
hṛdyānukūlaṃ ca valasya tasya
tathājñayā raivatarājaputryāḥ
cikrīḍur anyāś ca tathaiva tāsāṃ
taddeśabhāṣākṛtiveṣayuktaḥ
sahastatālaṃ lalitaṃ salīlaṃ
varāṅganāḥ sarvaratānatāṅgyaḥ
saṃkarṣaṇādhokṣajanandanāni
saṃkīrtayantyo 'tha ca maṅgalāni
kaṃsapralambādivadhaṃ ca ramyaṃ
cāṇūraghātaṃ ca tathaiva raṅge
yaśodayā ca prathitaṃ yaśo 'tha
dāmodaratvaṃ ca janārdanasya
vadhaṃ tathāriṣṭakadhenukābhyāṃ
vraje ca vāsaṃ śakunīvadhaṃ ca
tathā ca bhagnau yamalārjunau ca
sṛṣṭiṃ vṛkāṇām api kālamuktām
sa kāliyo nāgapatir hrade ca
kṛṣṇena dāntaś ca yathā durātmā
śaṅkhahradād uddharaṇaṃ ca vīra
padmotpalānāṃ madhusūdanena
govardhano 'rthe ca gavāṃ dhṛto 'bhūd
yathā ca kṛṣṇena janārdanena
kubjāṃ yathā gandhakapeṣikāṃ ca
kubjatvahīnāṃ kṛtavāṃś ca krṣṇaḥ
avāmanaṃ vāmanakaṃ ca cakre
kṛṣṇo yathātmānam ajo 'py anindyaḥ
saubhapramāthaṃ ca halāyudhatvaṃ
vadhaṃ murasyāpy atha devaśatroḥ
gandhārakanyāvahane nṛpāṇāṃ
rathe tathāyojanam ūrjitānām
tataḥ subhadrāharaṇe jayaṃ ca
yuddhe ca bālāhakajambumāle
ratnapravekaṃ ca yudhā jitair yat
samāhṛtaṃ śakrasamakṣam āsīt
etāni cānyāni ca cārurūpā
jaguḥ striyaḥ prītikarāṇi rājan
saṃkarṣaṇādhokṣajaharṣaṇāni
citrāṇi cānekakathāśrayāṇi
kādambarīpānamadotkaṭas tu
balaḥ pṛthuśrīḥ sa cukūrda rāmaḥ
sahastatālaṃ madhuraṃ samaṃ ca
sa bhāryayā revatarājaputryā
taṃ kūrdamānaṃ madhusūdanaś ca
dṛṣṭvā mahātmā harṣānvitātmā
cukūrda satyāsahito mahātmā
balasya bhīmān harṣāgamārtham
samudrayātrārtham athāgataś ca
cukūrda pārtho naralokavīraḥ
kṛṣṇena sārdhaṃ muditaś cukūrda
subhadrayā caiva varāṅgayaṣṭyā
gadaś ca dhīmān atha sāraṇaś ca
pradyumnasāmbau nṛpa satyakaś ca
sātrājitīsūnur udāravīryaḥ
sa cārūdeṣṇaś ca sucārūrūpaḥ
vīrau kumārau niśaṭholmukau ca
rāmātmajau vīratamau cukūrdatuḥ
akrūrasenāpatiśaṃkaraś ca
tathāpare bhaimakulapradhānāḥ
tad yānapātraṃ vavṛdhe tadānīṃ
kṛṣṇaprabhāvena janendraputra
āpūrṇam āpūrṇam udārakīrteś
cukūrdayadbhir nṛpa bhaimamukhyaiḥ
tai rāsasaktair atikūrdamānair
yadupravīrair amaraprakāśaiḥ
harṣānvitaṃ vīra jagat tadābhūc
chemuś ca pāpāni janendrasūno
devātithis tatra ca nārado 'tha
vipraḥ priyārthaṃ madhukeśiśatroḥ
cukūrda madhye yadusattamānāṃ
jaṭākalāpāgalitaikadeśaḥ
rāsapraṇetā dhuri rājaputra
sa eva tatrābhavad aprameyaḥ
madhyaṃ ca gatvā sa cukūrda bhūyo
helāvikāraiḥ saviḍ ambitāṅgaiḥ
sa satyabhāmām atha keśavaṃ ca
pārthaṃ subhadrāṃ ca balaṃ ca devam
devīṃ tathā raivatarājaputrīṃ
saṃdṛśya saṃdṛśya jahāsa dhīmān
tā hāsayām āsa sudhairyayuktās
tais tair ūpāyaiḥ parihāsaśīlaḥ
ceṣṭānukārair hasitānukārair
līlānukārair aparaiś ca dhīmān
ābhāṣitaṃ kiṃcid ivopalakṣya
nādātinādān bhagavān mumoca
hasan vihāsāṃś ca jahāsa harṣād
dhāsyāgame kṛṣṇavinodanārtham
kṛṣṇājñayā sātiśayāni tatra
yathānurūpāṇi dadur yuvatyaḥ
ratnāni vastrāṇi ca rūpavanti
jagat pradhānāni nṛdevasūno
mālyāni ca svargasamudbhavāni
saṃtānadāmāny atimuktakāni
sarvartukāny apy anayaṃs tadānīṃ
dadur harer iṅgitakālatajjñāḥ
rāsāvasāne tv atha gṛhya haste
mahāmuniṃ nāradam aprameyaḥ
papāta kṛṣṇo bhagavān samudre
sātrājitīṃ cārjunam eva cātha
uvāca cāmeyaparākramo 'tha
śaineyam īṣatprahasan pṛthuśrīḥ
dvidhākṛtāḥ sma patitāḥ sma bhūtvā
krīḍā jale no 'stu sahāṅganābhiḥ
sarevatīko 'stu balo 'rdhanetā
putrā madīyāś ca sahārdhabhaimāḥ
bhaimārdham evātha balātmajāś ca
matpakṣiṇaḥ santu samudratoye
ājñāpayām āsa tataḥ samudraṃ
kṛṣṇaḥ sthitaṃ prāñjalinaṃ pratītaḥ
sugandhatoyo bhava mṛṣṭatoyas
tathā bhava grāhavivarjitaś ca
dṛśyā ca te ratnavibhūṣitā tu
sā velikābhūr atha patsukhā ca
manonukūlaṃ ca janasya yat tat
prayaccha vijñāsyasi matprabhāvāt
bhavasva peyo 'py atha ceṣṭapeyo
janasya sarvasya manonukūlaḥ
vaidūryamuktāmaṇihemacitrā
bhavantu matsyās tvayi saumyarūpāḥ
vidhatsva ca tvaṃ kamalotpalāni
sugandhasusparśarasakṣamāṇi
ṣaṭpādajuṣṭāni manoharāṇi
cārūṇi kīlālasamanvitāni
maireyamādhvīkasurāsavānāṃ
kumbhāṃś ca pūrṇānsthapayasva toye
jāmbūnadaṃ pānanimittameṣāṃ
pātraṃ papur yeṣu dadasva bhaimāḥ
puṣpoccayair vāsitaśītatoyo
bhavāpramattaḥ khalu toyarāśe
yathā vyalīkaṃ na bhaved yadūnāṃ
sastrījanānāṃ kuru tat prayatnam
itīdam uktvā bhagavān samudraṃ
tataḥ pracikrīḍa sahārjunena
siṣeca pūrvaṃ nṛpa nāradaṃ tu
sātrājitī kṛṣṇamukheṅgitajñā
tato madāvarjitacārudehaḥ
papāta rāmaḥ salile salīlam
sākāram ālambya karaṃ kareṇa
manoharāṃ raivatarājaputrīm
kṛṣṇātmajā ye tv atha bhaimamukhyā
rāmasya patnyaḥ patitāḥ samudre
virāgavastrābharaṇāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ
kṛīḍābhirāmā madirāvilākṣāḥ
śeṣās tu bhaimā harim abhyupetāḥ
krīḍābhirāmā niśaṭholmukādyāḥ
vicitravastrābharaṇāś ca mattāḥ
saṃtānamālyāvṛtakaṇṭhadeśāḥ
vīryopapannāḥ kṛtacārucihnā
viliptagātrā jalayantrahastāḥ
jītāni taddeśamanoharāṇi
kharopapannāny atha gāyamānāḥ
tataḥ pracakrur jalavāditāni
nānāsvarāṇi priyavādyaghoṣāḥ
sahāpsarobhis tridivālayābhiḥ
kṛṣṇājñayā veśavadhūśatāni
ākāśagaṅgājalavādyatajjñaḥ
sadāyuvatyo madanaikacittāḥ
avādayaṃs tā jaladardurāṃś ca
vādyānurūpaṃ jagire ca hṛṣṭāḥ
kuśeśayākośaviśālanetrāḥ
kuśeśayāpīḍavibhūṣitāś ca
kuśeśayānāṃ ravibodhitānāṃ
jahruḥ śriyaṃ tāḥ suravāramukhyāḥ
strīvaktracandraiḥ sakalendukalpai
rarāja rājañ śataśaḥ samudraḥ
yadṛcchayā devavidhānato vā
nabho yathā candrasahasrakīrṇam
samudrameghaḥ sa rarāja rajañ
śatahradās trīprabhayābhirāmaḥ
saudāminībhinna ivāmbunātho
dedīpyamāno nabhasīva meghaḥ
nārāyaṇaś caiva sa nāradaś ca
siṣeca pakṣe kṛtacārucihnaḥ
balaṃ sapakṣaṃ kṛtacārucihnaṃ
sa caiva pakṣaṃ madhusūdanasya
hastapramuktair jalayantrakaiś ca
prahṛṣṭarūpāḥ siṣicus tadānīm
rāgoddhatā vāruṇimaṇḍamattāḥ
saṃkarṣaṇādhokṣajadevapatnyaḥ
āraktanetrā jalamuktisiktāḥ
strīṇāṃ samakṣaṃ puruṣāyamāṇāḥ
te noparemuḥ suciraṃ ca bhaimā
mānaṃ vahanto madanaṃ madaṃ ca
atiprasaṅgaṃ tu vicintya kṛṣṇas
tān vārayām āsa rathāṅgapāṇiḥ
svayaṃ nivṛtto jalavādyaśabdaiḥ
sanāradaḥ pārthasahāyavāṃś ca
kṛṣṇeṅgitajñā jalayuddhasaṅgād
bhaimā nivṛttā dṛḍhamānino 'pi
nityaṃ tathānandakarāḥ priyāṇāṃ
priyāś ca teṣāṃ nanṛtuḥ pratītāḥ
nṛtyāvasāne bhagavān upendras
tatyāja dhīmān atha toyasaṅgān
uttīrya toyād anukūlalepaṃ
jagrāha dattvā munisattamāya
upendram uttīrṇam athāśu dṛṣṭvā
bhaimā hi te tatyajur eva toyam
viliptagātrās tv atha pānabhūmiṃ
kṛṣṇājñayā te yayur aprameyāḥ
yathānupūrvyā ca yathāvayaś ca
yatsaṃniyaugaiś ca tadopaviṣṭāḥ
annāni vīrā bubhujuḥ pratītāḥ
papuś ca peyāni yathānukūlam
māṃsāni pakvāni phalāmlakāni
cukrottareṇātha ca dāḍimena
niṣṭaptaśūlān sakalān paśūṃś ca
tatropajahruḥ śucayo 'tha sūdāḥ
susvinnaśūlyān mahiṣāṃś ca bālān
sthūlān suniṣṭaptaghṛtāvasiktān
vṛkṣāmlasauvarcalacukrapūrṇān
paurogavoktān upajahrur eṣām
paurogavoktyā vidhinā mṛgāṇāṃ
māṃsāni siddhāni ca pīvarāṇi
nānāprakārāṇy upajahrur eṣāṃ
mṛṣṭāni pakvāni ca cukracūtaiḥ
pārśvāni cānye śakalāni tatra
daduḥ paśūnāṃ ghṛtamṛkṣitāni
sāmudracūrṇair avacūrṇitāni
cūrṇena mṛṣṭena samāricena
samūlakair dāḍimamātuluṅgaiḥ
parṇāsahiṅgvārdrakabhūstṛṇaiś ca
tadopadaṃśaiḥ sumukhottarais te
pānāni hṛṣṭāḥ papur aprameyāḥ
kaṭvaṅgaśūlair api pakṣibhiś ca
ghṛtāmlasauvarcalatailasiktaiḥ
maireyamādhvīkasurāvāṃs te
papuḥ priyābhiḥ parivāryamāṇāḥ
śvetena yuktān api śoṇitena
bhakṣyān sugandhāṃl lavaṇānvitāṃś ca
ārdrān kilāṭān ghṛtapūrṇakāṃś ca
nānāprakārān api khaṇḍakhādyān
apānapāścoddhavabhojamiśrāḥ
śākaiś ca sūpaiś ca bahuprakāraiḥ
peyaiś ca dadhnā payasā ca vīrāḥ
svinnāni rājan bubhujuḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ
tathā rasālāṃś ca bahuprakārān
papuḥ sugandhān api pālavīṣu
śṛtaṃ payaḥ śarkarayā ca yuktaṃ
phalaprakārāṃś ca bahūṃś ca khādan
tṛptāḥ pravṛttāḥ punar eva vīrās
te bhaimamukhyā vanitāsahāyāḥ
gītāni ramyāṇi jaguḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ
kāntābhinītāni manoharāṇi
ājñāpayām āsa tataḥ sa tasyāṃ
niśi prahṛṣṭo bhagavān upendraḥ
chālikyageyaṃ bahusaṃvidhānaṃ
yad devagāndharvam udāharanti
jagrāha vīṇām atha nāradas tu
ṣaḍgrāmarāgādisamādhiyuktām
hallīsakaṃ tu svayam eva kṛṣṇaḥ
suvaṃśaghoṣaṃ naradeva pārthaḥ
mṛdaṅgavādyān aparāṃś ca vādyān
varāpsarās tā jagṛhuḥ pratītāḥ
āsāritān te ca tataḥ pratītā
rambhotthitā sābhinayārthatajjñā
tayābhinīte varagātrayaṣṭyā
tutoṣa rāmaś ca janārdanaś ca
athorvaśī cāruviśālanetrā
hemā ca rājann atha miśrakeśī
tilottamā cāpy atha menakā ca
etās tathānyāś ca haripriyārtham
jagus tathaivābhinayaṃ ca cakrur
iṣṭaiś ca kāmair manaso 'nukūlaiḥ
tā vāsudeve 'py anuraktacittāḥ
svagītanṛtyābhinayair udāraiḥ
narendrasūno paritoṣitena
tāmbūlayogāś ca varāpsarobhiḥ
tadāgatābhir nṛvarāhṛtās tu
kṛṣṇepsayā mānamayās tathaiva
phalāni gandhottamavanti vīrāś
chālikyagāndharvam athāhṛtaṃ ca
kṛṣṇecchayā ca tridivān nṛdeva
anugrahārtha bhuvi mānuṣāṇām
sthitaṃ ca ramyaṃ haritejasaiva
prayojayām āsa sa raukmiṇeyaḥ
chālikyagāndharvam udārabuddhis
tenaiva tāmbūlam atha prayuktam
prayojitaṃ pañcabhiri ndratulyaiś
chālikyam iṣṭaṃ satataṃ narāṇām
śubhāvahaṃ vṛddhikaraṃ praśastaṃ
maṅgalyam evātha tathā yaśasyam
puṇyaṃ ca puṣṭyabhyudayāvahaṃ ca
nārāyaṇasyeṣṭam udārakīrteḥ
jayāvahaṃ dharmadhurāvahaṃ ca
duḥsvapnanāśaṃ parikīrtyamānam
karoti pāpaṃ ca tathā vihanti
śṛṇvan surāvāsagato narendra
chālikyagāndharvam udārakīrtim
mene kilaikaṃ divasaṃ sahasram
caturyugānāṃ nṛpa raivato 'tha
tataḥ pravṛttā ca kumārajātiḥ
gāndharvajātiś ca tathāparāpi
dīpād yathā dīpaśatāni rājan
viveda kṛṣṇaś ca sa nāradaś ca
pradyumnamukhyair nṛpa bhaimamukhyaiḥ
vijñātam etad dhi parair yathāvad
uddeśamātrāṇi janās tu loke
jānanti chālikyaguṇodayānāṃ
toyaṃ nadīnām atha vā samudraḥ
jñātuṃ hi śakyaṃ hi mahāgirir vā
phalāgrato vā guṇato 'tha vāpi
śakyaṃ na chālikyam ṛte tapobhis
tālair vidhānāny atha mūrchanāsu
ṣaḍgrāmarāgeṣu ca tatra kāryaṃ
tasyaikadeśāvayavena rājan
leśābhidhānaṃ sukumārajātiṃ
niṣṭāṃ suduḥkhena narāḥ prayānti
chālikyagāndharvaguṇodayeṣu
ye devagandharvamaharṣisattvāḥ
niṣṭāṃ prāyāntīty avagaccha buddhyā
chālikyam evaṃ madhusūdanena
bhaimottamānāṃ naradeva dattam
lokasya cānugrahakāmyayeha
gataṃ pratiṣṭām amaropageyam
bālā yavānaś ca tathaiva vṛddhāḥ
krīḍanti bhaimāḥ pravarotsaveṣu
pūrvaṃ tu bālāḥ samudāharanti
vṛddhās tu paścāt pratimānayanti
sthāneṣu nityaṃ pratimānayanti
martyeṣu martyān yadavo 'tivīrāḥ
svavaṃśadharmaṃ samanusmarantaḥ
purātanaṃ dharmavidhānatajjñāḥ
prītipramāṇaṃ ha vayaḥpramāṇam
prītipramāṇāni ha sauhṛdāni
prītiṃ puraskṛtya hi te daśārhāḥ
vṛṇyandhakāḥ putrasakhā babhūvur
visarjitāḥ keśivināśanena
svargaṃ gatāś cāpsarasāṃ samūhāḥ
kṛtvā praṇāmaṃ madhukaṃsaśatroḥ
prahṛṣṭarūpasya suhṛṣṭarūpāḥ
vinoditāḥ keśiniṣūdanena
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
teṣāṃ krīḍāprasaktānāṃ yadūnāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām
chidram āsādya durbuddhir devaśatrur durāsadaḥ
kanyāṃ bhānumatīṃ nāma bhānor duhitaraṃ nṛpa
jahārātmavadhākāṅkṣī nikumbho nāma dānavaḥ
antarhito mohayitvā yadūnāṃ pramadājanam
māyāvī māyayā rājan pūrvavairam anusmaran
bhrātur hi vajranābhasya tasya kanyā prabhāvatī
pradyūmnena hṛtā vīra vajranābhas tathā hataḥ
bhānor eva tathāraṇye vasaty avasareṇa hi
asvādhīne durādharṣe chidrajño dānavādhamaḥ
kanyāpure mahānādaḥ sahasā samupasthitaḥ
tasyāṃ hṛtāyāṃ kanyāyāṃ rudantyāṃ samitiṃjaya
vasudevāhukau vīrau daṃśitau nirgatāv ubhau
ārtanādam upaśrutya bhānoḥ kanyāpure tadā
na dṛṣṭigocare tau tu dadṛśate 'pakāriṇam
tathaiva daṃśitau yātau yatra kṛṣṇo mahābalaḥ
śrutārthaḥ svaṃ vimānaṃ tad āruroha janārdanaḥ
pārthena sahitas tārkṣyaṃ nāgaśatrum ariṃdamaḥ
rathe tvam anugaccheti saṃdiśya makaradhvajam
tvareti garuḍaṃ vīraḥ saṃdideśa ca kāśyapam
vajraṃ nagaram āyāntaṃ nikumbhaṃ raṇadurjayam
pārthakṛṣṇau mahātmānāv āsedatur ariṃdamau
pradyumnaś ca mahātejā māyināṃ pravaro nṛpa
nikumbhas tv atha taṃ dṛṣṭvā tridhātmānam athākarot
tān sarvān yodhayām āsa nikumbhaḥ prahasann iva
bahukaṇṭakagurvībhir gadābhir amaropamaḥ
savyenālambya hastena kanyāṃ bhānumatīṃ nṛpa
dakṣiṇenātha hastena gadayā praharaty uta
kanyārthaṃ na ca kṛṇṣau vā kāmo vā nṛpasattama
nirdayaṃ praharanti sma nikumbhe ca mahāsure
samarthās te mahātmānaḥ śatruṃ hantuṃ durāsadāḥ
niśaśvasur narapate dayābhārāvapīḍitāḥ
śreṣṭho dhanuṣmatāṃ pārthaḥ sarvathā kuśalo yudhi
nārācair vidhinā daityaṃ śaraśaktyā jaghāna ha
te tu vaitastikair bāṇair vividhur dānavaṃ yudhi
na kanyāṃ kalayā yuktyā śikṣayā ca mahīpate
tataḥ sa kanyayā sārdhaṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata
āsurīm āśrito māyāṃ na tāṃ vetti hi kaś cana
taṃ kṛṣṇau raukmiṇeyaś ca pṛṣṭhato 'nuyayus tadā
hārītaḥ śakuno bhūtvā tasthāv atha mahāsuraḥ
taṃ bāṇaiḥ punar evātha vīro bhūyo dhanaṃjayaḥ
vaitastikair marmabhidbhiḥ kanyāṃ rakṣann atāḍayat
sa imāṃ pṛthivīṃ kṛtsnāṃ saptadvīpāṃ mahāsuraḥ
babhrāmānugataś caiva tair vīrair arimardanaḥ
gokarṇasyopariṣṭāt tu parvatasya mahāsuraḥ
papāta celagaṅgāyāḥ puline saha kanyayā
na devā nāsurā vāpi laṅghayanti tapodhanāḥ
gokarṇaṃ tejasā guptaṃ mahādevasya bhārata
etad antaram āsādya pradyumnaḥ śīghravikramaḥ
kanyāṃ bhānumatīṃ bhaimo jagrāha raṇadurjayaḥ
asuraḥ so 'rdito rājan kṛṣṇābhyāṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
tyaktvāthottaragokarṇāṃ nikumbho dakṣiṇāṃ diśam
jagāma pṛṣṭhato yātau kṛṣṇau tārkṣyagatau tadā
viveśa ṣaṭpuraṃ caiva jñātīnām ālayaṃ tadā
tatra vīrau guhādvāri kṛṣṇau rātriṃ tadoṣatuḥ
raukmiṇeyo 'pi kṛṣṇena saṃdiṣṭo dvārakāṃ purīm
anayad bhānutanayāṃ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
nayitvā cāyayau vīraḥ ṣaṭpuraṃ dānavākulam
dadarśa ca guhādvāri kṛṣṇau bhīmaparākramau
ūṣatur dvāram ākramya ṣaṭpurasya mahābalau
kṛṣṇau pradyumnasahitau nikumbhavadhakāṅkṣiṇau
tato 'nantaram etasmād bilād atibalas tadā
nirjagāma balī yoddhuṃ nikumbho bhīmavikramaḥ
tasya nirgacchatas tasmād bilāt pārtho viśāṃ pate
rurodha sarvato mārgaṃ śarair gāṇḍīvaniḥsṛtaiḥ
so 'bhisṛtya gadāṃ ghorām udyamya bahukaṇṭakām
śirasy atāḍayat pārthaṃ nikumbho balināṃ varaḥ
gadayābhihate pārthe raktaṃ vamati muhyati
hasitvā so 'suro dṛpto raukmiṇeyam atāḍayat
taṃ prāṅmukhamukhaṃ vīraṃ māyāvī māyināṃ varam
adṛṣṭenāhato vīraḥ śirasy atha mumoha saḥ
tathāgatau tu dṛṣṭvā tau muhyamānau sutāḍitau
abhidudrāva govindo nikumbhaṃ krodhamūrchitaḥ
kaumodakīṃ samudyamya gadapūrvodbhavo gadām
tāv anyonyaṃ durādharṣau garjantāv abhipetatuḥ
airāvatagataḥ śakraḥ sarvair devagaṇaiḥ saha
dadarśa tan mahāyuddhaṃ ghoraṃ devāsuraṃ tadā
dṛṣṭvā devān hṛṣīkeśaś citrair yuddhair ariṃdamaḥ
iyeṣa dānavaṃ hantuṃ devānāṃ hitakāmyayā
sa maṇḍalāni citrāṇi darśayām āsa keśavaḥ
kaumodakīṃ mahābāhur lālayan yuddhakovidaḥ
tathaivāsuramukhyo 'pi gadāṃ tāṃ bahukaṇṭakām
śikṣayā bhrāmayāṇo 'tha maṇḍalāni cacāra ha
ṛṣabhāv iva garjantau bṛṃhantāv iva kuñjarau
vāsitāntaram āsādya kruddhau sālāvṛkāv iva
ājaghāna nikumbhas tu gadayā gadapūrvajam
spaṣṭāṣṭaghaṇṭayā vīra nādaṃ muktvātidāruṇam
tatkālam eva kṛṣṇo 'pi bhrāmayitvā mahāgadām
nikumbhamūrdhani tadā pātayām āsa bhārata
avaṣṭabhya muhūrtaṃ tu hariḥ kaumodakīṃ gadām
tasthau jagadgurur dhīmān mumoha patitaḥ kṣitau
hāhābhūtaṃ jagat sarvaṃ tatkālam abhavat tadā
tathā gate vāsudeve naradeve mahātmani
ākāśagaṅgātoyena śītena ca sugandhinā
siṣecāmṛtamiśreṇa kṛṣṇaṃ deveśvaraḥ svayam
nūnam ātmecchayā kṛṣṇas tathā cakre surottamaḥ
ko hi śakto mahātmānaṃ yuddhe mohayituṃ harim
kṛṣṇaḥ pratyāgataprāṇaś cakram udyamya bhārata
pratīccheti durātmānam uvāca ripunāśanaḥ
nikumbho 'py atimāyāvī utpapāta durāsadaḥ
śarīraṃ tat parityajya na tu taṃ vetti keśavaḥ
mumūrṣati mṛto vāyam iti matvā janārdanaḥ
rarakṣa smaramāṇo 'tha vīro vīravrataṃ vibho
atha pradyumnakaunteyāv āgatau labdhacetanau
sthitau nārāyaṇābhyāśe nikumbhavadhaniścitau
pradyumno 'py atha māyāvī viditaḥ kṛṣṇam abravīt
nikumbhas tāta nāsty atra gataḥ kvāpi sudurmatiḥ
pradyumnenaiva mukte tu tan nanāśa kalevaram
prajahāsātha bhagavān arjunena saha prabhuḥ
tathāyutasahasrāṇi nikumbhānāṃ janādhipa
dadṛśus te tadā vīrāḥ kṣitau divi ca sarvataḥ
sahasrāṇy eva kṛṣṇaṃ tu tathā pārtham ariṃdamam
raukmiṇeyaṃ tathā vīraṃ tad adbhutam ivābhavat
pāṇḍavasya dhanuḥ kecit kecid asya mahāśarān
anye 'sya jagṛhur hastāv anye pādau mahāsurāḥ
evaṃ grahāya te vīram agamaṃs te vihāyasi
pārthānām api koṭyas tu gṛhītānāṃ tadābhavan
nāntaṃ dadarśa kṛṣṇaś ca kārṣṇiś ca ripunāśanau
vicchidya tau śarair vīrau nikumbhaṃ pārthavarjitau
ekaikas tu dvidhā chinno dvaidhībhavati bhārata
divyajñānas tadā kṛṣṇo bhagavān atra dṛṣṭvān
nikumbhaṃ tattvataś cāpi dadarśa madhusūdanaḥ
sraṣṭāraṃ sarvamāyānāṃ hartāraṃ phalgunasya ca
sa cakreṇa śiras tasya cakartāsurasūdanaḥ
paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ bhūtabhavyabhavo hariḥ
sa muktvā phalgunaṃ rājaṃś chinne śirasi bhārata
papātāsuramukhyo 'tha chinnamūla iva drumaḥ
athākāśagataṃ pārthaṃ patamānaṃ vihāyasaḥ
kṛṣṇavākyena jagraha kārṣṇir viyati mānada
nikumbhe patite bhūmau samāśvāsya dhanaṃjayam
jagāma dvārakāṃ devaḥ pārthakāmasamanvitaḥ
samiyāyātha dāśarho dvārakāṃ mudito vibhuḥ
nāradaṃ ca mahātmānaṃ vavande yadunandanaḥ
nārado 'tha mahātejā bhānuṃ yādavam abravīt
bhāno mā kārṣīr manyuṃ tvaṃ śrūyatāṃ bhaimanandana
krīḍantyā raivatodyāne durvāsāḥ kopito 'nayā
sa śaśāpa tato roṣān munir duhitaraṃ tava
atidurlalitaiḥ kanyā śatruhastaṃ gamiṣyati
sutārthe te mayā sārdhaṃ munibhiḥ sa prasāditaḥ
bālāṃ vratavatīṃ kanyām anāgasam imāṃ mune
śaptavān asi dharmajña kathaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
anantaraṃ vidhatsvātra vayaṃ vijñāpayāmahe
asmābhir evam uktas tu durvāsā bhaimanandana
uvācādhomukho bhūtvā muhūrtaṃ kṛpayānvitaḥ
yad avocam ahaṃ vākyaṃ tat tathā na tad anyathā
ripuhastam avaśyaṃ hi gamiṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
adūṣitā tu dharmeṇa bhartāram upalapsyati
bahuputrā bahudhanā subhagā ca bhaviṣyati
sugandhagandhā ca sadā kumārī ca punaḥ punaḥ
na ca śokām imaṃ ghoraṃ tan vaṅgī dhārayiṣyati
evaṃ bhānumatī vīra sahadevāya dīyatām
śraddadhānaḥ sa śūraś ca dharmaśīlaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
tato bhānumatīṃ bhānur dadau mādrīsutāya vai
sahadevāya dharmātmā nāradasya vacaḥ smaran
ānītaḥ sahadevaś ca preṣite cakrapāṇinā
vivāhe ca tadā vṛtte sabhāryaḥ svapuraṃ gataḥ
imaṃ kṛṣṇasya vijayaṃ yaḥ paṭhec chṛṇuyād atha
vijayaṃ sarvakṛtyeṣu śraddadhāno labhen naraḥ
janamejaya uvāca
bhānumatyāpaharaṇaṃ vijayaṃ keśavasya ca
chālikyānayanaṃ caiva devalokān mahāmune
krīḍāṃ ca sāgare divyāṃ kṛṣṇīnām atitejasām
aśrauṣaṃ paramāścaryaṃ mune dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
vajranābhavadhaṃ hy uktaṃ nikumbhavadhakīrtane
tan me kautūhalaṃ śrotuṃ prasādād bhavato mune
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
hanta te kīrtayiṣyāmi vajranābhavadhaṃ nṛpa
vijayaṃ caiva kāmasya sāmbasya ca mahātmanaḥ
meroḥ sānau narapate tapaś cakre mahāsuraḥ
vajranābha iti khyāto niścitaḥ samitiṃjayaḥ
tasya tuṣṭo mahātejā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
vareṇa cchandayām āsa tapasā paritoṣitaḥ
avadhyatāṃ sa devebhyo vavre dānavasattamaḥ
puraṃ vajrapuraṃ caiva sarvaratnamayaṃ śubham
svacchandena praveśaś ca na vāyor api bhārata
acintitena kāmānām upapattir narādhipa
śākhānagaramukhyānāṃ saṃvāhānāṃ śatāni ca
nagarasyāprameyasya samantāj janamejaya
tathā tad abhavat tasya varadānena bhārata
uvāsa vajranagare vajranābho mahāsuraḥ
koṭiśo varalabdhaṃ tam asurāḥ parivārya te
ūṣur vajrapure rājan saṃvāheṣu tathaiva ca
śākhānagaramukhyeṣu ramyeṣu ca narādhipa
hṛṣṭapuṣṭapramuditā nṛpa devasya śatravaḥ
vajranābho 'tha duṣṭātmā varadānena darpitaḥ
purasya cātmanaś caiva jagad bādhitum udyataḥ
mahendram abravīd gatvā devalokaṃ viśāṃ pate
aham īśitum icchāmi trailokyaṃ pākaśāsana
atha vā me prayacchasva yuddhaṃ devagaṇeśvara
sāmānyaṃ hi jagat kṛtsnaṃ kāśyapānāṃ mahātmanām
sa bṛhaspatinā sārdhaṃ mantrayitvā sureśvaraḥ
vajranābhaṃ suraśreṣṭhaḥ provāca kuruvaṃśaja
satreṣu dīkṣitaḥ saumya kaśyapo naḥ pitā muniḥ
tasmin vṛtte yathā nyāyyaṃ tathā sa hi kariṣyati
tataḥ sa pitaraṃ gatvā kaśyapaṃ dānavo 'bravīt
yathoktaṃ devarājena tam uvācātha kaśyapaḥ
satre kṛtte kariṣyāmi yathā nyāyyaṃ bhaviṣyati
tvaṃ tu vajrapure putra vasa gaccha samāśritaḥ
evam ukte vajranābhaḥ svam eva nagaraṃ gataḥ
mahendro 'pi yayau devo dvārakāṃ dvāramālinīm
gatvā cāntarhito devo vāsudevam athābravīt
vajranābhasya vṛttāntaṃ tam uvāca janārdanaḥ
śaurer upasthito deva vājimedho mahākratuḥ
tasmin vṛtte vajranābhaṃ pātayiṣyāmi vāsava
tatropāyaṃ praveśe tu cintayāvaḥ satāṃ gate
nānicchayā praveśo 'sti tatra vāyor api prabho
tato gato devarājo vāsudevena satkṛtaḥ
vājimedhe ca saṃprāpte vasudevasya bhārata
tasmin yajñe vartamāne praveśārthaṃ surottamau
cintayām āsatur vīrau devarājācyutāv ubhau
tatra yajñe vartamāne sunāṭyena naṭas tadā
maharṣīṃs toṣayām āsa bhadranāmeti nāmataḥ
taṃ vareṇa muniśreṣṭhāś chandayām āsur ātmavān
sa vavre tu naṭo bhadro varaṃ deveśvaropamaḥ
devendrakṛṣṇacchandena sarasvatyā pracoditaḥ
prāṇipatya muniśreṣṭhān aśvamedhe samāgatān
bhojyo dvijānāṃ sarveṣāṃ bhaveyaṃ munisattamāḥ
saptadvīpāṃ ca pṛthivīṃ vicareyam imām aham
prasiddhākāśagamanaḥ satkurvaṃś ca viśeṣataḥ
avadhyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sthāvarā ye ca jaṅgamāḥ
yasya yasya va veṣeṇa praviśeyam ahaṃ khalu
mṛtasya jīvato vāpi bhāvenotpāditasya vā
sa bhūyas tādṛśaḥ syāṃ vai jarārogavivarjitaḥ
tuṣyeyur munayo nityam anye ca mama sarvadā
evam astv iti sa prokto brāhmaṇair nṛpate naṭaḥ
saptadvīpāṃ vasumatīṃ paryaṭaty amaropamaḥ
purāṇi dānavendrāṇām uttarāṃś ca kurūṃs tathā
bhadrāśvān ketumālāṃś ca kālāpadvīpam eva ca
parvaṇīsu tu sarvāsu dvārakāṃ yadumaṇḍitām
āyāti varadattaḥ sa lokavīra mahānaṭaḥ
tato haṃsān dhārtarāṣṭrān devalokanivāsinaḥ
uvāca bhagavāñ śakraḥ sāntvayitvā sureśvaraḥ
bhavanto bhrātaro 'smākaṃ kāśyapā devapakṣiṇaḥ
vimānavāhā devānāṃ sukṛtīnāṃ tathaiva ca
devānām asti kartavyaṃ kāryaṃ śatruvadhānvitam
tat kartavyaṃ na mantraś ca bhettavyo vaḥ kathaṃcana
akurvatāṃ devatājñām ugro daṇḍaḥ pated api
sarvatrāpratiṣiddhaṃ vo gamanaṃ haṃsasattamāḥ
gatvāpraveśyam anyeṣāṃ vajranābhapurottamam
ito 'ntaḥpuravāpīṣu caradhvam ucitaṃ hi vaḥ
tasyāsti kanyāratnaṃ hi trailokyātiśayaṃ śubham
nāmnā prabhāvatī nāma candrābheva prabhāvatī
varadānena sā labdhā mātrā kila varānanā
haimavatyā mahādevyāḥ sakāśād iti naḥ śrutam
svayaṃvarā ca sā kanyā bandhubhiḥ sthāpitā satī
ātmecchayā patiṃ haṃsā varayiṣyati śobhanā
tad bhavadbhir guṇā vācyāḥ pradyumnasya mahātmanaḥ
sadbhūtāḥ kularūpasya śīlasya vayasas tathā
yadā sā raktabhāvā ca vajranābhasutā satī
tasyāḥ sakāśāt saṃdeśo nayitavyaḥ samādhinā
pradyumnasya punas tasmād ānayadhvaṃ tathaiva ca
svabuddhyā prāptakālaṃ ca saṃvidheyaṃ hitaṃ mama
netravaktraprasādaś ca kartavyas tatra sarvathā
tathā tathā guṇā vācyāḥ pradyumnasya mahātmanaḥ
yathā yathā prabhāvatyā manas tatra bhavet sthiram
vṛttāntaś cānudivasaṃ pradeyo mama sarvathā
dvāravatyāṃ ca kṛṣṇasya bhratur mama yavīyasaḥ
tāvad yatnaś ca kartayaḥ pradyumno yāvad ātmavit
paryāvarted varārohāṃ vajranābhasutāṃ vibhuḥ
avadhyās te tu devānāṃ brahmaṇo varadarpitāḥ
devaputrair hi hantavyāḥ pradyumnapramukhair yudhi
naṭo dattavaras tasya veṣam āsthāya yādavāḥ
pradyumnādyā gamiṣyanti vajranābhavināśanāḥ
etac ca sarvaṃ kartavyam anyac ca svayam eva hi
prāptakālaṃ vidhātavyam asmākaṃ priyakāmyayā
praveśas tatra devānāṃ nāsti haṃsāḥ kathaṃcana
vajranābhepsite tatra praveśaḥ khalu sarvathā
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
te vāsavavacaḥ śrutvā haṃsā vajrapuraṃ yayuḥ
pūrvocitaṃ hi gamanaṃ tatra teṣāṃ janādhipa
te dīrghikāsu ramyāsu nipetur vīra pakṣiṇaḥ
padmotpalair āvṛtāsu kañcanaiḥ sparśanakṣamaiḥ
te vai nadanto madhuraṃ saṃskṛtāpūrvabhāṣiṇaḥ
pūrvam apy āgatās te tu vismayaṃ janayanti hi
antaḥpuropabhogyāsu cerūr vāpīṣu te nṛpa
iṣṭās te vajranābhasya triviṣṭapanivāsinaḥ
ālapantaḥ sumadhuraṃ dhārtarāṣṭrā janeśvara
sa tān uvāca daiteyo dhartarāṣṭrān idaṃ vacaḥ
triviṣṭape nityaratā bhavantaś cārubhāṣiṇaḥ
yadaivehotsavo 'smākaṃ bhavadbhir avagamyate
āgantavyaṃ jālapādāḥ svam idaṃ bhavatāṃ gṛham
viśrabdhaṃ ca praveṣṭavyaṃ triviṣṭapanivāsibhiḥ
te tathoktāḥ śakunayo vajranābhena bhārata
tathoty uktvā hi viviśur dānavendraniveśanam
cakruḥ paricayaṃ te ca devakāryavyapekṣayā
mānuṣālāpinas te tu kathāś cakruḥ pṛthagvidhāḥ
vaṃśabaddhāḥ kāśyapānāṃ sarvakalyāṇabhāginām
striyo remur viśeṣeṇa śṛṇvantyaḥ saṃgatāḥ kathāḥ
tato vicaratīṃ haṃsā dadṛśuś cāruhāsinīm
prabhāvatīṃ varārohāṃ vajranābhasutāṃ tadā
haṃsāḥ paricitāṃ cakrus tāṃ tataś cāruhāsinīm
sakhīṃ śucimukhī cakre haṃsī rājasutāṃ tadā
sā tāṃ kadācit papraccha vajranābhasutāṃ sakhīm
viśrambhitāṃ pṛthagyuktair ākhyānakaśatair varām
trailokyasundarīṃ vedmi tvām ahaṃ hi prabhāvati
rūpaśīlaguṇair devi kiṃcit tvāṃ vaktum utsahe
vyatikrāmati te bhīru yauvanaṃ cāruhāsini
yad atītaṃ punar naiti gataṃ srota ivāmbhasaḥ
kāmopabhogatulyā hi ratir devi na vidyate
strīṇāṃ jagati kalyāṇi satyam etad bravīmi te
svayaṃvaratve nyastā tvaṃ pitrā sarvāṅgaśobhane
na ca kiṃcid varayase devāsurakulodbhavam
vrīḍitā yānti suśroṇi pratyākhyātās tvayā śubhe
rūpaśauryaguṇair yuktāḥ sadṛśās tvatkulasya hi
āgatān necchase devi sadṛśān kularūpayoḥ
ihaiṣyati kim arthaṃ tvāṃ pradyumno rukmiṇīsutaḥ
trailokye yasya rūpeṇa sadṛśo 'tha kulena vā
gunair vā cārusarvāṅgi śauryeṇāpy atha vā śubhe
deveṣu devaḥ suśroṇi dānaveṣu ca dānavaḥ
mānuṣeṣv api dharmātmā mānuṣaḥ sa mahābalaḥ
yaṃ sadā devi dṛṣṭvā hi sravanti jaghanāni hi
āpīnānīva dhenūnāṃ srotāṃsi saritām iva
na pūrṇacandreṇa mukhaṃ nayane vā kuśeśayaiḥ
utsahāmopamātuṃ hi mṛgendreṇātha vā gatim
jagataḥ sāram uddhṛtya putraḥ sa vihitaḥ śubhe
kṛtvānaṅgaṃ vaśe sāṅgaṃ viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
hṛtena śambaro bālye yena pāpo nibarhitaḥ
māyāś ca sarvāḥ saṃprāptā na ca śīlaṃ vināśitam
yān yān guṇān pṛthuśroṇi manasā kalpayiṣyasi
eṣṭavyās triṣu lokeṣu pradyumne sarva eva te
rucyā vahnipratīkāśaḥ kṣamayā pṛthivīsamaḥ
tejasā sūryasadṛśo gāmbhīryeṇa hradopamaḥ
prabhāvatī śucimukhīm iti hovāca bhāvinī
viṣṇur mānuṣalokasthaḥ śrutaḥ sa bahuśo mayā
pituḥ kathayataḥ saumye nāradasya ca dhīmataḥ
śatruḥ sa kila daityānāṃ varjanīyaḥ kilānaghe
kulāni kila daityānāṃ tena dagdhāni mānini
pradīptena rathāṅgena śārṅgeṇa gadayā tathā
śākhānagaradeśeṣu vasanti kila ye 'surāḥ
ity ete dānavendreṇa saṃdiśyante hi taṃ prati
manoratho hi sarvāsāṃ strīṇām evaṃ śucismite
bhaved dhi me patikulaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ pitṛkulād iti
yadi nāmābhyupāyaḥ syāt tasyehāgamanaṃ prati
mahān anugraho me syāt kulaṃ syāt pāvitaṃ ca me
samarthanāṃ me pṛṣṭā tvaṃ prayaccha śucilāpini
pradyumnaḥ syād yathā bhartā mama vṛṣṇikulodbhavaḥ
atyantavairī daityānām udvejanakaro hariḥ
asurāṇāṃ striyo vṛddhāḥ kathayantyo mayā śrutāḥ
pradyumnasya tathā janma purastād api me śrutam
yathā ca tena nihato balavān kālaśambaraḥ
hṛdi me vartate nityaṃ pradyumnaḥ khalu sattame
hetuḥ sa nāsti tasyārthe yathā mama samāgamaḥ
dāsī tavāhaṃ sakhyārhe dūtye tvāṃ ca visarjaye
paṇḍitāsi vadopāyaṃ mama tasya ca saṃgame
tatas tāṃ sāntvayitvā sā prahasantīdam abravīt
tatra dūtī gamiṣyāmi tavāhaṃ cāruhāsini
imāṃ bhaktiṃ tavodārāṃ pravakṣyāmi śucismite
tathā caiva kariṣyāmi yathaiṣyati tavāntikam
sākṣāt kāmena suśroṇi bhaviṣyasi sakāminī
iti me bhāṣitaṃ satyaṃ smarethāḥ śucilocane
kathākuśalatāṃ pitre kathayasvāyatekṣaṇe
mama tvaṃ tatra me devi hitaṃ samyak prapatsyase
ity uktvā sā tathā cakre yat tat sā tām athābravīt
dānavendraś ca tāṃ haṃsīṃ papracchāntaḥpure tadā
prabhāvatyā samākhyātā kathākuśalatā tava
tattvaṃ śucimukhi brūhi kathāṃ yogyatayā vare
kiṃ tvayā dṛṣṭam āścaryaṃ jagaty uttamapakṣiṇi
adṛṣṭapūrvam anyair vā yogyāyogyam anindite
sovāca vajranābhaṃ tu haṃsī naravarottama
śrūyatām ity athāmantrya dānavendraṃ mahādyutim
dṛṣṭā me śāṇḍilī nāma sādhvī dānavasattama
āścaryaṃ karma kurvantī merupārśve manasvinī
sumanā caiva kausalyā sarvabhūtahite ratā
tathāvidūre śāṇḍilyāḥ śailaputryāḥ śubhā sakhī
naṭaś caiva mayā dṛṣṭo munidattavaraḥ śubhaḥ
kāmarūpī ca bhojyaś ca trailokye nityasaṃmataḥ
kurūn yātyuttarān vīra kālāmradvīpam eva ca
bhadrāśvān ketumālāṃś ca dvīpān anyāṃs tathānagha
devagandharvageyāni nṛtyāni vividhāni ca
sa vetti devān nṛtyena vismāpayati sarvadā
vajranābha uvāca
śrutam etan mayā haṃsi nacirād iva vistaram
cāraṇānāṃ kathayatāṃ siddhānāṃ ca mahātmanām
kutūhalaṃ mamāpy asti sarvathā pakṣinandini
naṭe dattavare tasmin saṃstavas tu na vidyate
haṃsy uvāca
saptadvīpān vicarati naṭaḥ sa ditijottama
guṇavantaṃ janaṃ śrutvā guṇahāryaḥ sa sarvathā
tava cecchṛṇuyād vīra sadbhūtaṃ guṇavistaram
naṭaṃ tadāgataṃ viddhi puraṃ tava mahāsura
vajranābha uvāca
upāyaḥ sṛjyatāṃ haṃsi yeneha sa naṭaḥ śubhe
āgacchen mama bhadraṃ te viṣayaṃ pakṣinandini
te haṃsā vajranābhena kāryahetor visarjitāḥ
devendrāyātha kṛṣṇāya śaśaṃsuḥ sarvam eva tat
adhokṣajena pradyumno niyuktas tatra karmaṇi
prabhāvatyāś ca saṃsarge vajranābhavadhe tathā
daivīṃ māyāṃ samāśritya saṃvidhāya harir naṭam
naṭaveṣeṇa bhaimānāṃ preṣayām āsa bharata
pradyumnaṃ nāyakaṃ kṛtvā sāmbaṃ kṛtvā vidūṣakam
pāripārśvaṃ gadaṃ vīram anyān bhaimāṃs tathaiva ca
vāramukhyā naṭīḥ kṛtvā tat tūryasadṛśaṃ tadā
tathaiva bhadraṃbhadrasya sahāyāṃś ca tathāvidhān
pradyumnavihitaṃ ramyaṃ vimānaṃ te mahārathāḥ
jagmur āruhya kāryārthaṃ devānām amitaijasām
ekaikasya samā rūpe puruṣāḥ puruṣasya te
strīṇāṃ ca sadṛśāḥ sarve svararūpair narādhipa
te vajranagarasyātha śākhānagaram uttamam
jagmur dānavasaṃkīrṇaṃ supuraṃ nāma nāmataḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tataḥ supuravāsīnām asurāṇāṃ narādhipa
pūrvaśruto naṭaḥ prāptaḥ kautūhalam ajījanat
naṭasyātha dadur daityāḥ satkāraṃ parayā mudā
pratyayārthaṃ daduś cāpi ratnāni subahūny atha
tataḥ sa nanṛte tatra varadatto naṭas tadā
supure puravāsīnāṃ paraṃ harṣaṃ samādadhat
rāmāyaṇaṃ mahākāvyam uddeśaṃ nāṭakīkṛtam
janma viṣṇor ameyasya rākṣasendravadhepsayā
lomapādo daśaratha ṛśyaśṛṅgaṃ mahāmunim
śāntāmānāyayām āsa gaṇikābhiḥ sahānagha
rāmalakṣmaṇaśatrughnā bharataś caiva bharata
ṛśyaśṛṅgaś ca śāntā ca tathārūpair naṭaiḥ kṛtaiḥ
tatkālajīvito vṛddhā dānavā vismayaṃ gatāḥ
ācacakṣuś ca teṣāṃ vai rūpatulyatvam acyuta
saṃskārābhinayau teṣāṃ prastāvānāṃ ca dhāraṇam
dṛṣṭvā sarve praveśaṃ ca dānavā vismayaṃ gatāḥ
te raktā vismayaṃ nedur asurāḥ parayā mudā
utthāyotthāya nāṭyasya viśeṣeṣu punaḥ punaḥ
dadur vastrāṇi tuṣṭāś ca graiveyavalayāni ca
hārān manoharāṃś caiva hemavaidūryabhūṣitān
pṛthagartheṣu datteṣu ślokais te tuṣṭuvur naṭāḥ
asurāṃś ca munīṃś caiva gotrair abhijanair api
preṣitaṃ vajranābhasya śākhānagaravāsibhiḥ
naṭasya divyarūpasya narendrāgamanaṃ tadā
purā śrutārtho daityeśaḥ preṣayām āsa bharata
ānīyatāṃ vajrapuraṃ naṭo 'sāv iti harṣitaḥ
dānavendravacaḥ śrutvā śākhānagaravāsibhiḥ
nītā vajrapuraṃ ramyaṃ naṭaveṣeṇa yādavāḥ
āvāsaś ca tato dattaḥ sukṛto viśvakarmaṇā
eṣṭavyaṃ yac ca tat sarvaṃ dattaṃ śataguṇottaram
atha kālotsavaṃ cakre vajranābho mahāsuraḥ
kārayām āsa ramyaṃ ca raṅgavāṭaṃ prahṛṣṭavat
tatas tān pariviśrāntān prekṣārthāya pracodayat
dattvā ratnāni bhūrīṇi vajranābho mahāsuraḥ
upaviṣṭaś ca tān draṣṭuṃ saha jñātibhir ātmavān
chatre cāntaḥpuraṃ sthāpya cakṣur dṛśye janādhipa
bhaimāpi baddhanepathyā naṭaveṣadharās tathā
kāryārthaṃ bhīmakarmāṇo nṛtyārtham upacakramuḥ
tato ghanaṃ saśuṣiraṃ murajānakabhūṣitam
tantrīsvaraguṇair viddham ātodyān anvavādayan
tatas tu devagāndhāraṃ chālikyaṃ śravaṇām ṛtam
bhaimastriyaḥ prajagire manaḥśrotrasukhāvaham
āgāndhāragrāmarāgaṃ gaṅgāvataraṇaṃ tadā
viddham āsāritaṃ ramyaṃ jagire svarasaṃpadā
layatālasamaṃ śrutvā gaṅgāvataraṇaṃ śubham
asurāṃs toṣayām āsur utthāyothāya bhārata
nāndīṃ ca vādayām āsa pradyumno gada eva ca
sāmbaś ca vīryasaṃpannaḥ kāryārthaṃ naṭatāṃ gataḥ
nāndyante ca tadā ślokaṃ gaṅgāvataraṇāśritam
raukmiṇeyas tadovāca samyak svabhinayānvitam
rambhābhisāraṃ kauveraṃ nāṭakaṃ nanṛtus tataḥ
śūro rāvaṇarūpeṇa rambhāveṣā manovatī
