nalakūbaras tu pradyumnaḥ sāmbas tasya vidūṣakaḥ
kailāso rūpitaś cāpi māyayā yadunandanaiḥ
śāpaś ca dattaḥ kruddhena rāvaṇasya durātmanaḥ
nalakūbareṇātha yathā rambho cāpy atha sāntvitā
etat prakaraṇaṃ vīrā nanṛtur yadunandanāḥ
nāradasya muneḥ kīrtiṃ sarvajñasya mahātmanaḥ
pādoddhāreṇa nṛtyena tathaivābhinayena ca
tuṣṭuvur dānavā vīrā bhaimān amitatejasaḥ
te dadur vastramukhyāni ratnāny ābharaṇāni ca
hārāṃs taralaviddhāṃś ca vaidūryamaṇibhūṣitān
vimānāni vicitrāṇi rathāṃś cākāśagāminaḥ
gajān ākāśagāṃś caiva divyanāgakulodbhavān
candanāni ca divyāni śītāni rasavanti ca
gurūṇy agurumukhyāni gandhāḍhyāni ca bhārata
cintāmaṇīn udārāṃś ca cintite sarvakāmadān
prekṣāsu tāsu bahvīṣu dadanto dānavās tadā
dhanaratnair virahitāḥ kṛtāḥ puruṣasattama
striyo dānavamukhyānāṃ tathaiva ca janeśvara
tato haṃsī prabhāvatyāḥ sakhī prāha prabhāvatīm
gatāsmi dvārakāṃ ramyāṃ bhaimaguptām anindite
pradyumnaś ca mayā dṛṣṭo vivikte cārulocane
bhaktiś ca kathitā tasya mayā tava śucismite
tena hṛṣṭena kālaś ca kṛtaḥ kamalalocane
adya pradoṣasamaye tvayā saha samāgamaḥ
tad adya ruciraśroṇi tava priyasamāgamaḥ
na hy ātmavanto bhāṣanti mithyā bhaimakulodbhavāḥ
tataḥ prabhāvatī hṛṣṭā haṃsīṃ tām idam abravīt
uṣitāsi mamāvāse svaptum arhasi sundari
tvayāhaṃ sahitāvāse draṣṭum icchāmi kaiśavim
niḥsādhvasā bhaviṣyāmi tvayā saha vihaṃgame
haṃsī tatheti covāca sakhīṃ kamalalocanām
āruroha ca tad dharmyaṃ prabhāvatyā vihaṃgamā
viśvakarmakṛte tasmin harmyapṛṣṭhe prabhāvatī
saṃvidhānaṃ cakārāśu pradyumnāgamanakṣamam
tasmin kṛte saṃvidhāne kāmam ānayituṃ yayau
prabhāvatīm anujñāpya haṃsī vāyusamā gatau
sā gatvābhyāgatā haṃsī prabhāvatim athābravīt
abhyeti raukmiṇeyo 'sāv āśvasāyatalocane
pradyumno nīyamānaṃ tu dadṛśe mālyam ātmavān
bhramarair āvṛtaṃ vīraḥ sugandham arimardana
nililye tatra mālye tu bhūtvā madhukaras tadā
prabhāvatyā nīyamāne viditārthaḥ pratāpavān
praveśitaṃ ca tan mālyaṃ strībhir madhukarāyutam
avidūre ca vinyastaṃ prabhāvatyā janādhipa
bhramarās te yayuḥ saumya saṃdhyākāle hy upasthite
sa bhaimapravaro vīras taiḥ sahāyair vihinataḥ
karṇotpale prabhāvatyā nililye śanakair iva
tataḥ prabhāvatī haṃsīm uvāca vadatāṃ varā
udyacchantaṃ pūrṇacandraṃ samīkṣyātimanoharam
sakhi dahyanti me 'ṅgāni mukhaṃ ca pariśuṣyati
autsukyaṃ hṛdi cātīva ko 'yaṃ vyādhir anauṣadhaḥ
dadhad dviguṇam autsukyam asau pūrṇaniśākaraḥ
navoditaḥ śītaraśmiḥ saṃvihārocitapriyaḥ
na dṛṣṭapūrvo hi mayā śrutimātreṇa kāṅkṣitaḥ
aho dhūmayate 'ṅgāni strīsvabhāvasya dhik khalu
kalpayāmi yathā buddhyā yadi nābhyeti me priyaḥ
kumudvatīgataṃ mārgaṃ hā gamiṣyāmy akiṃcanā
madanāśīviṣeṇāsmi daṣṭā hāhā manasvinī
śītavīryāḥ prakṛtyaiva jagato hlādanāḥ sukhāḥ
dahanti mama gātrāṇi kiṃ nu candragabhastayaḥ
prakṛtyā śītalo vāyur nānāpuṣparajovahaḥ
dāvāgnisadṛśo me 'dya daṃdahīti śubhāṃ tanum
tataḥ saṃkalpaye eva sthairyaṃ kāryam ivātmanaḥ
nāvatiṣṭhati nirvīryaṃ manaḥ saṃkalpadharṣitam
vimanaskāsmi muhyāmi vepathur me mahān hṛdi
baṃbhramīti ca me dṛṣṭir hā hā yāmi dhruvaṃ kṣayam
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
āviṣṭeyaṃ mayā bālā sarvathety avagamya tu
kārṣṇir hṛṣṭena manasā saṃsīm idam uvāca ha
daityendratanayāṃ prāptam avagacchasva mām iha
ṣaṭpadaiḥ saha ṣaṭpādo bhūtvā mālye nilīya tu
vidheyo 'smi prabhāvatyā yatheṣṭaṃ mayi vartatām
ity uktvā darśayām āsa surūpo rūpam ātmanaḥ
tad dharmyapṛṣṭhaṃ prabhayā dyotitaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ
abhibhūtā prabhā caiva rājaṃś candrodbhavā śubhā
prabhāvatyās tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā vavṛve kāmasāgaraḥ
candrasyevodaye prāpte parvaṇyāṃ saritāṃ patiḥ
salajjādhomukhī kiṃcit kiṃcit tiryag avekṣiṇī
prabhāvatī tadā tasthau niścalevāmalekṣaṇā
kareṇādhaḥpradeśe tāṃ cārubhūṣaṇabhūṣitām
spṛṣṭvovāca varārohāṃ romāñcitatanus tanum
manorathaśatair labdhaṃ kiṃ pūrṇendusamaprabham
adhomukhaṃ mukhaṃ kṛtvā na māṃ kiṃcit prabhāṣase
prabhopamardaṃ mā kārṣīr vadanasya varānane
sādhvasaṃ tyajyatāṃ bhīru dāsaḥ sādhv anugṛhyatām
na kālam iva paśyāmi bhīru bhīrutvam utsṛja
yācāmy eṣo 'ñjalaṃ kṛtvā prāptakālaṃ nibodha me
gāndharveṇa vivāhena kuruṣvānugrahaṃ mama
deśakālānurūpeṇa rūpeṇānuttamā satī
upaspṛśya tato bhaimo maṇisthaṃ jātavedasam
juhāva samaye vīraḥ puṣpair mantrān udīrayan
jagrahātha karaṃ tasyā varābharaṇabhūṣitam
cakre pradakṣiṇaṃ caiva taṃ maṇisthaṃ hutāśanam
prajajvāla sa tejasvī mānayann acyutātmajam
bhagavāñ jagataḥ sākṣī śubhasyāthāśubhasya ca
uddiśya dakṣiṇāṃ vīro viprāṇāṃ yadunandanaḥ
uvāca haṃsīṃ dvārasthāṃ tiṣṭhāvāṃ rakṣa pakṣiṇi
tasyāṃ praṇamya yātāyāṃ kāmas tāṃ cārulocanām
grahāya dakṣiṇe haste nināya śayanottamam
ūrāv evopaveśyaināṃ sāntvayitvā punaḥ punaḥ
cucumba śanakair gaṇḍe vāsayan mukhamārutaiḥ
tato 'syā āpapau vaktraṃ padmaṃ madhukaro yathā
āliliṅge ca suśroṇīṃ krameṇa ratikovidaḥ
arāmayad rahasy enāṃ na codvejigavāṃs tadā
āpi kṛtsnaṃ caraty arthaṃ ratikāryaviśāradaḥ
uvāsa sa tayā sārdhaṃ raman kṛṣṇasutaḥ prabhuḥ
aruṇodayakāle ca yayau yatra naṭālayaḥ
akāmayā prabhāvatyā kathaṃcit sa visarjitaḥ
tām eva manasā kāntāṃ kāntarupaḥ samudvahan
ta ūṣur naṭaveṣeṇa kāryārthaṃ bhaimavaṃśajāḥ
pratīkṣantas tadā vākyam indrakeśavayos tadā
udyogaṃ vajranābhasya trailokyavijayaṃ prati
pratīkṣanto mahātmāno guhyasaṃrakṣaṇe ratāḥ
kaśyapasya muneḥ satraṃ yāvat tāvan narādhipa
devāsurāṇāṃ sarveṣām avirodho mahātmanām
trailokyavijayārthāya jayatāṃ dharmacāriṇām
evaṃ kālapratīkṣāṇāṃ vasatāṃ tatra dhīmatām
saṃprāptaḥ prāvṛṣo ramyaḥ sarvabhūtamanoharaḥ
ahar niśaṃ ca vṛttāntaṃ prayacchanti manojavāḥ
śakrakeśavayor haṃsāḥ kumārāṇāṃ mahātmanāṃ
reme saha prabhāvatyā pradyumnaś cānurūpayā
rātrau rātrau mahātejā dhārtarāṣṭrābhirakṣitaḥ
tair hi vajrapuraṃ haṃsair vasadbhir vāsavājñayā
vyāptaṃ nṛpa naṭāṃs tāṃś ca na viduḥ kālamohitāḥ
divāpi raukmiṇeyas tu prabhāvatyā nṛpālaye
tiṣṭhaty antarhito vīro haṃsasaṃghābhirakṣitaḥ
māyayāsya praticchāyā dṛśyate hi naṭālaye
dehārdhena tu kauravya siṣeva sa prabhāvatīm
saṃnatiṃ vinayaṃ śīlaṃ līlāṃ dākṣyaṃ vilāsitām
spṛhayanty asurā dṛṣṭvā vidvattāṃ ca mahātmanām
rūpaṃ vilāsaṃ gandhaṃ ca mṛjāṃ bhāṣām athāryatām
tāsāṃ yādavanārīṇāṃ spṛhayanty asurastriyaḥ
vajranābhasya tu bhrātā sunābho nāma viśrutaḥ
duhitṛdvayaṃ ca nṛpates tasya rūpaguṇānvitam
ekā candravatī nāmnā guṇavaty atha cāparā
prabhāvatyālayaṃ te tu vrajataḥ khalu nityadā
dadṛśāte tu te tatra ratisaktāṃ prabhāvatīm
paripapracchatuś caiva viśrambhopagatāṃ satīm
sovāca mama vidyāsti yādhītā kāṅkṣitaṃ patim
ratyartham ānayaty āśu saubhagyaṃ ca prayacchati
devaṃ vā dānavaṃ vāpi vivaśaṃ sadya eva hi
sāhaṃ ramāmi kāntena devaputreṇa dhīmatā
dṛśyatāṃ matprabhāvena pradyumnaḥ supriyo mama
te dṛṣṭvā vismayaṃ yāte rūpayauvanasaṃpadam
punar evābravīt te tu bhaginyau cāruhāsinī
prabhāvatī varārohā kālaprāptam idaṃ vacaḥ
devā dharmaratā nityaṃ dambhaśīlā mahāsurāḥ
devās tapasi raktā hi sukharaktā mahāsurāḥ
devāḥ satyaratā nityam anṛte tu mahāsurāḥ
dharmastapaś ca satyaṃ ca yatra tatra jayo dhruvam
devaputrau varayataṃ patividyāṃ dadāmy aham
ucitau matprabhāvena sadya evopalapsyatha
tāṃ tathety ūcatur hṛṣṭe bhaginyau cārulocanām
paripapraccha bhaimaṃ ca kāryaṃ tat prati māninī
sa pitṛvyaṃ gadaṃ vīraṃ sāmbaṃ cāpy abravīt tadā
rūpānvitau suśīlau ca śūrau ca raṇakarmaṇi
prabhāvaty uvāca
parituṣṭena dattā me vidyā durvāsasā purā
parituṣṭena saubhāgyaṃ sadā kanyātvam eva ca
devadānavayakṣāṇāṃ yaṃ dhyāsyasi sa te patiḥ
bhaviteti mayā caiva vīro 'yam abhikāṅkṣitaḥ
gṛhṇītaṃ tad imāṃ vidyāṃ sadyo vāṃ priyasaṃgamaḥ
tato jagṛhatur hṛṣṭe tāṃ vidyāṃ bhaginīmukhāt
dadhyatur gadasāmbau ca vidyām abhyasya te śubhe
tau pradyumnena sahitau praviṣṭau bhaimanandanau
pracchannau māyayā vīrau kārṣṇinā māyinā nṛpa
gāndharveṇa vivāhena tāv apy aribalārdanau
pāṇiṃ jagṛhatur vīrau mantrapūrvaṃ satāṃ priyau
candravatyā gadaḥ sāmbo guṇavatyā tu kaiśaviḥ
remire 'surakanyābhir vīrās te yadupuṃgavāḥ
mārgamāṇās tv anujñāṃ te śakrakeśavayos tadā
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
nabho nabhasye 'tha nirīkṣya māsi
kāmas tadā toyadavṛndakīrṇam
prabhāvatīṃ cāruviśālanetrām
uvāca pūrṇendunikāśavaktraḥ
tavānanābho varagātri candro
na dṛśyate sundari cārubimbaḥ
tvatkeśapāśapratimair niruddho
balāhakaiś cārunirantaroru
saṃdṛśyate subhru taḍid ghanasthā
tvaṃ hemacārvābharaṇānviteva
muñcanti dhārāś ca ghanā nadantas
tvaddhārayaṣṭeḥ sadṛśā varāṅgi
ghanapradeśeṣu balākapaṅktayas
tvadṛntapaṅktipratimā vibhānti
nimagnapadmāni saraḥsu subhru
na bhānti toyāni rayākulāni
amī ghanā vāyuvaśopayātā
balākamālāmalacārudantāḥ
anyonyam abhyāhanituṃ pravṛttā
vaneṣu nāgā iva śukladantāḥ
dhanus trivarṇaṃ varagātri paśya
kṛtaṃ tavāpāṅgam ivānanastham
vibhūṣayantaṃ gaganaṃ ghanāṃś ca
praharṣaṇaṃ kāmijanasya kānte
ghanānnadantaḥ pratinardamānān
nirīkṣya suśroṇi śikhīn prahṛṣṭān
samāhṛtān ucchritapicchabhārān
priyābhirāmānupanṛtyamānān
harmyeṣu cānye śaśipāṇḍureṣu
rājanti suśroṇi mayūrasaṃghāḥ
muhūrtaśobhām aticārurūpāṃ
dattvā patanto valabhīmukheṣu
praklinnapakṣās tarumastakeṣu
muhūrtacūḍāmaṇitāṃ vidhāya
prayānti bhūmiṃ navaśādvalānām
āśaṅkamānā dhṛtacārudehāḥ
pravāti dhārāntaraniḥsṛtaś ca
sukho 'nilaś candanapaṅkaśītaḥ
kadambasarjārjunapuṣpabhūtaṃ
samāvahan gandham naṅgabandhum
ratiśramasvedavināśahetur
navodabhārānayane ca hetuḥ
na mārutaḥ syād yadi cārugātri
na meghakālo mama vallabhaḥ syāt
evaṃvidheṣu priyasaṃgameṣu
ratāvasāne yad upaiti vāyuḥ
ratiśramasvedaharaḥ sugandhī
tataḥ paraṃ kiṃ sukham asti loke
jalāplutān īkṣya mahānadīnāṃ
sugātri haṃsāḥ pulināny adhṛṣṭāḥ
gatāḥ śramaṃ mānasavāsalubdhāḥ
sasārasāḥ krauñcagaṇānuviddhāḥ
na bhānti nadyo 'dya sarāṃsi caiva
hatatviṣaś cāyatacārunetre
gateṣu haṃseṣv atha sāraseṣu
rathāṅgatulyāhvayaneṣu caiva
bhogaikadeśena śubhaṃ śayānaṃ
druvaṃ jagannātham upendram īśam
nidrābhyupetā varakālatajjñā
śriyaṃ praṇamyottamacārurūpām
nidrāyamāṇe bhagavaty upendre
meghāmbarākrāntaniśākaro 'dya
padmāmalābhaḥ kamalāyatākṣi
kṛṣṇasya vaktrānukṛtiṃ karoti
kadambanīpārjunaketakānāṃ
srajo dhruvaṃ kṛṣṇam upānayanti
puṣpāṇi cānyāny ṛtavaḥ samastāḥ
kṛṣṇāt prasādān abhikāṅkṣamāṇāḥ
nāgāś caranto viṣadigdhavaktrāḥ
spṛśanti puṣpāṇy atha pādapānām
pepīyamānān bhramarair janānāṃ
kautūhalaṃ te janayanty atīva
toyātibhārāmbudavṛndanaddhaṃ
nabhaḥ patiṣyantam ivābhīvīkṣya
nipātagambhīram atipraviṣṭaṃ
manoharaṃ cārumukhastanoru
balākamālākulamālyadāmnā
nirīkṣya ramyaṃ ghanavṛndam etat
sasyāni bhūmāv abhivarṣamāṇaṃ
jagaddhitārthaṃ vimalāṅgayaṣṭi
jalāvalambāmbudavṛndakarṣī
ghanair ghanān yodhayatīva vāyuḥ
pravṛttacakro nṛpatir vanasthān
gajān gajaiḥ svair iva vīryadṛptān
abhaumam ambho visṛjanti meghāḥ
pūtaṃ pavitraṃ pavanaiḥ sugandhi
harṣāvahaṃ cātakabarhiṇānāṃ
varāṇḍajānāṃ jaladapriyāṇām
plavaṃgamaḥ ṣoḍaśapakṣaśāyī
virauti goṣṭhaḥ saha kāminībhiḥ
ṛco dvijātiḥ priyasatyadharmā
yathā suśiṣyaiḥ paricaryamāṇaḥ
guṇo mahāṃs toyajakālajo 'yaṃ
pravṛddhameghasvanabhīṣitā yat
pariṣvajantyaḥ parivardhayanti
vināpi śayyāsamayaṃ priyāṇām
doṣo 'yam ekaḥ salilāgamasya
māṃ pratyudārān vayavarṇaśīle
na dṛśyate yat tava vaktratulyo
ghanagrahagrastatanuḥ śaśāṅkaḥ
pradṛśyate bhīru yadā śaśāṅko
ghanāntarastho jagataḥ pradīpaḥ
tadā nu paśyanti janāḥ prahṛṣṭā
banduṃ pravāsād iva saṃnivṛttam
vilāpasākṣī priyahīnitānāṃ
saṃdṛśyate bhīru yadā śaśāṅkaḥ
netrotsavaḥ proṣitakāmukānāṃ
dṛṣṭvaiva kāntaṃ bhavatīty avaimi
netrotsavaḥ kāntasamāgatānāṃ
dāvāgnitulyaḥ priyahīnitānām
tenaiva dehena varāṅganānāṃ
candro 'pi tāvat priyavipriyaś ca
vināpi candreṇa pure pitus te
yataḥ prabhā candragabhastigaurī
guṇāguṇaṃ candramaso na vetsi
yatas tato 'haṃ praśaśaṃsayiṣye
avāpa yo brāhmaṇarājyam īḍyo
durāpamanyaiḥ sukṛtais tapobhiḥ
gāyanti viprāḥ pavamānasaṃjñaṃ
yaṃ sāmagāḥ parvaṇi cāpy udāram
pitā budhasyottamavīryakarmā
purūravā yasya suto nṛdevaḥ
prāṇāgnir īḍhyo 'gnim ajījanad yo
naṣṭaṃ śamīgarbhabhavaṃ bhavātmā
tathaiva paścāc cakame mahātmā
puror vaśīm apsarasāṃ variṣṭhām
pītaḥ purā yo 'mṛtasarvadeho
munipravīrair varagātri ghoraiḥ
nṛpaḥ kuśāgraiḥ punar eva yaś ca
dhīmān gato 'gnir divi pūjyate ca
āyuś ca vaṃśe nahuṣaś ca yasya
yo devarājatvam avāpa vīraḥ
devātidevo bhagavān prasūto
vaṃśe harir yasya jagat praṇetā
bhaimapravīraḥ surakāryahetor
yaḥ subhru dakṣasya vṛtaḥ sutābhiḥ
babhūva rājā ca vasuś ca yasya
vaṃśe mahātmā śāśivaṃśaketuḥ
yaś cakravartitvam avāpa vīraḥ
svaiḥ karmabhiḥ śakrasamaprabhāvaḥ
yaduś ca rājā śāśivaṃśamukhyo
yo 'vāpa mahyām adhirājabhāvam
bhojāḥ kule yasya narādhipasya
vīrāḥ prasūtāḥ surarājatulyāḥ
na kutsito yasya nṛpo 'sti vaṃśe
na nāstiko naikṛtiko 'tha vāpi
aśraddadhāno 'py atha vā kadaryaḥ
śauryeṇa vā vāriruhākṣi hīnaḥ
vaṃśe vadhūs tvaṃ kamalāyatākṣi
ślāghyā guṇānām api pātrabhūtā
kuru praṇāmaṃ śikharāgradanti
tasya tvamīśasya satāṃ priyasya
nārāyaṇātmabhavāyanāya
lokāyanāya tridaśāyanāya
khagendraketoḥ puruṣottamāya
kuru praṇāmaṃ śvaśurāya devi
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
satrāvasāne tu muneḥ kaśyapasyātitejasaḥ
jagmur devāsurāḥ svāni sthānāny amitavikramāḥ
vajranābho 'pi nirvṛtte satre kaśyapam abhyagāt
trailokyavijayākāṅkṣi tam uvācātha kaśyapaḥ
vajranābha nibodhasva śrotavyaṃ yadi cen mama
vasa vajrapure putra svajanena samāvṛtaḥ
tapasābhyadhikaḥ śakraḥ śaktaś caiva svabhāvataḥ
brahmaṇyaś ca kṛtajñaś ca jyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhatamo gunaiḥ
rājā kṛtsnasya jagataḥ pātrabhūtaḥ satāṃ gatiḥ
saṃprāpto lokarājyaṃ sa sarvabhūtahite rataḥ
naiva śakyas tvayā jetuṃ vajranābha vihanyase
ahiṃ padā vyutkraman vai na cirād vinaśiṣyasi
vajranābhas tu tad vākyaṃ nābhinandati bharata
kālapāśaparītāṅgo martukāma ivauṣadham
abhivādya sa durbuddhiḥ kaśyapaṃ lokabhāvanam
trailokyavijayārambhe matiṃ cakre durāsadaḥ
jñātiyodhān samānīya mitrāṇi subahūni ca
pratasthe svargam evāgre vijigīṣur viśāṃ pate
etasminn antare devau kṛṣṇendrau ca mahābalau
preṣayām āsatur haṃsān vajranābhavadhaṃ prati
samāgatās tu tac chrutvā yadumukhyā mahābalāḥ
mantrayitvā mahātmānaś cintām āpedire tadā
vajranābho 'dya hantavyaḥ pradyumnenety asaṃśayam
tayor duhitaro bhāryā bhaktyā tāḥ sarvabhāvanāḥ
sarvāḥ sagarbhās tāś caiva kiṃ tu kāryam anantaram
prāptaḥ prasavakālaś ca tāsāṃ nāticirād iva
saṃmantrayitvaitad arthaṃ haṃsān ūcur mahābalāḥ
ākhyeyam arthavat kṛtsnaṃ śakrakeśavayos tadā
haṃsair gatvā tadākhyātaṃ devayos tad yathātatham
tābhyāṃ haṃsās tu saṃdiṣṭā na bhetavyam iti prabho
utpatsyanti gunaiḥ ślāghyāḥ putrā vaḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
garbhasthāḥ sarvavedāṃś ca sāṅgān vetsyanty aninditāḥ
tathā cānāgataṃ sarvam astrāṇi vividhāni ca
sadya eṣa yuvānaś ca bhaviṣyanti supaṇḍ itāḥ
evam uktvā gatā haṃsāḥ punar vajrapuraṃ vibho
śaśaṃsuś caiva bhaimānāṃ śakrakeśavabhāṣitam
prabhāvatī tadā putraṃ suṣuve sadṛśaṃ pituḥ
sadyoyauvanasaṃprāptaṃ sarvajñaṃ caiva bhārata
māsamātreṇa suṣuve devī candravatī nṛpa
candraprabham iti khyātaṃ tanayaṃ sadṛśaṃ pituḥ
sadyaś ca yauvanaprāptaṃ sarvajñatvaṃ ca bhārata
guṇavaty api putraṃ ca guṇavantam aninditā
yuvānāv atha sadyas tau sarvaśāstrārthakovidau
indropendraprasādena saṃvṛttau yadunandanau
harmyapṛṣṭhe vardhamānā hṛṣṭās te yadunandanāḥ
indropendrecchayā vīra nānyathety avadhāryatām
niveditāś ca saṃbhrāntair dautair ākāśarakṣibhiḥ
vajranābhāya vīrāya triviṣṭapajayaiṣiṇe
vicārya sarve gṛhyantāṃ mamaite gṛhadharṣakāḥ
ity uvācāsurapatir vajranābho durāsadaḥ
tataḥ sainyaṃ samājñaptam asurendreṇa dhīmatā
āvārayām āsa diśaḥ sarvāḥ kurukulodvaha
gṛhyantām āśu vadhyantām iti vācas tatas tataḥ
uccerur asurendrasya śāsanād ariśāsana
tac chrutvā vyathitās teṣāṃ mātaraḥ putravatsalāḥ
rurudus tā rudantyo 'tha pradyumnaḥ sahasābravīt
mā bhaiṣṭa jīvamāneṣu sthiteṣv asmāsu sarvathā
kiṃ no daityāḥ kariṣyanti sarvathā bhadram astu vaḥ
prabhāvatīm athovāca pradyumno viklavāṃ sthitām
pitā tava gadāpāṇiḥ pitṛvyaś ca sthitas tava
bhrātaraś caiva te devi jñātayaś ca tathāpare
ete pūjyāś ca mānyāś ca tavārthe khalu sarvathā
bhaginyau pṛccha bhadraṃ te kāle 'yaṃ khalu dāruṇaḥ
maraṇaṃ sahamānānāṃ yudhyatāṃ vijayo dhruvam
dānavendrādayo hy ete yotsyante 'smadvadhaiṣiṇaḥ
kim atra kāryam asmābhiḥ sarvaiś cakrāntarasthitaiḥ
prabhāvatī rudantī tu pradyumnam idam abravīt
śirasy añjalim ādhāya jānubhyāṃ patitā kṣitau
gṛhāṇa śastram ātmānaṃ rakṣa śatrunibarhaṇa
jīvanputrāṃś ca dārāṃś ca draṣṭāsi yadunandana
āryāṃ nṛvara vaidarbhīm aniruddhaṃ ca mānada
smṛtvaitān mokṣayātmānaṃ vyasanād arimardana
durvāsasā varo datto muninā mama dhīmatā
vaidhavyarahitā hṛdyā jīvaputrā bhaviṣyasi
eṣa me hṛdayāśvāso bhavitā na tad anyathā
sūryāgnitejaso vākyaṃ muner indrānujātmaja
ity uktvā sāsim ādāya sūpaspṛṣṭvā manasvinī
pradadau raukmiṇeyāya jayasveti varaṃ varā
sa taṃ jagrāha dharmātmā prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
praṇamya śirasā dattaṃ priyayā bhaktiyuktayā
candravaty api nistriṃśaṃ gadāya pradadau mudā
tathā guṇavatī caiva sāmbāyāsiṃ mahātmane
haṃsaketum athovāca pradyumnaḥ praṇataṃ prabhuḥ
ihaiva sāmbasahitau yudhyasva saha dānavaiḥ
ākāśe dikṣu sarvāsu yotsyāmy aham āriṃdama
ity uktvātha rathaṃ cakre māyayā māyināṃ varaḥ
sahasraśirasaṃ nāgaṃ kṛtvā sārathim ātmavān
anantabhogaṃ kauravya sarvanāgottamottamam
sa tena rathamukhyena harṣayan vai prabhāvatīm
cacārāsurasainyeṣu tṛṇeṣv iva hutāśanaḥ
śarair āśīviṣaprakhyair ardhacandrānukāribhiḥ
bhedanair gādhanaiś caiva tatarda ditisaṃbhavān
asurāś ca raṇe mattāḥ kārṣṇiṃ śatrair itas tataḥ
jaghnuḥ kamalapatrākṣaṃ paraṃ niścayam āsthitāḥ
ciccheda bāhūn keṣāṃcit keyūravalayojjvalān
sukuṇḍalāni cānyeṣāṃ śirāṃsy api sa cicchide
kṣuracchinnaiḥ śirobhis taiḥ kāyaiś ca śakalair api
asurāṇāṃ mahī kīrṇā pradyumnenātitejasā
deveśvaro devagaṇaiḥ sahitaḥ samitiṃjayaḥ
dadarśa mudito yuddhaṃ bhaimānāṃ ditijaiḥ saha
ye gadaṃ caiva sāmbaṃ ca daityāḥ samabhidudruvuḥ
te yayur nidhanaṃ sarve yādāṃsīva mahodadhau
viṣamaṃ tu tadā yuddhaṃ dṛṣṭvā devapatir hariḥ
gadāya preṣayām āsa svarathaṃ harivāhanaḥ
dideśa mātalisutaṃ yantāraṃ ca suvarcasam
sāmbāyairāvaṇaṃ nāgaṃ preṣayām āsa ceśvaraḥ
jayantaṃ raukmiṇeyasya sahāyam adadād vibhuḥ
airāvaṇam adhiṣṭhātuṃ pravaraṃ sa niyuktavān
devaputradvijau vīrāv aprameyaparākramau
anujñāpya varādhyakṣaṃ brahmāṇaṃ lokabhāvanam
taṃ mātalisutaṃ caiva gajam airāvaṇaṃ tadā
devaḥ preṣitavāñ śakro vidhijño varakarmasu
kṣīṇam asya tapo vadhyo yadunām eṣa durmatiḥ
praviśanti tu bhūtāni sarvatra tu yathepsitam
pradyumnaś ca jayantaś ca prāptau harmyaṃ mahābalau
asurāñ śarajālaughair vikrāmantau praṇeśatuḥ
parighair vikramantau ca yudhyantau ca raṇājire
gadaṃ kārṣṇis tadovāca durvāryaṃ raṇadurjayaḥ
upendrānuja śakreṇa ratho 'yaṃ preṣitas tava
hariyuṅ mātalisuto yantā cāyaṃ mahābalaḥ
pravarādhiṣṭhitaś cāyaṃ sāmbasyairāvaṇo gajaḥ
adyopahāro rudrasya dvārakāyāṃ mahābala
śva eṣyati hṛṣīkeśas tasmin vṛtte 'cyutānuja
tasyājñayā vadhiṣyāmo vajranābhaṃ sabāndhavam
abhyutthānakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ triviṣṭapajayaṃ prati
kariṣyāmi vidhānaṃ tu naiṣa śakraṃ sutānvitam
vijeṣyaty apramādas tu kartavya iti me matiḥ
kalatrarakṣaṇaṃ kāryaṃ sarvopāyair narair yudhi
kalatradharṣaṇaṃ loke maraṇād atiricyate
evaṃ saṃdiśya bhaimaḥ sa gadasāmbau mahābalau
pradyumnakoṭyaḥ sasṛje māyayā divyarūpayā
tamaś ca nāśayām āsa daityasṛṣṭaṃ durāsadam
jahṛṣe devarājaś ca taṃ dṛṣṭvā ripumardanam
dadṛśuḥ sarvabhūtāni kārṣṇiṃ sarveṣu śatruṣu
antarātmani vartantaṃ kṣetrajñam iti taṃ viduḥ
evaṃ vyatītā rajanī raukmiṇeyasya yudhyataḥ
asurāṇāṃ tribhāgaś ca nihato nātitejasā
yāvad dhi yodhayām āsa kārṣṇir daityān raṇājire
saṃdhyopāstā jayantena tāvad viṣṇupadījale
ayodhayaj jayantaś ca yāvad daityān mahābalaḥ
tāvad ākāśagaṅgāyāṃ bhaimaḥ saṃdhyām upāsta vān
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
jagataś cakṣuṣi tatas trimuhūrtodite ravau
prādurāsīd dharir devas tārkṣyeṇoragaśatruṇā
haṃsavāyumanobhiś ca suśīgrataragaḥ khagaḥ
tasthau viyati śakrasya samīpe kurunandana
sametya ca yathānyāyaṃ kṛṣṇo vāsavasaṃnidhau
pāñcajanyaṃ vibhur dadhmau daityānāṃ bhayavardhanam
taṃ śrutvābhyāgatas tatra pradyumnaḥ paravīrahā
vajranābhaṃ jahīty uktaḥ keśavena tvareti ca
tārkṣyam āruhya gaccheti punar eva pracoditaḥ
cakāra sa tathā vīraḥ praṇipatya surottamau
sa manoraṃhasā vīras tārkṣyeṇāśu yayau nṛpa
abhyāśaṃ vajranābhasya mahādvaṃdvasya bhārata
tatas tārkṣyagato vīras tatarda raṇamūrdhani
vajranābhaṃ sthiro bhūtvā sarvāstravid aninditaḥ
tena tārkṣyagatenaiva gadayā kṛṣṇasūnunā
urasy abhihato vīro vajranābho mahātmanā
sa tenābhihato vīro daityo mohavaśaṃ gataḥ
cakṣāra ca bhṛśaṃ raktaṃ babhrāma ca gatāsuvat
āśvasety atha taṃ kārṣṇir uvāca raṇadurjayaḥ
labdhasaṃjñaḥ sa vīras tu pradyumnam idam abravīt
sādhu yādava vīryeṇa ślāghyo mama ripur bhavān
pratiprahārakālo 'yaṃ sthiro bhava mahābala
evam uktvā mahānādaṃ muktvā meghaśatopamam
gadāṃ mumoca vegena saghaṇṭāṃ bahukaṇṭakām
tayā lalāṭe 'bhihataḥ pradyumno gadayā nṛpa
udvaman rudhiraṃ bhūri mumoha yadupuṃgavaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ pāñcajanyaṃ jalodbhavam
dadhmāv āśvāsanakaraṃ putrasya ripunāśanaḥ
taṃ pāñcajanyaśabdena pratyāśvastaṃ mahābalam
dṛṣṭvā pramuditā lokā viśeṣeṇendrakeśavau
tasya cakraṃ kare jātaṃ kṛṣṇacchandena bhārata
kṣuranemisahasrāraṃ daityasaṃghakulāntakam
taṃ mumocācyutasutaḥ śatrunāśāya bhārata
namaskṛtvā surendrāya namaskṛtvā mahātmane
vajranābhasya tatkāyād uccakarta śiras tadā
nārāyaṇasutonmuktaṃ daityānām anupaśyatām
gadaḥ sunābham avadhīd yatamānaṃ raṇājire
harmyapṛṣṭhe jighāṃsantaṃ raṇadṛptaṃ bhayānakam
sāmbaḥ samaramadhyasthān asurān arimardanaḥ
nināya niśitair bāṇaiḥ pretādhipaparigraham
nikumbho 'pi hate vīre vajranābhe mahāsure
jagāma ṣaṭpuraṃ vīro nārāyaṇabhayārditaḥ
nibarhite devaripau vajranābhe durāsade
avatīrṇau mahātmānau harī vajrapuraṃ tadā
labdhapraśamanaṃ caiva cakratuḥ surasattamau
sāntvayām āsatuś caiva bālavṛddhaṃ bhayārditam
indropendrau mahātmānau mantrayitvā mahābalau
āyatyāṃ ca tadātve ca bṛhaspatimatānugau
vajranābhasya tad rājyaṃ caturdhā cakratur nṛpa
vijayasya caturbhāgaṃ jayantatanayasya vai
pradyumnasya caturbhāgaṃ raukmiṇeyasutasya ca
candraprabhasya dadatuś caturbhāgaṃ janeśvara
koṭyaś catasro grāmāṇām adhikās tā viśāṃ pate
śākhāpurasahasraṃ ca sphītaṃ vajrapuropamam
caturdhā cakratus tatra saṃhṛṣṭau śakrakeśavau
kambalājinavāsāṃsi ratnāni vividhāni ca
caturdhā cakratur vīrau vīra vāsavakeśavau
tato 'bhiṣiktās te vīro rājāno vāsavājñayā
devaduṃdubhivādyena nṛpa viṣṇupadījalaiḥ
svayaṃ śakreṇa devena keśavena ca dhīmatā
ṛṣivaṃśe mahātmānaḥ śakramādhavanandanāḥ
vijayasya prasiddhaiva gātir viyati dhīmataḥ
mātṛjane guṇenāpi mādhavānāṃ mahātmanām
abhiṣicya jayantaṃ tu bhagavān vāsavo 'bravīt
tvayaite vīra saṃrakṣyā rājānaḥ samitiṃjaya
mama vaṃśakaro 'traikaḥ keśavasya trayo 'nagha
avadhyāḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ bhaviṣyanti mamājñayā
gamanāgamanaṃ caiva divi siddhaṃ bhaviṣyati
triviṣṭapaṃ dvārakāṃ ca ramyāṃ bhaimābhirakṣitām
diśāgajasutān nāgān hayāṃś coccaiḥśravonvayān
icchayaiṣāṃ prayacchasva rathāṃs tvaṣṭṛkṛtān api
gajāv airāvaṇasutau śatruṃjayaripuṃjayau
prayacchākāśagau vīra sāmbasya ca gadasya ca
ākāśena purīṃ yāntu dvārakāṃ bhaimarakṣitām
āyāntu ca sutaṃ draṣṭuṃ yatheṣṭaṃ bhimanandanau
iti saṃdiśya bhagavān devarājaḥ puraṃdaraḥ
jagāma bhagavān svargaṃ dvārakām api keśavaḥ
ṣaṇmāsān uṣitas tatra gadaḥ pradyumna eva ca
sāmbaś ca dvārakāṃ yātā yānārūḍhā mahābalāḥ
adyāpi tāni rājyāni meroḥ pārśve nṛpottare
sthāsyanti ca jagad yāvat tāvat te 'marasaṃnibhāḥ
nivṛtte mausale yuddhe svargaṃ yāteṣu vṛṣṇiṣu
gadapradyumnasāmbās te gatā vajrapuraṃ vibho
tataḥ proṣya punar yānti svargaṃ svaiḥ karmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ
prasādena ca kṛṣṇasya lokakartur janeśvara
pradyumnottaram etat te nṛdeva kathitaṃ mayā
dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ śatrunāśanam eva ca
putrapautrā vivardhante ārogyadhanasaṃpadaḥ
yaśo vipulam āpnoti dvaipāyanavaco yathā
sarvamāyāsv abhijño 'sau nāma viśrāvya cāvyayaḥ
aho dānava duṣṭātman keśavasyātmajaṃ śiśum
harate nirbhayaś caiva bhayam adya karomy aham
kathaṃ vai krodham āgacched badhyate vā kathaṃ mayā
prathamaṃ kiṃ kariṣyāmi yena kupyati mandadhīḥ
asti cāsya dhvajaṃ siṃhaketuvibhūṣitam
toraṇaṃ gṛham āsādya ucchritaṃ meruśṛṅgavat
etad unmathya pātiṣye bhallena niśitena vai
dhvajacchedaṃ viditvātha śambaro niṣkramiṣyati
tato yuddhena hatvājau gantāsmi dvārakāṃ prati
ity uktvā sajyam ācakre saśaraṃ cāpam ojasā
ciccheda dhvajaratnaṃ tu śambarasya mahābhujaḥ
tac chrutvā tu dhvajacchedaṃ pradyumnena mahātmanā
kruddhas tv ājñāpayām āsa putrān vai kālaśambaraḥ
jighāṃsata mahāvīrā raukmiṇeyaṃ tvarānvitaḥ
naitaṃ vai draṣṭum icchāmi mama vipriyakārakam
śrutvā tu śambarād vākyaṃ sutās te śambarasya ha
saṃnaddhā niryayur hṛṣṭāḥ pradyumnavadhakāṅkṣayā
citraseno 'tisenaś ca viṣvakseno 'jitas tathā
śrutesenaḥ suṣeṇaś ca somaseno damas tathā
senānīḥ sainyahantā ca senahā sainikas tathā
senaskandho 'tisenaś ca senako 'sanakas tathā
sutaḥ sākocavikalaḥ sātulaḥ sarakaḥ śuciḥ
kumbhaketuḥ sudaṃṣṭraś ca keśir ity evam ādayaḥ
cakratomaraśūlāni paṭṭiśāni paraśvadhān
gṛhītvā niryayur hṛṣṭā manyunā paricoditāḥ
āhvayantam amitraṃ vai tasthuḥ saṃgrāmamūrdhani
pradyumnas tu mahābāhū ratham āruhya satvaraḥ
niryayau cāpam ādāya saṃgrāmābhimukhas tadā
tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
śambarasya ca putrāṇāṃ keśavasya ca sūnunā
tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ samahoragacāraṇāḥ
devarājaṃ puraskṛtya vimānāgreṣu dhiṣṭhitāḥ
nāradas tumbarus caiva hāhā hūhūś ca gāyanāḥ
apsarobhiḥ parivṛtāḥ sarve tatrāvatasthire
devarājapratīhāro gandharvaś citram adbhutam
śaśaṃsa devarājāya vajriṇe citram adbhutam
śambarasya śataṃ putrā ekaḥ kṛṣṇasya cātmajaḥ
bahūnāṃ yudhyatām eṣa kathaṃ vijayam āpnuyāt
tac chrutvā bhāṣitaṃ tasya prahasya balasūdanaḥ
uvāca vacanaṃ cedam śṛṇu yo 'sya parākramaḥ
kāmo 'yaṃ pūrvadehe tu harakrodhāgninirjitaḥ
ratyā prasādito devaḥ kāmapatnyā trilocanaḥ
parituṣṭena devena varam asyāḥ pradīyate
viṣṇur manuṣyadehas tu dvārakāyāṃ bhaviṣyati
tasya putratvam asyaiva bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
anaṅga iti vikhyātas trilokeṣu mahāyaśāḥ
tatrotpanno mahātejāḥ śambaraṃ ghātayiṣyati
saptāhajātamātraṃ tu rukmiṇyāḥ kroḍasaṃsthitam
āsthāya śambaro māyāṃ pradyumnam apaneṣyati
tac gaccha śambaragṛhaṃ bhāryā māyāvatī bhava
māyārūpapraticchannā śambaraṃ mohayiṣyasi
tatra tvam ātmanaḥ kāntaṃ bālarūpaṃ vivardhaya
prāptayauvanadehas tu śambaraṃ nihaniṣyati
tatas tvayā sahānaṅgo dvārakāṃ vai gamiṣyati
ramiṣyati tvayā sārdhaṃ śailāputryā tv ahaṃ yathā
evam ādiśya deveśo jagāma puruṣottamaḥ
kailāsaṃ merusaṃkāśaṃ siddhacāraṇasevitam
kāmapatnī praṇamyātha devadevam umāpatim
jagāma śambaragṛhaṃ kālasyāntaṃ pratīkṣatī
evam eṣa mahābāhuḥ śambaraṃ nihaniṣyati
saputriṇo vai pradyumno hantā tasya durātmanaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
śambarasya tu putrāṇāṃ rukmiṇyā nandanasya ca
tataḥ kruddhā mahādaityāḥ śaraśaktiparaśvadhān
cakratomarakuntāni bhuśuṇḍīr musalāni ca
yugapat pātayanti sma pradyumnopari vegitāḥ
kārṣṇāyanis tu saṃkruddhaḥ sarvāstrair dhanuṣaś cyutaiḥ
ekaikaṃ paṅcabhiḥ kruddhaś ciccheda raṇamūrdhani
tato 'surā kruddhatarāḥ sarve te kṛtaniścayāḥ
vavarṣuḥ śarajālāni pradyumnavadhakāṅkṣayā
tataḥ prakupito 'naṅgo dhanur āyamya satvaraḥ
śambarasya jaghānāśu daśa putrān mahaujasaḥ
tato 'pareṇa bhallena kupitaḥ keśavātmajaḥ
cicchedāśu śiras tasya citrasenasya vīryavān
tatas te hataśeṣās tu sametya samayudhyata
śaravarṣaṃ vimuñcanto abhyadhāvañ jighāṃsitum
tataḥ saṃdhāya bāṇāṃs tu vimuṅcan sa raṇotsukaḥ
krīḍann iva mahātejās teṣāṃ śīrṣāṇy apātayat
nihatya samare sarvāñ śatam uttamadhanvinām
pradyumnaḥ samarākaṅkṣī tasthau saṃgrāmamūrdhani
hataṃ putraśataṃ śrutvā śambaraḥ krodham ādadhe
sūtaṃ saṃcodayām āsa rathaṃ me saṃprayojaya
rājño vākyaṃ niśamyātha praṇamya śirasā bhuvi
sa sainyaṃ codayām āsa rathaṃ ca susamāhitam
yuktam ṛkṣasahasreṇa sarpayoktreṇa yoktritam
śārdūlacarmasaṃceṣṭaṃ kiṃkiṇījālamālinam
īhāmṛgagaṇākīrṇaṃ paṅktibhaktivirājitam
tārācitrapinaddhāṅgaṃ svarṇakūbarabhūṣitam
sapatākaṃ mahocchrāyaṃ mṛgarājograketanam
suvibhaktavarūthaṃ ca loheṣāvajrabandhuram
mandarodagraśikharaṃ cārucāmarabhūṣitam
nakṣatramālāpihitaṃ hemadaṇḍasamāhitam
virājamānaṃ śrīmantam ārohac chambaras tadā
kāñcanaṃ citrasaṃnāhaṃ dhanur gṛhya śarāṃs tathā
prasthitaḥ samarākāṅkṣī mṛtyunā paricoditaḥ
caturbhiḥ sacivaiḥ sārdhaṃ sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥ
durdharaḥ ketumālī ca śatruhantā pramardanaḥ
etaiḥ parivṛto 'mātyair yuyutsuḥ prasthito raṇe
daśa nāgasahasrāṇi rathānāṃ dve śate tathā
hayānāṃ cāṣṭasāhasraiḥ prayutaiś ca padātinām
etaiḥ parivṛto yodhaiḥ śambaraḥ prayayau tadā
prayātasya tu saṃgrāme utpātāny utthitāni vai
gṛdhracakrākule vyomni saṃdhyākārābhranādite
garjanti puruṣaṃ medhā nirghātaś cāmbarāt patat
śivā vinedur aśivaṃ sainyaṃ saṃkālayan mahat
dhvajaśīrṣe 'patad gṛdhraḥ kāṅkṣan vai dānavāsṛjam
rathāgre patitaś cāsya kabandho bhuvi dṛśyate
cīcīkūcīti vāśanti śambarasya rathopari
svarbhānugrasta ādityaḥ parighaiḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ
sphurate nayanaṃ cāsya savyaṃ bhayanivedanam
bāhuḥ prakampate savyaḥ prāskhalan rathavājinaḥ
dhvāṅkṣo mūrdhni nipatitaḥ śambarasya surāriṇaḥ
vavarṣa rudhiraṃ devaḥ sīkarodgāramiśritam
ulkāpātasahasrāṇi nipetū raṇamūrdhani
pratodo nyapatad dhastāt sārather hayayāyinaḥ
etān acintayitvā tu utpātān samupasthitān
prayayau śambaraḥ kruddhaḥ pradyumnavadhakāṅkṣayā
bherīśaṅkhamṛdaṅgānāṃ paṇavānakaduṃdubheḥ
yugapat tāḍyamānānāṃ pṛthivī samakampata
tena śabdena mahatā saṃtrastā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ
samastād dudruvus tasmād bhayaviklavacetanāḥ
raṇamadhye sthitaḥ kārṣṇiś cintayan nidhanaṃ ripoḥ
sainyaiḥ parivṛtaḥ saṃkhye yuddhāya kṛtaniścayaḥ
kruddhaḥ śarasahasreṇa pradyumnaṃ samatāḍayat
asaṃprāptāṃś ca tān bāṇāṃś ciccheda kṛtahastavat
pradyumno dhanur ādāya śaravarṣaṃ mumoca ha
na tasya sainye 'bhimukho yo na viddhaḥ śareṇa vai
pradyumnaśarapātena tat sainyaṃ vimukhīkṛtam
śambarasya tathābhyāśe sthitaṃ saṃhṛtya bhītavat
svabalaṃ vidrutaṃ dṛṣṭvā śambaraḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
ājñāpayām āsa tadā sacivān dānaveśvaraḥ
gacchadhvaṃ manniyogena praharadhvaṃ ripoḥ sutam
nopekṣaṇīyaḥ śatrur vai vadhyatāṃ kṣipram eṣa vai
upekṣita iva vyādhiḥ śarīraṃ nāśayed dhruvam
tad eṣa durgatiḥ pāpo vadhyatāṃ matpriyecchayā
tatas te sacivāḥ kruddhāḥ śirasā gṛhya śāsanam
śaravarṣaṃ pramuñcantas tvaritāś codayan rathān
tān dṛṣṭvā dhāvataḥ saṃkhye kruddho makaraketanaḥ
cāpam udyamya saṃbhrāntas tasthau pramukhato balī
durdharaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
bibheda sumahātejāḥ ketumāliṃ triṣaṣṭibhiḥ
saptatyā śatruhantāraṃ dvyaśītyā tu pramardanam
bibheda paramāmarṣī rukmiṇyā nandivardhanaḥ
tatas te savicāḥ kruddhā pradyumnaṃ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
ekaikaśo bibhedājau ṣaṣṭibhiḥ ṣaṣṭibhiḥ śaraiḥ
tān aprāptāñ śarān bāṇaiś ciccheda makaradhvajaḥ
tato 'rdhacandram ādāya durdharasya sa sārathim
jaghāna paśyatāṃ rājñāṃ sarveṣāṃ sainikasya vai
caturbhir atha nārācaiḥ suparvaiḥ kaṅkavājitaiḥ
jaghāna caturaḥ so 'śvān durdharasya rathaṃ prati
ekena yoktraṃ chatraṃ ca dhvajam ekena bandhuram
ṣaṣṭyā ca yugacakrākṣaṃ ciccheda makaradhvajaḥ
athāparaṃ śaraṃ gṛhya kaṅkapatraṃ sutejitam
mumoca hṛdaye tasya durdharasyālpajīvinaḥ
sa gatāsur gataśrīko gatasattvo gataprabhaḥ
nipapāta rathopasthāt kṣīṇapuṇya iva grahaḥ
durdhare nihate śūre dānave dānaveśvaraḥ
ketumālī śaravrātair abhidudrāva kṛṣṇajam
pradyumnam abhisaṃkruddho bhrukuṭībhīṣaṇānanam
kṛtvābhyadhāvat sahasā tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
saṃkruddhaḥ kṛṣṇasūnus tu śaravarṣair avākirat
parvataṃ vāridhārābhiḥ prāvṛṣīva yathā ghanaḥ
sa viddho dānavāmātyaḥ pradyumnena dhanuṣmatā
cakram ādāya cikṣepa pradyumnavadhakaṅkṣayā
tam aprāptaṃ sahasrāraṃ kṛṣṇacakrasamadyutim
nipatyotpatya jagrāha sarveṣām eva paśyatām
tenaiva tasya ciccheda ketumāleḥ śiras tadā
tad dṛṣṭvā karma vipulaṃ raukmiṇeyasya devarāṭ
vismayaṃ paramaṃ prāptaḥ sarvair devagaṇaiḥ saha
gandharvāpsarasaś caiva puṣpavarṣair avākiran
ketumāliṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā śatruhantā pramardanaḥ
mahābalasamūhena pradyumnam atha dudruve
te gadāṃ musalaṃ cakraṃ prāsatomarasāyakān
bhindipālān kuṭhārāṃś ca bhāsvarān kūṭamudgarān
yugapat saṃkṣipanti sma vadhārthaṃ kṛṣṇanandane
so 'pi tāny astrajālāni śastrajālair anekadhā
ciccheda bahudhā vīro darśayan pāṇilāghavam
gajān so 'bhyahanat kruddho gajārohān sahasraśaḥ
rathān sārathibhiḥ sārdhaṃ hayāṃś caiva tu mardayan
pātayaṃs tāñ śaravrātair nāviddhaḥ kaś cid īkṣyate
evaṃ sarvāṇi sainyāni mamantha makaradhvajaḥ
nadīṃ prāvartayad ghorāṃ śoṇitāmbutaraṃgiṇīm
muktāhārormibahulāṃ māṃsamedosthipaṅkinīm
chatradvīpaśarāvartāṃ rathaiḥ pulinamaṇḍitām
keyūrakuṇḍalākūrmāṃ dhvajamatsyavibhūṣitām
nāgagrāhavatīṃ raudrīṃ matsyanakravibhūṣitām
keśaśaivālasaṃchannāṃ śroṇisūtramṛṇālikām
narānanasupadmāṃ ca haṃsacāmaravījitām
śirastimisamākīrṇāṃ śoṇitaughapravartinīm
nadīṃ dustaraṇīṃ bhīmām anaṅgena pravartitām
duṣprekṣāṃ durgamāṃ raudrāṃ hīnatejaḥsudustarām
śastragrāhavatīṃ ghorāṃ yamarāṣṭravivardhanīm
tān rukmiṇīṣutaḥ śrīmān viloḍayati dhanvinaḥ
śatruhantāram āśritya śarān abhyakiran bahūn
śatruhantā punaḥ kruddho mumoca śaram uttamam
pradyumnaṃ sa samāsādya hṛdaye nipapāta ha
sa viddhas tena bāṇena pradyumno na vyakampata
śaktiṃ jagrāha balavāñ śatruhantre mumūrṣave
sā kṣiptā raukmiṇeyena śaktir jvālākulā raṇe
patāta hṛdayaṃ bhittvā vajrāśanisamasvanā
bhinnahṛdayaḥ srastāṅgo muktamarmāsthibandhanaḥ
papāta rudhirodgārī śatruhantā mahābalaḥ
patitaṃ śatruhantāraṃ dṛṣṭvā tasthau pramardanaḥ
jagrāha musalaṃ so'tha vacanaṃ cedam ādade
tiṣṭha kiṃ prākṛtair ebhiḥ kariṣyasi raṇapriya
māṃ yodhaya sudurbuddhe tatas tvaṃ na bhaviṣyasi
vṛṣṇivaṃśakule jātaḥ śatrur asmatpitā tava
putraṃ hantāsmy ahaṃ tasya tato 'sau nihato bhavet
mṛtena tena durbuddhe sarvadevakṣayo bhavet
daiteyā dānavāḥ sarve modantāṃ hataśatravaḥ
hate tvayi mamāstreṇa tvatsamutthaiś ca śoṇitaiḥ
śambarasya tu putrāṇāṃ karomy udakasatkriyām
adya bhīṣmasutā mandā karuṇaṃ vilapiṣyati
nihataṃ tvāṃ ca śrutvaiva yauvanasthaṃ gatāyuṣam
sa te pitā cakradharo viphalāśo bhaviṣyati
hataṃ tvāṃ sa viditvā tu prāṇāṃs tyakṣyati mandadhīḥ
ity uktvā parigheṇāśu tāḍayad rukmiṇīsutam
sa tāḍito mahātejā raukmiṇeyaḥ pratāpavān
dorbhyām ākṣipya tasyaiva rathamukhyaṃ vyacūrṇayat
so 'vaplutya rathāt tasmāt padātir avatasthivān
tāṃ gadāṃ gṛhya sahasā raukmiṇeyam upādravat
tathaiva gadayā kāmaḥ pramardanam apothayat
hataṃ pramardanaṃ daityaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve pradudruvuḥ
na śaktāḥ pramukhe sthātuṃ siṃhatrāsād gajā iva
sārameyaṃ yathā dṛṣṭvā vigaṇo vipraṇaśyate
tathā sainyā viṣīdanti pradyumnasya bhayārditāḥ
kṣatajādigdhavaktrā vai muktakeśā hy aśobhata
rajasvaleva yuvatiḥ senā samavagūhate
madanaśaravibhinnā sainikān abhyupāyād
yuvatisadṛśaveṣā sādhvasaiḥ pīḍyamānā
ratisamaram aśaktā vīkṣituṃ socchvasantī
svagṛhagamanakāmā necchate sthātum atra
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
śambaras tu tataḥ kruddhaḥ sūtam āha viśāṃ pate
śatrupramukhato vīra rathaṃ me śīgram āvaha
yāvad enaṃ śarair hanmi mama vipriyakārakam
tato bhartur vacaḥ śrutvā sūtas tatpriyakārakaḥ
ṛkṣān saṃcodayaām āsa cāmīkaravibhūṣitān
taṃ dṛṣṭvā ratham āyāntaṃ pradyumnaḥ phullalocanaḥ
saṃdadhe cāpam ādāya śaraṃ kanakabhūṣaṇam
tenāhanat susaṃkruddhaḥ kopayañ śambaraṃ raṇe
hṛdaye tāḍitas tena devaśatruḥ suviklavaḥ
rathopasthaṃ samāśritya tasthau so 'tha vicetanaḥ
sa cetanāṃ punaḥ prāpya dhanur ādāya śambaraḥ
vivyādha kārṣṇiṃ kupitaḥ saptabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
tān aprāptāñ śarān so 'tha saptabhiḥ saptadhācchinat
śambaraṃ ca jaghānātha saptatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
punaḥ śarasahasreṇa kaṅkabarhiṇavāsasā
ahanac chambaraṃ krodhād dhārābhir iva parvatam
pradiśo vidiśaś caiva śaradhārāsamāvṛtāḥ
andhakārīkṛtaṃ vyoma dineśo naiva dṛśyate
tato 'ndhakāram utsārya vaidyutāstreṇa śambaraḥ
pradyumnasya rathopasthe śaravarṣaṃ mumoca ha
tad astrajālaṃ pradyumnaḥ śareṇānataparvaṇā
ciccheda bahudhā rājan darśayan pāṇilāghavam
hate tasmin mahāvarṣe śarāṇāṃ kārṣṇinā tadā
drumavarṣaṃ mumocātha māyayā kālaśambaraḥ
drumavarṣocchritaṃ dṛṣṭvā pradyumnaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
āgneyāstraṃ mumocātha tena vṛkṣān aśātayat
bhasmībhūte vṛkṣvarṣe śilāsaṃghātam utsṛjat
pradyumnas taṃ tu vāyavyaiḥ protsārayata saṃyuge
tato māyāṃ parāṃ cakre devaśatruḥ pratāpavān
siṃhān vyāghrān varāhāṃś ca tarakṣūn ṛkṣavānarān
vāraṇān vāridaprakhyān hayān uṣṭrān viśāṃ pate
mumoca dhanur āyamya pradyumnasya rathopari
gāndharvāstreṇa ciccheda sarvāṃs tān khaṇḍaśas tadā
pradyumnena tu sā māyā hatā tāṃ vīkṣya śambaraḥ
anyāṃ māyāṃ mumocātha śambaraḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
gajendrān bhinnavadanān ṣaṣṭihāyanayauvanān
mahāmātrottamārūḍhān kalpitān raṇagarvitān
tām āpatantīṃ māyāṃ tu kārṣṇiḥ kamalalocanaḥ
saiṃhīṃ māyāṃ samutsraṣṭuṃ cakre buddhiṃ mahāmanāḥ
sṛṣṭāyāṃ siṃhamāyāyāṃ raukmiṇeyena dhīmatā
māyā nāgamayī naṣṭā ādityeneva śarvarī
nihatāṃ hastimāyāṃ tu dṛṣṭvāsau dānaveśvaraḥ
māyāṃ saṃmohanīṃ nāma so 'sṛjad dānaveśvaraḥ
tāṃ sṛṣṭāṃ mohinīṃ nāma māyāṃ mayavinirmitām
saṃjñāstreṇa tu pradyumno nāśayām āsa vīryavān
śambaras tu tataḥ kruddho māyayā naṣṭayā tathā
saiṃhīṃ māyāṃ mahātejāḥ so 'sṛjad dānaveśvaraḥ
siṃhān āpatato dṛṣṭvā raukmiṇeyaḥ pratāpavān
astraṃ gāndharvam ādāya śarabhān asṛjat tadā
te 'ṣṭāpadā balodagrā nakhadaṃṣṭrāyudhā raṇe
siṃhān vidrāvayām āsur vāyur jaladharān iva
siṃhān vidrāvitān dṛṣṭvā māyayāṣṭāpadena vai
śambaraś cintayām āsa katham enaṃ nihanmi vai
aho mūrkhasvabhāvo 'haṃ yan mayā na hataḥ śiśuḥ
prāptayauvanadehas tu kṛtāstraś cāpi durmatiḥ
tat kathaṃ nihaniṣyāmi śatruṃ raṇaśiraḥsthitam
māyā sā tiṣṭhate tīvrā pannagī nāma bhīṣaṇā
dattā me devadevena hareṇāsuraghātinā
tāṃ sṛjāmi mahāmāyām āśīviṣasamākulām
tayā dahyeta duṣṭātmā hy eṣa māyāmayena vai
sā sṛṣṭā pānnagī māyā viṣajvālāsamākulā
tayā pannagamayyā tu sarathaṃ sahavājinam
sasūtaṃ sa hi pradyumnaṃ babandha śarabandhanaiḥ
badhyamānaṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā ātmānaṃ vṛṣṇivaṃśajaḥ
māyāṃ saṃcintayām āsa sauparṇīṃ sarpanāśanīm
sā cintitā mahāmāyā pradyumnena mahātmanā
suparṇā vicaranti sma sarpā naṣṭā mahāviṣāḥ
bhagnāyāṃ sarpamāyāyāṃ praśaṃsanti surāsurāḥ
sādhu vīra mahābāho sādhu rukmiṇinandana
yat tvayā dharṣitā māyā tena sma paritoṣitāḥ
hatāyāṃ sarpamāyāyāṃ śambaro 'cintayat punaḥ
asti me kāladaṇḍābho mudgaro hemabhūṣitaḥ
tam apratihataṃ yuddhe devadānavamānuṣaiḥ
mayā sṛṣṭaṃ svadehena tapas taptvā suduścaram
purā yo mama pārvatyā dattaḥ paramatuṣṭayā
gṛhāṇa śambaremaṃ tvaṃ mudgaraṃ hemabhūṣitam
māyāntakaraṇaṃ nāma sarvāsuravināśanam
anena dānavau raudrau balinau nagacāriṇau
śumbhaś caiva niśumbhaś ca sagaṇau sūditau mayā
prāṇasaṃśayam āpanne tvayā mokṣyaḥ sa śatrave
ity uktvā pārvatī devī tatraivāntaradhīyata
tad ahaṃ mudgaraśreṣṭhaṃ mocayiṣyāmi śatrave
tasya vijñāya cittaṃ tu devarājo 'bhyabhāṣata
gaccha nārada śīgraṃ tvaṃ pradyumnasya rathaṃ prati
saṃbodhaya mahābāhuṃ pūrvajātiṃ ca smāraya
vaiṣṇavāstraṃ prayacchāsmai vadhārthaṃ śambarasya ca
abhedyaṃ kavacaṃ cāsya prayacchāsurasūdanam
evam ukto maghavatā nāradaḥ prayayau tvaran
ākāśo 'dhiṣṭhito 'vocan makaradhvajaketanam
kumāra paśya māṃ prāptaṃ devagandharvanāradam
preṣitaṃ devarājena tava saṃbodhanāya vai
smara tvaṃ pūrvakaṃ bhāvaṃ kāmadevo 'si mānada
harakopānalād dagdhas tenānaṅga ihocyase
tvaṃ vṛṣṇivaṃśe jāto 'si rukmiṇyā garbhasaṃbhavaḥ
jāto 'si keśavena tvaṃ pradyumna iti kīrtyase
āhṛtya śambareṇa tvam ihānīto 'si mānada
saptarātre tv asaṃpūrṇe sūtikāgāramadhyataḥ
vadhārthaṃ śambarasya tvaṃ hriyamāṇo hy apekṣitaḥ
keśavena mahābāho devakāryārthasiddhaye
yaiṣā māyāvatī nāma bhāryā vai śambarasya tu
ratiṃ tāṃ viddhi kalyāṇīṃ tava bhāryāṃ purātanīm
tava sā rakṣaṇārthāya śambarasya gṛhe 'vasat
māyāṃ śarīrajāṃ nyasya mohanārthaṃ durātmanaḥ
rater utpādanārthāya preṣayaty aniśaṃ tadā
evaṃ pradyumna buddhyā vai tava bhāryā pratiṣṭhitā
hatvā tvaṃ śambaraṃ vīra vaiṣṇavāstreṇa saṃyuge
gṛhya māyāvatīṃ bhāryāṃ dvārakāṃ gantum arhasi
gṛhāṇa vaiṣṇavaṃ cāstraṃ kavacaṃ ca mahāprabham
śakreṇa tava saṃgṛhya preṣitaṃ śatrusūdana
śṛṇu me hy aparaṃ vākyaṃ kriyatām aviśaṅkayā
asya devaripos tāta mudgaro nityapūjitaḥ
pārvatyā tuṣṭayā dattaḥ sarvaśatrubarhaṇaḥ
amoghaś caiva saṃgrāme devadānavamānavaiḥ
tad astrapratighātārthaṃ devīṃ saṃsmartum arhasi
stavyā caiva namasyā ca mahādevī raṇotsukaiḥ
tatra vai kriyatāṃ yatnaḥ saṃgrāme ripuṇā saha
ity uktvā nārado vākyaṃ prayayau yatra vāsavaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
śambaras tu tataḥ kruddho mudgaraṃ taṃ samādade
mudgare gṛhyamāṇe tu dvādaśārkāḥ samutthitāḥ
parvatāś calitāḥ sarve calitaṃ vasudhātalam
udmārgāḥ sāgarā jātāḥ saṃkṣubdhāś cāpi devatāḥ
gṛdhracakrākulaṃ vyoma ulkāpāto babhūva ha
vavarṣa rudhiraṃ devaḥ puruṣaṃ pavano vavau
evaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahotpātān pradyumnaḥ sa tvarānvitaḥ
avatīrya rathād vīraḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭaḥ sthitaḥ
devīṃ sasmāra manasā pārvatīṃ śaṃkarapriyām
praṇamya śirasā devīṃ stotuṃ samupacakrame
pradyumna uvāca
oṃ namaḥ kātyāyanyai guhasya jananyai namaḥ
namas trailokyamāyāyai kātyāyanyai namo namaḥ
namaḥ śatruvināśinyai namo gārgyai girīśaye
namasye śumbhahananīṃ niśumbhahṛdidāraṇīm
kālarātriṃ namasye 'haṃ kumārīṃ cāpi nityaśaḥ
kāntāravāsinīṃ devīṃ namasyāmi kṛtāñjaliḥ
vindhyavāsinīṃ durgaghnīṃ raṇadurgāṃ raṇapriyām
namasyāmi mahādevīṃ jayāṃ ca vijayāṃ tathā
aparājitāṃ namasye 'ham ajitāṃ śatrutāpanīm
ghaṇṭāhastāṃ namasyāmi ghaṇṭāmālākulāṃ tathā
triśūlinīṃ namasyāmi mahiṣāsuraghātinīm
siṃhavāhāṃ namasyāmi siṃhapravaraketanām
ekānaṃśāṃ namasyāmi gāyatrīṃ yajñasatkriyām
sāvitrīṃ cāpi viprāṇāṃ namasye 'haṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ
rakṣa māṃ devi satataṃ saṃgrāme vijayaṃ kuru
iti kāmavacaḥ śrutvā durgā suprītamānasā
uvāca vacanaṃ devī suprītenāntarātmanā
paśya paśya mahābāho rukmiṇyānandavardhana
varaṃ varaya vatsa tvam amoghaṃ darśanaṃ mama
devyāstu vacanaṃ śrutvā romāñ codgatamānasaḥ
praṇamya śirasā devīṃ vijñaptum upacakrame
yadi tvaṃ devi tuṣṭāsi dīyatāṃ me yadīpsitam
varaṃ ca varade yāce sarvāmitreṣu me jayaḥ
yas tvayā mudgaro dattaḥ śambarasyātmasaṃbhavaḥ
eṣa me gātram āsādya mālā padmamayī bhavet
tathāstv iti ca sāpy uktvā tatraivantaradhīyata
pradyumnas tu mahātejā hṛṣṭo ratham athāruhat
mudgaraṃ tu gṛhītvā ca śambaraḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
bhrāmayitvā sa cikṣepa pradyumnorasi vīryavān
sa gatvā madanābhyāśaṃ mālā bhūtvātha pauṣkarī
pradyumnasya ca kaṇṭhe sā samāyuktā vyarājata
nakṣatrāṇāṃ tu mālāyāṃ yathā parivṛto vidhuḥ
tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ siddhāś ca paramarṣayaḥ
sādhu sādhv iti vācocuḥ pūjayan keśavātmajam
mudgaraṃ puṣpabhūtaṃ tu dṛṣṭvā pradyumnasaṃnidhau
vaiṣṇavaṃ paramāstraṃ tu nāradena yadāhṛtam
saṃdadhe cāpam āyamya idaṃ vacanam abravīt
yady ahaṃ rukmiṇīputraḥ keśavasyātmajo hy aham
tena satyena bāṇemaṃ jahi tvaṃ śambaraṃ raṇe
ity uktvā cāpam ākṛṣya saṃdhāya ca mahāmanāḥ
cikṣepa śambarāāyātha dahaṃl lokatrayaṃ tviṣā
sa kṣipto vṛṣṇisiṃhena bāṇaḥ kravyādamohanaḥ
hṛdayaṃ śambarasyātha bhittvā dharaṇim āgamat
naivāsya māṃsaṃ na snāyur nāsthi na tvaṅ na śoṇitam
sarvaṃ tadbhasmasādbhūtaṃ vaiṣṇavāstrasya tejasā
hate daitye mahākāye dānave śambare 'dhame
jahṛṣur devagandharvā nanṛtuś cāpsarogaṇāḥ
ūrvaśī menakā rambhā vipracittis tilottamā
nanṛtur hṛṣṭamanaso jagatsthāvarajaṃgamam
devarājas tu suprītaḥ sarvair devagaṇaiḥ saha
pradyumnaṃ puṣpavarṣeṇa samabhyarcya prahṛṣṭavat
atha samarahate tu daityarāje
madhumathanasya sutena vaiṣṇavāstraiḥ
vigataripubhayāḥ surāś ca jagmur
makaravibhūṣaṇaketanaṃ stuvantaḥ
sa ca samarapariśramaṃ vahan vai
nagaramukhaṃ praviveśa raukmiṇeyaḥ
priyatama iva kāntayā prahṛṣṭas
tvaritapadaṃ ratidarśanaṃ cakāra
